Kochchooruwa
Xaafoy doomettanaappe kase asa ubbay issi mala ogiya qofaa laammees. Hegee asaa daro darchcheyiidi takkoogee erettidabaa. Heede asay eraa, hekkaa woykko meeziya issoy issuwara laamettiyoynne issi yeletaappe hankkuwa pinttiyogee mulekka qofettenna. Issi issi deree konssoonidi maachchaa immiyobaa woykko wolqqaama wudissiyo allaalle gidikkokka coo heeraa cimay shiiqin timettaa demmees. Beni Oroomaa biittan Kaassaare kawotettaa wode galla galla yaa’ettiyo allaalliya asay godan xaafi kaqqi wottoosona; he kaquwan de’iyagaa xeellidi bari yaa’iyo allaalliyaw kuushsha qofaa asay eroosona. Hagee xaafuwassi hiixa gididoogaa daro tamaari luxidaageeti ammanettoosona. Xaafoy doomettanaappe kase asay issibaa malaatidi woykko misiliya hebaa sohuwan gelissi go’’ettees. Toophphiyan miidee zammaana ogiyan eqqoy 141 layttappe kase. 

Wodala ganjjee naqaashaa demmiyo heezzu pulttoti: oyshaa, xeelaanne xaaduquwa. Oyshi baynnan naqaashi shiiqenna. Pulttoy/waabee wodala ganjjiyassi suutta xapho. Wodalaa ganjjee yo’uwassi kulkkaa demmanaw eqqidi ooni, ay, awan, ayssi, awdenne waanidi giya qaalatun amppidi oyshaa kitinttees. Xaafoy, xeelay, ezggoy, ayfe yo’uwa qashamiyogeenne wurssetta xaaxi waaxo oyshay wodala ganjjee asay dabaaban haasayaa kelkkiyo wode baassi naqaashaa koshaa saamuwa alanaw gixxi denddidi oottanaw guyye geenna wogata. Nu Toophphiya Saara Bazzuwappe xadeera diya Afrkkaa biittatun ba pitalee diyo biitti I kanchche gidiyogee keehi ceeqqissiyabaa. Hegaa gidoshin xaafonne nabbabo bilaa dichchay hanno gakkanaw nu biitten keehi yiilloyiya xekkan de’ees. Miidee issi biitaassi gutaraa, issipetettaanne aqotaa laamiya ehanaw hara dooroy baynna miishsha. Hagaa oonne kashi gi palamettiya uri baawa. 

Miidiyan pissiya shiishshiyo wode aybippenne aatti xeelliyobay naa’’u baggaa (ubba zawaa) bixe ootti xeellidi xillo pirddaa immiyogaa. Ee, xaafoy deexo miishsha gidikkonne lo’’o xaafoy asaa nabbabanaassi wuttees. Bixaali baynnan yeddi bessiyo biiree guuttiyo ganxxin tinkkiri ootti woriya marzze mala. Hegaa gishshaw ‘hallitay onggiichchin haniira aadhdharkkina’ gin oottenna; xaafanchchay xaafiidi bana siridi wolqqaama wudaa immidi tiree qaaxxi kokkoriidi haniya qaalaa dooridi xaafanaw bessees. Ziba peeshoti nabbabiyageetussi kahan misiliya medhdhoosona; haray qassi 18 qaalatuppe guuxxiya qaalata issi qofa qashuwan go’’ettiyokka nabbabanaw wayssenna. Geediyagee issi xissi (senkkoy) beettikko harqqidi diggirggees. Oduwassi na’ee daashshaa. Daashshay oduwassi naqaashaa puulayees; maattametti shiiqiyabaassikka boolimaa naagissees. Qaalaa doori go’’ettiyogee daashshaw keehi koshshiya yo’o. Coraa gattiyo naqaashay erissosappe attin qonccissosa gidenna; hegaappe denddidaagan A xaafiyageeti xaqqayiyageeta geetettoosona. Keehi daro giishin televizhzhiiniyan oduwa aattiyogee mexi naa’’u daqiiqa gidishin 20ppe bi 30 sekkonddee gida. Coraa gattiyo naqaashaw ha’’i wode peeshota xaafuwassi qassi aadhdhida wode peeshota go’’eteettees.

Jorinaale qofay awdenne deriyakko simmees; issi jorinaaliya lo’’o gaanay koyro aw halchchoy lo’’iina. Ha wodiya naqaashaa pulttuwa maaraa oyttanaagee daro meto. Deriya ekettenna jorinaaliizimee allaalle kessenna yaatiyo gishshaw issi jorinaalee bari qofaa issi baggi zaari wottidi deriya qofaakko simmiyogaanne deriya qofaassi bana yarshshi oottishin gakkiya xubetakka tiran ekki oottees. Tumi jorinaaliizimiyassi ayfe yo’o. Jorinaaliizime oosoy porxxu gi kiyi puriis giyogee wurssettan tumaa koyidi demmiyo wode.















   KOYRO SHEMPPUWA
JORINAALIIZIME HAYDAA
1.1.	XAAFUWA XUUSSAA
Koyro kochchooro xaafoy doomettanaappe kasetidi naa''u metoti pagalettanaw koshshees. Hegeetikka: koyoy ha nu haasayiyo cenggurssay woykko qofay ay misiliyan sohuwan gelissiyo giyagaa gidishin naa''anttoy aybin ha misileti xaafettanee yaagiya gaa. Koyro metoy naa"u ogiyan pagalettiis. Beni wode asay issibaa malaata woykko misiliya A sohuwan gelissi go"ettees. Issibaa xeessanaassinne sunttanaassi koyikko hebaa milatiya misiliya medhdhees. Hegee laafabaa bessanaw cora misileta go''ettanaadan oottees. Hegaadan misiliyan go''ettiyogee Kiristtoosa Yeletaappe Kase (KYK) 3500 layttaappe kase 'Sumeriyane' (ha"i wodiyan Iraaqe) biittan dicci dicci biis. Gibitstse biittaa asaykka guutta xeetu layttaappe kase hagaatto misiliyan go''ettoosona. Keehi gam''iya malaatan xaafiyogee Chaynaa biittan 200ppe 1500 KYK gakkanaw go''ettishin takkiis. Naa''antto xaafo hiillay dariya baggi malaataappe cenggurssan go''ettiyogaa. Hegaappe simmin qaalaa medhdhiya dumma dumma pitaletu citay merettiis. 'Poynishiyans' geetettiyageeti ha nu qofa qashuwa xaafiyo pitaliya medhdhana gatiya qanxxidosona. 'Poynishiyaneti' giddo abban zal''iyageeta; eta demoy Meedetiraaniyappe Giriike gakkin 24 pitaleti merettidosona. Xaafuwa metoy hagaa maaran polettiis. 

Sumeeriyaneti urqqaa laalukkidi pooto milatiya misiliya medhdhidi kobbe misiliya milatiya ooso miishsha oottidi qaalaa sohuwan gelissidi mazggaboosona. Ha urqqaappe merettida kobbe malatiyagee hano gakkanaw de''ees; keehippe al"onne moorettennan daro wodiya takkiya ooso miishsha. Haray qassi Gibitstseti Abbaa manttiyan mokkiya 'papyrus' geetettiya mittaappe woraqataa medhdhidosona. Xaafiyo miishshaa qassi Giriikenne Oroomaa biittaa asay pittiyogaa (buruushiya) malatiya biiriya medhdhidosona. He ooso miishshan go''ettidi xaafuwa doommidosona. He mayzzati xaafiyo miishshay calaappe merettees shin medhdhanaw keehippe deexxo; woraqataagaadan wayssennan kalali gi merettenna. Hegaappe simmin Chaynati xekkaa naagida woraqataa medhdhidosona. Eti ha woraqataa medhdhanaassi mittaa poquwanne golaa maldduwara gattidi caddi munaqqidi awan miccidi melissidi woraqataa medhdhidosona. Ha merettida woraqattay oykkanaw keehippe kawshsha, shammanaw gatee hiraysonne xaafanaw injjettees. 
1.2.	XAAFUWA GO"AA
Koyro kochchooruwan xaafoy asa giddon dummatettaa medhdhiis. Xaafoy doomettanaappe kase asaa ubbay issi mala ogiyan qofaa laamettoosona. Haasayoosonanne siyoosonappe attin xaafokkonanne nabbabokkona. Qofaa laamettanaassi naqaashaa koyiyageetussi koshshay doppe attin xaafidi woykko nabbabidi naqaasha demmanaagee salo xeera. 
•	Xaafoy issi yamiya oosuwa lefayiis.
•	Giiraa shiishshiyageeti sohuwara qanxxetta miishsha xaafi immidi ekkiyogee he oosuwa lefayiis.
•	Baadee asaa bogiyappenne bonqaappe naaganaw kawo garuwan dayettin assi damoozay qanxxettees.
•	Xaafoy zal''iya minttiis; miishshaa oosuwakka darissiis.
•	Haahuwan diyageeta matayidi dabidaabiyan gattiis.
Wurssettan meretaa eray gujji gujji boogee bari huuphphe bana danddayida laamiya ehida gaaso. Xaafoy doomettanaappe kase asay barchchiya be''iis. Eraa issi yeletaappe haraw aattiyogee keehippe xunttanne ubbakka qofettenna. Maacciyonne pirddaa immiyobata heeran shiiqida cima asay coo malan hagee likke hagee bala geetettidi coo pirddetteesinne maacettees. Haydan koyro bayra xaaduqoy, 'the code of Hummurabi' yaagiyagaa Sumeereti KYK 2000 layttaa giddon mucuuri giigissido xaaduquwa.
1.3. JORINAALIIZMIYASSI DENDDUWA
5antto layttan gaazeexaa doomettay hani kanttabaa ubbaappe malaalissiyabaa. Beni Kaasaarisa wode Oroomaa biittay gaazeexaa go''ettiyogaa doommiis. 'The Acta Durna' (galla galla oosuwa) issitoonne seeraa kessiyageeti yaa'iyode godan xaafetti uttees. Hegaa muletoo geliyanne kiyiya deree nabbabees. Yaatin asay aybi haniidi diyakkonne, aybi oottana halchchettaakkonne qonccissiyo gishshaw deree saamettidi nabbabees. Daro tamaari luxidaageeti hagee jorinaalizimiyassi baaso (hiixa) yaagi ammanoosona. Ha galla galla deriyanne gutaraabaa KYK 5antta wodiyan Juuliis Kaasaare wode asay xaafi godan kaqqiyogee gaazeexaw genddo gidi aggiis.

1.4. KOYRO GAAZEEXAA
Coraa haasayanaappe kasetidi ane, beni gaazeexay baynna wode sa''ay aymalakkonne be''os.
•	Woraqatay baawa giyogaa mala.
•	Odoy ha''iigaadan wodiyan wodiyan odettenna. 
•	La'an xaafiyogeenne ba qofaa qonccissiyogee biittaa wolqqan dargganttidi haaridaageetu huqqunaappe denddidaagan ubbakka qofettenna.
Ha nu nabbabiyo gaazeexay beni 17antto xeetu layttan Inggilandden pexi issi woraqatan ayfiyan geli qum''enna yo'ota qori shiisshshi kessin maxaafaa zal''anchchati bayzziyogaa. Ha zal''anchchati deriya naqaashaa koshshaa mishuwa be''idi eta koshshaa alanawnne he deriya ano biittan de'iya hasttamu laytta olaa dinnaaquwa allaalliya deriya nabbabissanaw bayzzoosona.

Inggilize biittaa xaafanchchati Naatinaa'eeli Butteeri, Toomaasa Arichcheerinne Niikoolaas Boorani wurssettan ha qommon qoxometta allaaletun amppidi oduwa xaafoosona. Ha asati 1641 layttan maattamuwa essi aggidosona. Hegaappe simmin heeraa oduwa qonccissiya xuufeti xaafettiyogaa doommidosona; yaatin hageeta eqettida galla galla gaazeexay xaafettiyogaa doommiis. 

Koyro Ingglizetto gaazeexay 'Londdone Gaazeexaa' geetettiyagee 1666 layttan maattamettiis. Hegee daro layttay aadhdhanaassi xekkaa naagidi kaw garuwan erettidi takkida gaazeexaa. 1690 layttan Bosttoona giyo maattamiyagee Benjjaamine Harisoy Amerkkaane koyro gaazeexaa maattamissiis. He gaazeexay 'Deriya Hanotaa Kareeninne Sooni,' yaagiyagaa. Ha gaazeexan de'iya issi allaallee kawo Piranissanne A machcheessi hanabaa yootees. Heede he biittaa haarida allaga biittay he gaazeexaa maattamuwa gorddidi teqqidi banttabaa kanchchiya qonccissiyanne bantta gutaraa halchchuwa biddaa kelkkiya gaazeexaa maattamuwan gede gelidosona.

Hegaappe kaallidi Jooni Kamppibeeli 1704 layttan 'Boston News Letters' yaagiya gaazeexaa maattamettaa doomminikka ha allaga biittaa huqqunay gallassa qamettin keehi sugidi sinttaw efanaw danddayibookkona. Laamiya olaa wurssetta heeran, Niyorkken allaga biittaa haariidaageetu hoolliya biddiya cora gaazeexati maattamettin giddo Amerikaane biittan daro layttaa maattamettiidi takkidosona. Ha allaga biittati he biitta huqqunidi haaridoogaappe denddidaagan he biittaa asay bari qofaa qaalanne qaattenaadan tucci oyqqidi bantta gutaraa hoolliya shociyo gina kanchchiya tohay biddidi Ingglize biittaara sigettidi la'atettaa demmanaashin xigidi oyqqidi banttabaa kanchchee bidettanaadan oottiidi takkidosona.
1.5. GAAZEEXAY AQOTAA KAAFIYOGAA
Miishshaa maattamuwappe kase gaazeexay aqotaassi immiyo kaafiya hagaa keena gaanaw danddayettenna. Ha gaazeexaappe geliya miishshay de'ees giyogaa. Hegaappe simmin bayzosinne shamaw maaddiya cora woraqata miishshay maattamettiis. Hegaadanikka heede diya gutaraa (polotikaa) equwanne asaa issipetettaa xekka qonccissiya gaazeexatu maattamoykka doometiis.

Haray qassi bantta oosuwa qaattaa erissanaw koyiyageetika gaazeexan maattamissi kessidi deriyassi erissidi bantta geliya miishshaa gujjidosona. Gaazeexatuppe dariya baggay ha bantta oosuwa erissidi geliya miishshaa dichchiya zal''anchchatu allaalliya qonccissees. Yunayttide Istteetisen baade gidenna asay issoy issuwara olan kambbaaseti simmin 1870 biidi 1900 laytta gakkanaashin ambban de'iya asay qoodan naa''u kushiya, kambban qassi heezzu kushiya diccin gaazeexaa koshshay asaappe daruwa ichchashu kushiya dicciis. He biittan ha gaazeexaa zal''ee wolqqaama woriya demissidi Amerikaa jorinaaliizime haydan aqotaassi xuussa gidiis.  
1.6. ODUWA SHIISHSHI GISHUWA
Beni wode oduwa gaazeexan xaafidi sohuwappe sohuwa dabidaabetto posttan kaaxidi gishettees. Gidoshin hegaappe simmin yo'oy aadhdhi wodhdhin gaazeexaa yelaga attuma naati ogiya gaxan yuushshiyogeenne ha oduwa woykko hanabaa siyana saamettida asay ha yuushshiya naappe shammi nabbabiyogee daro wodiyappe doommin meezetiis. Ha oduwa shishshuwa xeelliyagan odoy suyqiyan bayzettiyanne shamettiya shaqaxa mala. Ooratta odoy ha''i biron yiida maayuwappe aadhdhi koyettees. Wodee aadhdhido odoykka qassi daro laytta asi maayi takkin wodiyara beenna maayotudan asan ixettees. Wodee aadhdho odoy irxxa sasa shendderaa mala. Ha oduwa siyanaw asi hayqaychchas geenna. Oratta ododan oonee wodee aadhdhiichcho odossi pasotenna. Ha oduwa siyanawnne nabbabanaw asi ooninne buuxa geenna gishshaw wodala ganjjee ooratta oduwa sissanaw qammine galla baaxettees. Ha ooratta odoy keehippe al''onne siyanaw deree hayttaa corggochchidi naagiyogaa wodala ganjjee ammanettidi yaane haanne hasidi oduwa ha oduwa asaa sissanaassi baadees. Yaatiyo gishshaw odoy kafuwadan paallidi, horoophphpilliyaninne markkabiyan caanettidi issisaappe harasaa cuchchay malanaashin gakkees. Wodala ganjje ay garane geze kessennan oduwa (hanabaa) deriyass gattanaassi qamminne galla woxerettidi saluwa san diyabaa deriyassi shiishshi mucuuridi gattees. Odoy hagaa mala hanotay shiiqidi deriyassi gishettees.
1.7. DARGGIYA WODE MIIDIYA
Kase aadhdhaagaappenne Darggiya wodeegaappe diya dummatettay yesuwappe attin aybanne oorattabi deenna. Issitoo miidiya konttee tammu laytta miidiya dichchaa xeelliyagan hayyotoogaadan "ha wode gaazeexaaninne adhdhaa oyttamu layttaappe kase maattametta gaazeexan ayba dummatettinne baawa." (NRDC& CPSC, 1982b, p88). Hankko televizhzhiiniyanne iraaduwa miideekka hegaa mala. Ha''ikka ha miidee yesuwan kaseegaara issuwa, keehiippe tishsheena, sohuwan sohuwan zaarettidi issibaa xaafees, ha miidee biittaa dichchawkka denttettenna gishshaw nabbabanawkka wuttenna. Miide giyo miishshi biittaa dichchaa bolla ehiyo kaafee ubbakka qofettibeenna; ha aallaalliya xeelliyagan shiiqiya pisseekka yishkka gidenna shugo. Benibaappe attin ha''i ooratta tekinoojjiya eraara salonne sa'a. Ha gazeexan dariya baggi geediyobati de'oosona. Yamiya halchchuwanne pissiya kanchchiya biddaa kelkkees. 

Darggiya kawotettaa wode 'Serto Ader' giyo gaazeexay woykko ootti aqiya asaa xeelliyagan xaafeti kiyiyagee hankko ubbaappe sintta xeera gididi gishettees. Ha gaazeexay Toophphiya erettidi ootti asaa kontte yame gidin aatti aatti he yamiya halchchuwa hoolliya biddees. 1979 layttan eqqidi saaminttan issitoo Hamuusa gall galla kessidi qoodan 200000 gaazeexay gishettees. Markkisisttenne Leeninisttee gutaraa qaattaa sohuwan sohuwan xaafees. Koyro sinttan 'Serto Ader' yaagi Amaarattuwan xaafidi gidduwan muleera Markkisistte-Leeninisttee qofa xalaala guuppin giigees.
Ha ootti aqa asaa xeelliya gaazeexay he yamiya yaratussinne qofan etaara maayettiyageetussi eta sanssalataa macaraa maaran konttiya baggaara gakkees; haray qassi issi issi kotta konssoonotun gishettesppe attin gishanaw aawaatettaa ekkida asaw (maabaraw) imettenna.

Haray 'Abiyot police' geetettiya gaazeexaa gidishin ha gaazeexay 1961 laytta gakkanaashin heede diya kawotetaa polisiya halchchuwanne poluwa biddiyogaappe denddidaagaaninne danuwa pisseekka aani kiyiyo gishshaw daro asay nabbabees; qoodan 100,000 gaazeexay gishettees.

Simmidi 'Tatek' giyo gaazeexaa 1957 layttan saaminttan saaminttan Erissuwanne Deriya Meete Kaaletay  giigissin baadeti nabbabanaw issi kutti qoodan 28,000 gaazeexay muleera eta allaalle xalla biddiyo gishshaw etaw gishettees. 
1.8. 20tto XEETANTTA  LAYTAA GAAZEEXAA
1900 biidi 1920 layttatu giddon gaazeexay zal''ettanaadan issi maayettido maachchay polettiis. Hegaappe simmin ha gaazeexxaa zal''iyappe daro woree beettiis. Koyruwan ha gaazeexaa sohuwara maattamidi maashiniya tekinooloojje giigin issi kutta cora woraqataa maattamoy doomettiis. Naa''anttuwan bantta oottiyo kushe hiillaa woykko zal''iyogan woriya demmanaw gaazeexan bantta ooso qaattaa erissiya zal''anchchatu qooday keehi gujji gujji biis.

Hegaappe denddidaagan ha gaazeexaa yuushshoy keehiippe daro geliya miishshaa demmiyo oge gidiis. Heezzanttuwan zal''anchchati ushsha keettaa dooyiyogaadan, uteeliyan zal''iyogaadan gaazeexaa yuushshiyageetikka bantta oosuwan shukuluuliyoaa doommidosona. Hegaappe simmin 1919nne 1924 Niyorkke biittan dere asaa ufayssiya gaazeexay maattamettiyogaa doommiis. Hegeekka issi gaazeexaw bagga keena gididi qeeri woraqatan maattamettiya gaazeexaa. Pootuwara keehippe puulattidi garssaaranne bollaara asaa xellanaw lo''iya pootuwa gelissin he gaazeexay giigees. 
1.8.1. HEEDE DICHCHAA
1980 layttaa giddon Yunayttide Istteetisen gaazeexaa dichchay koyro doommiis. Hegeekka misiliyanne dumma dumma meraara diya gaazeexaa, qanttanne nabbabanaw injje, cora saaxineenne giraafeti de'iyogaanne garssan daro tumu yo'ota oyqqidaagaa. 

1.8.2. ULO MISHUWA QONCCISSIYA JORINAALIIZIMEYA
Ha ulo mishuwa qonccissiya jorinaalizimee higgiya allaalliya oduwa xeellin xeella xeella giyanne siyin siya siya giya kuushsha qofaa oyqqido gishshaw asay keehi saameti shammees. He gaazeexay hanabaa xoqqissi qonccissees, asaa wozanaa mishuwa kaashi laaliya, zigirssanne miidiya oosuwa erennan (issiban luxennan) geliyogaa bessees. Kamppibeeli (2001) ha gaazeexay cora galla galla hanabaa qonccissiya kuushsha yo'uwa, ispporttiyanne dumma dumma cora yo'ota oykkiya gaazeexaa yaagidi birshshiis. He gaazeexay he wodiyan issi moorettidabaa boriyogaa, luxennan gaazeexaa oosuwan geliyogaa  eqettiya, wogaa kanttiyogaa keehi ixxiyanne, issi polotikaa yamiya zokkuwa oykkiyogaa palqqiya gaazeexa. Ha gaazeexay asaa siyanaw ufayssiyanne miichchiya hanabata darotoo oyqqees. Pirankki Luzeeri Mooti (1941) ha gaazeexaw de'iya ichchashu eeshshaa hagaappe kaallidi xaafiis.
•	Kuushsha yo'uwa ayfe yo'uwa qoccissiya paca qofa qashuwa woykko qofa qashuwa koyro sinttan maattamiyogaa.
•	Coranne xeellanaw lo''iya misiletanne pootota oyqqees.
•	Cimo oysha, cimmiya ayfe yo'uwanne worddo luxobata go''ettiyogaa.
•	Kumetta meran, maattamettabaa geediyoganinne garanttiya (malaaliya) qofa qashuwa oykkida yafaraa bolli wudissiyagaa gidishin ha wodiya Yunayttide Istteetisen ha gaazeexay kiyees.
•	Diraamatoo giigidi issi yamiya worakaaba hanuwa qoncciya kessees. 
1.8.3. HA GAAZEEXAA QOHO MIYYIYA
ULO MISHO:-
•	Daroti hirggissiya (yashshiya) oduwa ha gaazeexan kessoosona.
•	Iita wogaa (qohiya meeziya) yedhdhi aadhdhennan kaashshi laaliyo wode he wogaawati ooni O wogaa toochchi giyogaa naa''u yaratu giddon kombbaasuwa denttees.
1.9. TOOPHPHIYA JORINAALE GAAZEEXAA DICHCHAA
Toophphiyan miide zamaana ogiyan eqoosappe 141 layttay adhdhiis. Afirikan bari xaafuwa bilaa dichchiya qoodan keehi guutta biitatuppe nu Toophphee issuwa. Hayda naqaashay qonccissi bessiyogaadan Toophphiyan koyro maattamiya maashiniya Turkke biittaa maashine hiillanchchay Hareytto Baynikeeri Maassaawa ambban de'iyagee 1963 layttan tokkiis. Ha maattamuwaw haggaaziyagaa geetettiya maashshinee Toophphiyan tohettoy bolaara ayssiya Teediroosa kawotetta wode, he kawoy wolqqaamanne erettidaagaa gidoogaappe denddidaagan 'Teediroosa Maattamo Haggaazaa' geetetti A sunttan ha maashshinee sunttettiis. Ha maashshiniya tossay nu Toophphiyo maattamo tekinooloojiya go''ettiyogan Arshsho Afrikan 1 ro  xekka, nu ano biittan 4 antto, salo gufanttuwan 46 antto xekka oottiis. 

Miisoonetu hoollee bantta ammanuwa aassiyogaanne sabbaa gidiyogaappe denddiddaagan eti maattamiyo ubbabay xaaxi waaxin ammanoora gayttida allaalle. Miisooneti Turkkeppe guye yiikkonne Turkketikka etaagaatto Gibitstseppe yiidi kerene ambban uttidi bantta ammanuwa aassanaw baaxettoosona. He heeran zal''ee lo''i qaaxxiyogaara gayttidaagan daro asay de'iyo gishshaw he asaassi maattamo haggaazaa immana giishshin hara baggaara maattamoy naanniis. Haray qassi maattamoy he heeraa allaana ambban Asimaranikka doomettin harati qofettibeenna gishshaw eta gakkibeenna. Hegaappe simmin issi layttappe guyyiyan Suwideta giyo hara miisooneti Asimaran 1886 layttan maattamo maashshiniya tokkidosona. 1995 layttaappe kase Minikuli geetettiya ambben guutta maattamo oosoy doomettiis. Tammanne udufuntta xeetu layttaa baggaa gakkanaashin Toophphiyan ammano allaalle kanchchiya oyqqa naqaashati dariya baggi maattamettoosona. Koyro maattamoy eqqidoy 1863 layttan Maassaawan Laazaristte miisoonee Abbaa Laarenzza Baynichchaara kaallida Siwudishe wonggeliya luxissiyagaa kiittay Maassaawan Manzzullo yaagiyo sohuwan 1885 layttan qiiba maattamo keettay eqqiis. Heede Hatstse Milileera kushettidi 1890 laytta giddon Piraanishiskkaane misoonee Bamaariidi ba maattamo zal''iya aassiis.1896 layttan I putiya maashshiniya go''ettidi issi giyan giyan Perenssetto-Amaaratto gaazeeexaa 'le Semayne a Itoophphpiya' yaagiya huuphphe yo'uwan inchchirichchaa harggiya eqqettiya gaazeexaa maattamees. Hegaappe simmin abbaa Barinaridi Hareren 'Le semaine a Ethiopia,' yaagiya gaazeexaa 1905 layttan giya payduwan payduwan maattamissiis. 

Simmidi Bilaata Gebire Igiziabiheri giyan giyan bari kushiyan xaafi giigissido gaazeexaa 1900 layttan giigissiis. Hegaappe simmiyo wode nu biittan koyo gaazeexay Aymiro geetettiyagee giigiis. Toophphpee zamaana maattamuwa doommidoy Naa''antto Milile wode Aymiro geetettiya gaazeexay 1895 layttan Amaarattuwan qaalan giigo wode. Ha gaazeexaykka issi giyan giyan maattamettees; issi giyan sintta 4, qoodan 24 gidiyagaa Anddiriyaasa Kanivaadiya geetettiya Giriikee giigissees. Ha gaazeexay biittaa siiquwanne bollaara ayssiyageetu qofaa keehiippe konccissees. Ha maattamissiyo gaazeexaa qoodaykka 200 gakkanaw dicciis. Hagee maattamuwa dichchiya nu biittan xaphphuwa yeddin asay nabbabanaw noocu gi ufayttiyo wode. Heede kawoykka hara garssaara de'iay dereekka nabbabuwan hekkaa demmin tamaari luxennan eraa xayoy biittaappe baqattin hara issi Biraanenaa Salaame geetettiya gaazeexay xaafetti giigin 500 gaazeexay maattamettin nu biittan gaazeexaa dichchay aakettaa gede geliis. 1927 layttan kiyida seeraa awaajjoynne heede maattamuwa xeelliyagan giigida seeray ha gaazeexaa dichchaw gittaa minttiis. 

Kase 'Merihaa Tibeb' geetettiyagee 1908 layttan eqaagee A garssan aqanaadan oosettin ha Biraaninaa Salaami giyo gaazexay 1927 layttan xekkaa naagidi gita maattamo keetta gididi kawonne buzo allaalleta maattamiyo haggaazaa immiidi takkiis. Heede Aymiro gaazeexay miishshaa metuwa, gaazeexaa maattamiyo woraqataa qaaxuwatuwanne Xaaliya olaa wode xuma wodiya aatti simmin kaalliya tammu layttatun wolqqaama laameenne dichchay biittan beettiis. Ha garssaara de'iya saaxiniyappe hegaa xeelli be''anaw danddayettees.

Asimara biittan Xaaliya kawotay issi giyan giyan giigiya 'Quirior Ertirea' yaagiya gaazeexaa 1936 laytta Ippiloogiraafike Maattamo Keettan attamissiis. Toophphiya wolqqan sugidi haaranaw qaaqida Xaalee kunddin 1941ppe biidi 1952 laytta gakkanaashin Xaaliya kawotay mootuwa denttin Biritishe kawoy Xaalliyassi pirddin 1984 layttan Darggee, baade kawotay Toophphpiya deriya heemmiyo wode, dumma dumma putiya maashshineta kooli giigissidi xaafiyobatanne haray atto shin kawo xaaduqotuura ubbay attennan maattamiyogaa doommiis. Hagaappe bollaara 'Ippiloogiraafee' dumma dumma gaazexata, maxiheeteta, Geeshsha Maaxafaanne qaalaa kochchaa maxaafata maattamiis. He wode maattamo keettaa sunttay 'Asimara Maattamo Keettaa' geetetti laamettidi gaazeexaa Eritera allaanaa xalaalan gidennan diishin biittaw huuphessa baggi Tigireeninne Gonddaren 1944 biidi 1956 layttaa gakkanaashin galla galla sinttaa naa''u Tigirettuwaninne Amaarattuwan gaazeexaa deriyassi ha bollan qonccida heeratun gishettesppe attin ubba heeraa gakkanaw danddayettibeena. 1956 layttan ''Hibret'' (Tigiretto) 1944 biidi 1970 gakkanaashin ''Contidiano Eritera'' (Xaalettuwan) 1978 layttaa heeran ''Toophphiya'' 1944ppe doommin ''Elete senbet'' giyageeti (naa''aykka Amaaratto) huuphessa Toophphpiya dalgga manttiyan gishettidosona. Ha woraqatatu xalaalay ha dalgga manttiya kambban de'iyageeti ooni erii tamaaribeenna yimma gidiyogaappe denddidaagan nabbabi erokkonna giidi qoppiyo gishshataassa. Yo'uwa qassi zamaana timirttee ehido ooso ayfee loddaara daro laamiya ehiis. Hara baggara qassi seeraa anqqetstsee dalgga manttiya allaalliya wudissiyo gishshaw he heeraa deriyassi asay qoodan guutta nabbabiyageetu wozanaa koshshaa alanaassi gaazeexay giigiis. Biraaninaa Selam maattamoy 1965 layttan keehippe aakkidi bin maattamiyageeti keehippe aakkin keehippe koshshiya miideti doomettin 1950 layttaappe 1960 doomettan wodiyan Afirikaa ikkonoomiya koomiishinee (1958)nne Afirikaa issipetettay (1963) gaazeexaa maattamiya yameti naa''u tohuwan eqqido wode. Heede Toophphee olan kombbaasettiyo wode gaazeexaa mucuuridi giigissuwan erettida xaafanchchay, Woldde Gorggis Woldde Yohaannis, 'Toophphiya jorinaalizime aawa geetetti xeessettiis. A sunttay Biraannaa Salaame gaazeexaaranne Addis Zemene gaazeexaara ohetti uttiis. Hegaappe kaallidi Gonddare Maattamo Keettay, Gonddare ambban Tisaase 14, 1965 M.L. eqqin he heeran maattamo haggaazay pol''atti laa'iis. Ha maattamiya yamee Gonddare ambbaa giigisso keettaagaa gidishin Biraane Salaame Maattamoynne Geeshsha Tirintte Kaatediraale maattamoti woriya ha maattamo keettaara shaakki oottoosona. Hegee Gonddarenne Goojjaame heeran de'iya kawo polissiyageetussinne oosanchchatussi ha''issaw go''ettiyo sanadiya, Vawchcheriya, erisso karddiya maattamanaw xuussa gidiis. Heede 1967 M.L. 'Tiyintte Gonddare' yaagiya gaazeexay maattamettiis. Yaatin hagee issi layttappe guyyiyan he sohuwan eqqi attin 'Felege Abiyot' geetettiya naa''antto zaarettidi maattamiyogee Masqqala aginaa 2, 1970 M.L. doomettiis. He wode gaazeexay kawotaa kaaletuwanne timirttiya deriyassi laa'ettiyogaa dariya baggi qonccissees.
1.10. BUZO MAATTAMO ALLAALETUPPE POXETTAA
Dumma dumma cora maattamettabati 1935 layttaappe kase polettidosona. Ha xaafetti giigiya gaazeexay kawobaa, misoonetuugaanne issi issi ammano allaalliyara gayttidaagan kare biittaa asati giigissidoogaa gidiyo gishshaw etaagaa. Usuppune 15, 1934 layttan Toophphiya bollaara ayssiya Hayle Silaasee maaxaafaanne gaazeexaa maattamuwa kawotaa oychchi anttissanaadan awaajjuwa kessiis. Ha awaajjoy giigissiyageetussi anttanaw hagaappe kaalliya yo'ota kunttanaw bessiyogaa mala qonccissees. Ichchashu layttaa (1936-1941) gakkanaashin Xaalee Toophphiya oyqqido wode, gaazeexaynne hara xaafettabati dariya baggi he huqquna kawotaa oosuwa buussaa qonccissoosona. Ha xigidi wolqqan darggantti oyqqida kawotay issi asaw ba buzo xaafi giigissiyobaa anttenna. Dottoree Malkkaamu Bayyani (Geediyagee) Toophphiya, Syliiviya Pankkihuret 'Toophphiyanne Ooratta Wodiya' giyagaa giigissoogee ha huqqunaa gaasuwan atti aggiis. He wodiyan gaazeexan misiletanne koshshiyabata xaafettenna mala ha allagaa biittaappe yi haarida tumukka gi uttaageeti Toophphiyan maattamoy diccenna mala xeellin beettiya daafaa gattidosona (Aforqqa 1983:28).

Simmidi la'atettaa wodiyan (1936-1941) ha huqqunaa gaasuwa kunddida maattamuwa zaarettidi essiyogeenne issi asi bari qofaa xuufiyaninne haasayan qonccissanaw la'atettay beettin ha buzo xaafanchchata anttiyogee 1924 (1934 E.C.) zaaretti biittaa ano seeraa giigissanaw 1974 (Isiine 30, 1966 M.L.) ha ano seeraa xeelliyagan yaa'ettin 'Addis Zemen' yaagiya gaazeexay Laappuniya aginan 1975 (Laappune 18, 1967 M.L.) cora gaazeexatinne hara xuufeti ikkonomiya, gutaraa, issipetettaanne ammanuwa xeelliyagan xaafettidi qoncciya kiyiyogaa doommidosona. Erissuwa moconay issi maattametta maxiheetenne gaazeexay kawobaa woykko buzo gi shaakkiyogee attenna yaagin dumma dumma maattamo oosoti polettidosona. (Kaplan 1971: 326-327) yaatin kawonne buzo maattamo keettati dummattidi haggaazaa imuwa doommidosona. Ha hanotay Toophphiya jorinaaliizimee zaarettidi yeletti xaphuwa yeddanaadan Hayle Sillaasee aawatettaa yeddiyo wode oosuwan pe'iis. Hegaappe simmin (1974-1991) layttatun Dargge kawotettay issi buzo maattamoynne polettennaadan naa''antto seeraa minttin ha''ikka zaaretti maattamo oosoy hayqqi aggin 1987 layttan kiyida ano seeran (Dimokiraase Repabilike Toophphiya anqqatste 49) maaran ha huqquna kawotaa polotikaa hoolliya maayettennaagaappe denddidaagan maattamo oosoy guyye simmiis. Heede Uddufune 28, 1991 layttan EPRDF Adisaaba oyqqin ay asinne la'atettan xaafannanne haasayana mala anttettiis. Hegaappe simmin Toophphiya buzo maattamoti ba muccuuri xaafiyobati giyan bayzzettidi zal''ettanaadan kawotay kaafiya immiis.

Yaatin hara salo gufanttuwa xaafetti mucureti bayzzetibatudan nu biittaanikka gaazeexatinne maxiheeteti bayzzettinne shamettiyogee doomettin deriyassi de'iya issipettettaa, gutaraa, wogaa dichchaa koshshaa oyshshaa tilla zaaro gidiis. Ha buzo giyaw pinnidoogee nu biittan gaazeexay, maxiheeteenne hara hara xaafetti bayzzettiyageetu dichchaasi baaso gidiis. Yaati issi kutti dumma dumma buzzo maattamettabati nu biittan gutaraanne aqotaa deriyassi qonccissanaw humbbuli gi aggiis.

Hegee asay bari wozanan siyettabaa xaafi kessiya gaazeexaykka maattamettitidi deriyassi haggaazaa immana malanne nu biittaa maattamo inddussitireekka diccidi geliya miishshaa aassanaw lo''o oge gididoogee erettidabaa. Buzo maattamoti gaazeexaynne maaxiheetee asaassi siyettibaa xeelliya odota xaafi kessoosona. Ha maattamoy issitoo issitoo daro laafa yo'otu bolli, palqqiya woykko gaadettiya odotu bolli, worddonne iitiyabatu bolli wudissees. Hagee nu biittan jorinaaliizime eraa pacaanne ha hiillan hekkay pacidoogaa bessees. Toophphiyan oonikka xaafanawnne nabbabanaw danddayikko jorinaalistte kiyanaw danddayees; hegee qassi nu biittaa issibaassi de'iya hiillaa enaninne biittaawtettaa maataa naagiyogaa bessees. Xekkaa naagida gaazexatanne maxiheeteta dumma dumma meraninne qottan giigiyogee bari huuphen bana danddayida biittay era hiillan ammanettiyogaa qonccissees. Hegaappe denddidaagan qoodan unddenna xaafettabati issi miishshata godati zal''anchchati bantta deriyassi erissanaw jorinaalisttetuura issippe gidin polettiis.

Yaatin dumma dumma miideti la'a-giyan bayzzetti shamettidi ba ooso ayfiya woykko woriya demmidi cora maattamettabata giyan peeshshidosona. Ha maattamettiyabata buzo bari oosuwa qaattaa deriyassi erissidi daro oosuwa oottidi woriya demmiyogaa koyidi erissanaassi ha gaazexaanne maxiheetiya go''ettoosona; hegan banttaa de'iya wozanaa koshshaa qonccissoosona. Koyidobaakka banttassi injjettiya ogiyan la'atettan qonccissanaw danddayoosona. Jimila zal''anchchati bantta oosuwa qaataa erissanaw gaazeexaa ooso miishshadan go''ettoosona. Bantta oottanau koyobaakka la'atettan liiqo inxxarssan geliya keenaa bidissidi asaassi wozanaa kahaa bashshidi ha gaazeexay etassi kushe miishsha gidiis. Ha zal''anchchati kushiya yeddoogee bari huuphen gaazeexay deriya giddon laa'anaadan bana danddayida gaaso gidiis. Gaazeexaa gishuwa bollikka ha zal''achchatu kushiya yedoy wolqqaama jette kiyiis. Ha jimila zal''anchchatu hoolliya dumma dumma meran leeleessidi pootuwaninne misiletun giigissiyogee etassikka ay asakka nabbabanaassi wuttiyo gishshaw ooninne maattamettibata shammiyogaanne nabbabiyogaa keehippe guyye geenna. Hagee qassi gaazeexaa zal''iya keehi sinttaw efiis. Ha gaazeexan corabati giigidi sohuwan sohuwan maattametti kiyiyoogee oosuwa boolimaanne oosoti era hiillan amppetti giigiyogaa keehippe darissoppe attin oonee gede zaari coo ta erays gi xaafiyogaa nabbabiyogaappe denddiaagan tumanne worddo oosota shakki qonccissi kessiyogee shuggiis.

1.11. QANTTA QOFAA
•	Koyro gaazeexay 'the acta durna' geetettiyagee Ooromaa biittan maattamettiis.
•	Deriya gaazeexay koyro gakkidoy 1830 layttaa giddon Benjjaami 'Days of New York Sun' yaagiyagee miishshaa maattamauwassi koyro.
•	Uluwa mishuwa qonccissiyo gaazeexay doomettoy asaassi de'iya wozanaa mishuwa, asaa koshshaa alanaassinne dumma dumma misiletun wozaa qooqissiyogaassidi nabbabuwassi wuttanaasa.
•	Xaafoy doomettanaappe kase issibaa malaataa woykko misiliya hebaa sohuwan gelissi go''ees.
•	Ooratta odoy ha''i biron yiida ooratta maayuwa mala koyettees; aadhdhichchida odoy qassi wodee aadhdhido maayuwa mala oone  A siyanaw koyenna.
•	Toophphiyan miidee zamaana ogiyan eqqoy 141 layttappe kase.
•	Nu biittan koyro gaazeexay 'Aymiro' geetettiyagaa.
•	1927 layttan kiyida kawotaa ano seeraa awaajjoy nu biittan gaazeexaa dichchaw gittaa minttiis.
•	Toophphee olan kambbaasettiyo wode gaazzexaa muccuuri giigissuwan erettida xaafanchchay Woldde Gorggis Woldde Yohaannis, Toophphiyan jorinaalizime aawa geetettiis.


NAA''NTTO SHEMPPUWA
                     NAQAASHAA SHISHSHI ODUWA GIIGISSUWA
1.3.	Naqaashaa Shiishuwa_odoy dumma dumma ginaara pulttottuppe yees. Wodala ganjjee oduwa hasiyo wode aduwa ucciyogaadan woykko worqqaa demmana gakkanaashin biittaa duge zaari bookkiyogaadan hanabaa demmana gakkanaashin koyees. Wodala ganjjee bari koyidobaa (hanabaa) demmanaashin cora hiillaa salettennan go''ettees. Wodala ganjjee hanabaw pultto gidiya asa keetttaa penggiya qoxxees, baassi gidiya naqaashaa demmana gakkanaashin yaanne haanne hasettaa bichchaarees. Wodala ganjjee hanabaw pultto
Naqaashshaw pultto yo'oti de'oosona. 
•	Oyshaa
•	Xeelaa
•	Xaaduquwa
Asaa, hanabaanne allaalliya naqaashaa shiishshiyo wode wodala ganjjee kase hani aadhdhabaa, pilggettaa, oyshaa sitta be'obaanne xaaduquwa pilggees. Wodala ganjjee siree baynna, boolimanne kumetta pissiya shiishshanaw ha issi issi hiillaa hayyota go''ettanaw bessees.
1.4.	Oyshaa_ Oyshay wodala ganjjeenne pultto gidiya asa oychchin zaaruwaw immiyo naqaashaa. Oyshi baynnan naqaashi shiiqiyo wodee mulekka baawa gaanaw danddayettees. Ha wodiyan oduwa shiishoy dariya baggi oyshaana gidiyogee erettidabaa. 

Jorinaaliizime oosuwa xalaala giddennan diishin hara eranchchatu oosuwakka naqaashaa asaappe (pulttotuppe) oychchi go''eteettees. Ha oychchiyo macarati zoriyassi, oosuwan gelissanaassi (moodanaassi), hayyuwa (qofaa) ekkanaassi, xaliyassi, luxettaa pilgganaassinne haratussa. Nuuni jorinaale oyshaa giyogee he sohuwan beettenna jamay oychchin zaariyo haasayan naqaashaa oychchi qoriyagaa. Hegeekka kase ha oychchiyo allaalliya xeelliyagan ha oyshettiya izaawssi kase eray (hekkay) de''ana danddayees. Ha oosuwa buussan, wodala ganjjiyassi hoollee kumetta, tillanne gida naqaashaa shiishshiyogaa. Lo''o oyshay sissaanne ero kanchchiya gidennan diishin deree ezgganaadan yeemoyees, boolimanne deriya garanttiya xuuraa kaashi laalees.

Wodala ganjjee shiishshiyo oyshay keehiippe akeekkan gididaagaa gidanaw bessishin hanabaa qommuwan dummattanaw danddayees. Haray qassi tilla hooliyaninne qanttan I oychchiyogaappe kase eriyo cora qommo hanabati de'oosona. 
Oduwan Hanabaa_ oduwan hanabaa oyshay kulkka hoollee; wodala ganjjee ba xaafanaw koyidobaassi kaafiya naqaashaa shiishshiyogaa. Oduwa xaafiyo maaran mankkan keten''i eqqidi A oyshay ooni, awde, ayssi, awaaninne issitoo issitoo waanidi hanabay polettidaakko ammaneti eranaassa.
Oduwa Daashaa_ oduwa daashan hanabay muletoo waani woykko ayssi kase hani kanttabaa oossi woykko aybi hanidaakko ha oduwa daashay hanabaa kaalli bessees.
Oduwa Sinttaa_ hagaa mala oyshaa muletoo wudissiyoy izaawussi pootuwa woykko misiliya ekkiina. Bitanee (mishiriya) jamaa garssan erettida asa gidikko wodala ganjjee issibaa ooraxxissi koyanaw bessees. Qassi bitanee erettenna asa gidikko wodala ganjjee bitaniya misiliya medhdhanaw koshshees.
Pilggo Hanabaa_ pilggo hanabay ''waanidi?''nne ''ayssi?'' giya oyshatussi zaaruwa immees. Hagaa mala hanabay darotoo jorinaalee eranaw koyiyobaassa. Wodala ganjjee hanabaassi issibaa eranaw koyidi demmido hanabaa pilggees. Wodala ganjjee ha shiishshido naqaashaappe, zoriyappe, pilggettaappenne oyshaappe kessees.
1.5.	Xeelaa_ Jorinaale xeelay wodala ganjjee be''idi, siyidi, singgidi, laacidinne oykki xeellidi hanabaa demmiyogaa. Hanabaa oosuwan xeelay hanabaa oduwassi woykko daashshaw meraa immees. Hegaappe denddidaagan wodala ganjjee koyrotidi hanabaa he sohuwa gakkidi be'ees. Wodee woykko sohoy injjettana xaykko wodala ganjjee naqaashaa silkkiya shocidi naa''antto kushiyappe ekkees; yo'uwan qassi wodala ganjjee bari ayfiyan sohuwa gakki be'i xaafiyo naqaashay hanabaa oduwassi keehiippe puulaa immees; muleera hanabay boroyennan shiiqanaadan maaddees; ha hanabay, siyanawkka (nabbabanawkka) keehi asaa yeemoyees. Wodala ganjjee tilla waabee googaa boroshshennan wotti aggiyo wode jamay A haasaya siyanaw danddayees; eti siyiyo wode ha oduwassi waabee haasayidinne oyshaw zaaruwa immidi bessiyo bolaa qaattaa (gesture), I bolli bolli haasayiyo qaalaa  woykka paca qofa qashuwa (mannerism) qanttan ha bitaniyappe asay yiilluwa woykko noocu guussaappe ezggiya jamay yo'uwa akeekanaw danddayees. Xeelay hanabaassi meraa immees; hegaa giyogee xeelay ha ezggiyo hanabaw misiliya medhdhees gaanaasa. Qommon sima huuphe yo'uwan qonccidoogaadan oyshaw bana danddayida hoolleenne qanttan he oychchiyo allaalliyassi hekkay de'iyogaadan xeellanawkka ha yo'oti attennaba. Wodala ganjje asi hanabaa polissishin be'anaw koykko he yo'oy polettishin woykko issibaa asi oottishin he sohuwan beettana bessees. Jorinaaleti muletoo naa''u bagga xeelaa xeelloosona.
Shaakkenna Xeelaa: - hagee koyro xeelaa gidishin hanabay polettiyode he sohuwan beettidi bana xeelliya allaalliya qoriyo xeelaa, dariya baggi wodala ganjjeti ha xeelan go''ettoosona. Leemisuwaw: -Ispporttiya allaalliya xeelliyogee kuwaasee kaa''ettiyo wode dembbaa gelees; miishshaa allaalliya aattiya wodala ganjjee layttan zal''iya xeelliyagan tobbido yaa'aa xeellees, diraaman geeddiyagee he diraamay be'ettiyo wode jamaara issippe b'ees. Parilaamaa wodala ganjjee parilaamaara issippe konssooniyo wode geli uttees. Hagee awdenne oduwa oosuwan meezetido allaalle. Wodala ganjjeti ubbatoo issibay haniyo wode woykko polettiyode be'oosonappe attin porogiraamiya shaakkokkona; woxxi qaaxxabaa xeelloosonappe attin bantta hoolliya halchchuwara issippe biya yo'uwa demminneekka qarphphi ootti oyqqinnee xaafiigoosona. Wodala ganjjee cora hiillatun go''ettidi dumma dumma hanabata xeellees. Parilaamaa pissiya bolli hara aaro aadhdhanaw bessiyabaa caridi, chilootan danuwa, ispporttiyanne diraamaa, kosha eqettiyo keehi wolqqaama salppiyaninne hegaara gayttida deree siyiyo sohotuninne issi yamiya qofaa kaafiyo salppiya garssi gelidi hanabaa deriyassi xaafanaw bessees. Qonccissi odiyobatinne poletabati doorettanaw koshshees ayssi giikko doorettidi hanabaa kaafettanaw bessees. 
Shaakkiyo Xeelaa: - Wodala ganjjeti issitoo issitoo banttana erissennan yaa'ay woykko jamay tobbiyo allaalliya naqaashaa shiishshanaw he porogiraamiya shaakkoosona. Wodala ganjjeti qasho keettan keettaa pittiyagaattonne huuphe garssa sahuwa hosppitaaliyan pilggiyo kifiliya gelidi kaalli banttana erissennan naqaashaa ekkana danddayoosona. Hegaa mala hanotan asay eti wodala ganjje gidiyogaa eridi issi issi gede coo combbayidi haasayiyo haasayaappe naagettoosona. Wodala ganjjetu oosoy asi eqettiyonne bala gi boriyo oosota qoncciya kessees (kaashi laalees). Sohuwa biidi naqaashaa xeelli shiishshiyogee wodiya keerettidi biidi naqaashaa pilggiyo wodee 60ninne 70 layttaa wodiyana gidikkonne ha"i wodiyan bana erissennan bi naqaashaa shiishshoy cora wodala ganjjetinne eta oosuwa geediyageeti mereto gishshaw atti atti bes. Haray qassi wodala ganjjetussi de'iya maaray mankkay bana qottiyogaa anttenna. Eti ha sohuwa biidi xeelliyogeekka maara hanabaa misiliya siyiyanne nabbabiyageetussikka qonccissennan ixxanaw danddayees. Hanabaa koyro kochchoora haruwara xeelliyogee wodala ganjjeta: -
•	Hanabaa muleera issibaynne attennan qoncciyan asaabaa, sohuwanne polettidabaa ho''o ododan asaassi aattanaw danddayissees.
•	Harati wottido huqqunaa baqiya qoncciyan allaallee xelliyo kifiliyassi erissanaw danddayissees.
•	Waabetuppe beettenna naqaashaa demmanaadan oottees.
•	Nabbabiyageetussi woykko siyiyageetussi hanabay huuphiya kahan merettanaadan oottees.
•	Oduwa hanoy saro, woppanne ufayssiyagaa gidissanaw danddayissees.
1.6.	Duuqettabaa Go''ettiyogaa
Wodala ganjjeti kase duuqetta kawobaanne kawo gidenna yametu allaalliya nabbabidi woykko ezggidi awdenne gayttenna odo naqaashaa demmanaw danddayoosona. Ha naqaashay darotoo xaaduquwappe beetteesppe attin oyshan woykko xeelan beettennan ixxanaw danddayees. Ha duuqettabaa go''ettiyogee wodala ganjjiyassi kase hanabaw de'iya eraa demmanaassi keehi maaddees. Galla galla shiishshiyo pissiyassikka keehi maaddees. Issi issi pilggiyo projekitiyassikka wolqqaama kaafiya immees. Leemisuwassi pirdda keettan chilootan ootti kanttabaa duuqqi wottoogee de'ikko wodala ganjjee A zaarettidi xeellidi daro koshshiya naqaashaa demmana danddayees. Duuqetabati ha aadhdha dere akeekenna kanttiichchidaagaa zaarettidi eranaw keehippe lo''o miishsha. Cora qommo deriyabaa qonccissiya naqaashati doosona. Hageeta demmanaw wodala ganjjee eti de'iyosaanne oossi aybi de'i giyogaa eranaw bessees. Issitoo issitoo waabeti ha duuqetta naqaashata demmiyo ginaa wodala ganjjetussi qonccissoosona. Haray qassi waabee ha naqaashaa wodala ganjjiyassi woygiyakko aybaa xeelliya allaallee duuqettidaakkonne qonccissiyo hanotaykka de'ees. Leemisuwaw miishshaa oosuwara gayttidaban hanaban balay beettikko ha allaalliyan luxi loohida eranchchay wodala ganjjee giigissanaadan assi ginaa bessees.
1.7.	Duuqettabatu Qommuwa
Wodala ganjjetussi ha duuqetta naqaashaa demmiyo eray woykko hiillay de'anaw bessees. Darotoo deriyabaa duuqin (xaafetti uttin) wodala ganjjee goettiyobat: -
Maachchanne Xaafetabata: - xaafettidanne teeppiyan duuqetabati dere konssoonota, asi siyiyobata, pirdda keettaa allaalleta, issi issi hara yaa'atun tobettabata.
•	Maaci kanttobati darotoo tobettabaw kuushshaa oyqqoosona.
•	Xaafetabati deree tobbidi kuushshaw gakko yo'ota ubbaa xaaxi waaxi oykkoosona.
Xaafeta Miishshata: - miishshaa kessiyanne oottanaw go''ettiyobati leemisuwaw: - maashshiniya hiixay (tossay), keettay, keettay uttido sohoy zawan shaahettidaagee, shametto gatee, simmidi qassi bayzziyo gatee, eta qoodaa maaraara, ha ubba xaafetabati naqashadan go''ettanaadan maaddoosona. 
Aqaafiya: - Issi ooso miishshay obaakkonne, heede ooni he yamiya kaalettidaakkonne, oosanchchatu sunttay he yamiyassi de'iya halchchoy h.h.m. xaafi wotto naqaashshay simmi xaaduqoto go''ettanaadan maaddees.
Pirdda Keettaa Payliya: - daanatu maatafay wodhdhin maayettobati, daronne saro asatu mazggabay, higgee, piddaa kuushshay imettobay, dano oosuwa qoncciyagan daanatinne hara yarati (allaallee xeelliyogeeti) maayettidi paramettobati, mooranchchaa qonccissiyagan xaafettabati oosanchchatunne erachchatu qooday mooroy baynna asati chilootan palametti shatimobati, pirdda keettaa azazo woraqatati, xeessa woraqatati, pirddi kanttobati h.h.m. Simmidi naqaashattoo go''ettanaw maaddoosona. 
Miishshaa Mazggabaa: - ha mazggabay layttaw dayettida baajjeetiya, aginan aginan qanxxo damoozaa, wolqqa oosuwa oottissidi qanxxobaa, geliyanne kiyiya miishshaa, miishshaa go''ettoogaa geedidi pilggo pissiya, vawuchcheriya, sanadiya, peerooliya, keesiya sanadiya, konttiraatiya oottisso maachchaa, h.h.m. xaafetti uttoosona. 
Izaawu Naqaashaa: - issi oosanchchaw yeletta layttaa, mattumaa, ekko gelo hanotaa, azinaa woykko machcheeppe shaahetto maachchaa, layttan shemppo gallassaa, gakka metuwa, anttettidi oosuwappe kiyo wodiya, oosuwappe atto gallassaa, moori maqqacetti kanttobaa, buzo hayttaw haydaw oottobaa, ooso meeziya, eeshshaa, minno miyyiya, paca miyyiya, hayqqo wodiya h.h.m. xaafetti uttoosona.
Antettaa: - issi asi kaamiya laagganaw hinxxaa, keexxanaw, zal''anaw, ushsha keettaa dooyanaw, seeraa haggaazaa deriyassi immanaw, quma keettaa dooyanaw, suyqiya dooyanaw ha ubbaassi anttiyo (eeniyo) woraqatay imettin A bolli maqqacettidobay, giiraa qanxxoogee, siraaway, harshshuushiya malkkachcay, eeshsha metoy diikko maqqacetti kanttobay, dumma dumma loohissota ekkido markka woraqatay hagee ubbay xaaxi waaxin xaafetti uttees.

Issi issi mazggabati galla galla polettoosona. Leemisuwassi: Xaacee galla galla qashettidaageetanne birshshettida asaa mazggaban xaafi oyqqees. Ha mazggabata wodala ganjjee yiidi hagee deriya maaddees hagee qassi deriya xeellenna allaalle gi pilggidi baassi go''iya naqaashaa demmees. 

Wodala ganjjeti issi issi daafaanne danuwa teqqanaw xaafettabati deriya go''ees giidi qoppobaa pilggi xeellidi gaazeexan woykko oduwan deriyassi aattees.
•	Issi issi naqaashata shiishsha wodala ganjjeti he yo'oy xeelliyo asata woykko eranchchata oychchikko etassi ooninne eenidi qonccissees. Wodala ganjjiyassi chii! Hagee tana xeellenna giidi yiilluwan zaaruwa immiyogee daro pokko ayssi giikko I dere harshshuushiyanne dumma dumma dichchaassi xube gidiyabata pagalanaw deriya yara gididi qamminne galla waayettiya asa. I nu erennabaa oychchikko onakko woykko onakka oychcha yaagidi allaallee xeelliyo izaawa malaateettees.
•	Ha shiiqida naqaashati wodala ganjjiya woykko jorinaaliya sirissanaw danddayoosona. Hegeekka worddo naqaashay ohettabaa gidikko allaalee xeelliyo kifiliya (asaa) oychchidi tumaa shaakkees. 'Shutidabay cooshshiidi keha' wodala ganjjee ay laallanttiya qofi de'ikkonne cuchchay melanaashin allaallee xeelliyo kifiliya oychchidi geeshshi eranaw bessees. 
•	Issi asa wogi baynna ogiyan mootobati ubba coo sunttaa moorobati, hegaanne hegaa malatiyageeta wodala ganjjee koshshennabaa gidikko oychchi shaakkidi diggirggees/kessiichchees. Hegaa oottanaappe kasetidi allaalliyassi Diya tumaa woykko wordduwa kalkkottenna mala pultto gidiya asappe oychchi shaakkees.
1.8.	KASE ERAA
'Malvviina Manchcheeroy' 'News Reporting and Writing' giya hosppuntta yuushuwan maattametta maxaafan kase eraw heezzu birshshettaa immiis.
•	Minjjo eraa: - Wodala ganjjeee kase daro wodiya oosuwan takko meeziyappe demmo eraa gidishin kase meeze baynnan coo mela wodala ganjjee naqaashaa shiishshees giyogee aybbanne sinttaw kiyiyo gini baynna daafura.
•	Issi issi xaafetti mucurettabati giigi uttikko nabbabidi eraa qashamanaw danddayees. Kase eray xaykko wodala ganjjiya oosoy para gaariyadan sitta yafara kanchchiya oyqqidi bees. Corabaa eranaw danddayenna. Wodala ganjjiyassi hana keenaa woxxi qaaxxabaw eray de'ana xaykko I oottiyo oosoy keehi puridi sinttaw baanaw danddayenna.
•	Pultto gidiya asi immanaw koyenna naqaashatikka de'anaw danddayoosona. Waabee bari sheniyan asaw immanaw woykko yootanaw woga ootti naagettiyobatikka de'oosona. 
Wodala ganjjiyassi naa''u qommo kase eray de'anaw bessees. Hegeekka ubba ginanne sitta eraa. 
Ubba Gina Eraa: - wodala ganjjee bari oosuwaw go''ettiyo corabaa eriyogaa. Ha eray beettiyoy loytti nabbabin, ooso meeziyappenne timirtte luxeettaappe. Ane Malvviina Maxaafaappe ubba gina eraa leemisuwa be'oos.
Leemisuwassi issi wodala ganjjiya lasttiqe paabirikay taman xuugettoogaa siyada naqaashaa ekkanaw koyada ba oosuwa geediyagaassi yaagaasu. Ane taani baada ha tamaa xuussaa daafay waani gakkidaakko shaakkays. Paabirkkay keexxettanaappe kase he metoy inddustture mooteeyye paabirkkay keexxetti simmin inddustture moota kiyidee? Taassi hegaa heeran siree de'ees gaada oychcha siranaw bari beeruwappe kiyada he sohuwa baasu. Ha yo'uwa A pilggiyo gaasoy kase issi paabirkkay keexxettiyo sohoy inddustture mootaappe attin asi diyo heeran gidenaagee erettees. Yaatiyo gishshaw ha wodala ganjjiya kase eran amppada hanabaa pilggawsu. Hegaa gishshaw hanabaw ubbawkka kase eray koshshees giyogaa. Hegaa giishin issibaa cora baggaara eriyogee wodala ganjjiyassi daro lo''o yaaganaasa.
Sitta eraa: - issibay saynisiya woykko tekinoolloojiya gidanaw danddayees; ha yo'uwa wodala ganjjee luxidi eranaw danddayees. Wodala ganjjee koyro goshshanchcha, asttamaare, tamaare, hisaabe oosanchcha, kaamiya laaggiyagaa, mehe henttanchcha woykko pootuwa denttiyagaa gidanaw danddayees. Yaatiyo gishshaw wodala ganjjiyassi issibaw koyro luxi loohidi erido eray de'anaw danddayees. Hegee sitta era geetettees.

Hegaappe aadhdhidi wodala ganjjiyassi (jorinaaliyassi) danddayetta keena ubbabaassi woykko woxxi qaaxxabaa eray, hekkaynne meezee de'ikko lo''o. Aybissi giikko A eray ubbasan hanabaa deriyassi geema xuuraa deriyassi kaashi laallees. Hegaassi assi cora macaraara (yaara haara) eraa qashamanaagee attennabaa. I yaappe haappe shiishshido eray polotika, Toophphiya Pederaale maaraa mankkaa, etassi pederaale kawotettaara de'iya meetiya, danuwa oottaageeta qachchi birshshi tamaarissi zuuqi zaariya bilaa, dere asaa wogaa, parilaaman doorettida bonchchettida deriya tachchidaageeta moorikko etassi kawo seeraa haggaazaa waati immiyakko, ha deree dooridoogeetu maata, eta oosuwa kawo miishshaanne aqotaa maara mankkaa, kase hani kantta haydaa, Toophphiya asaa kochchaa wogaa (issoy issuwara milatiyonne dummattiyogaa), ha wodala ganjjiyassi issi sitta eraakko simmiyode, ane parilaamaa pissiya qoppos. Leemisuwassi: ha pissiya wodala ganjjee giigissiyo wode assi qommonne xade zoreta keettaa, eta maataynne ooso beeray dummatettaynne gaytotay ha wodala ganjjiyassi qoncce gidanaw bessees. Issi kawotaanne deriya garssan kombbaasuwa denttiya moorobay de'ikko diggirggidi ay ufurinne baynna hanabaa deriyassi sissees woykko xaafidi nabbabissees. Yaatiyo gishshaw senkko gidabaa pilgganaassi koyro kochchooro wodala ganjjiyassi deree doorido zoreta keettaassinne pedereeshshine zoreta keettaassi (eta oosuwa xeelliyaga) eray woykko hekkay de'anaw bessees. Wurssettan ane manttaa Dolassi issibaw sitta eray de'iyogaa hagaappe kaallidi be'os.

Wodala ganjjiya Dola Xoonni koyro pootuwa denttiya eranchcha. Simmidi ha oosuwan geliidi kaamiya daafan asi qohettin he daafay poletto sohuwa biyo wode kaamiya ogiyappe gaxan daafay gakkoogaa tiraafikiya pootuwappe be'idi he daafan balay de'iyogaanne baassi kaamiya laagganaw anttetta ogiyappe gaxaara ba shenaa hano gi laaggidi asa bolla qohuwa gattoogee bala gidiyogaa mala hanabaa deriyassi qonccissiis. Ero, ane A izaawussi koyro pooto eray baynnaakko ha daafaa gattida kaamiya laaggiyagaa wodala ganjjee Xooni waati deriyassi qonccissidi hanabaa xaafanaw danddayii? Yaagiya oyshaassi A koyro pootuwa denttiya eranchcha gidiyogee maaddiis.
2.7. WAABIYA/PULTTUWA
Pultto giyogee asa, xaaduqo woykko duuqetta naqaashaa wodala ganjjee oduwassi woykko hanabaw go''ettobaa gidanaw danddayees. Wodala ganjjee pulttoy baynnan odonne hanabaa deriyassi shiishshees giyogee ubbakka qofettennabaa. Wodala ganjjee tishshanne ziba pulttuwa (waabiya) demmanaagee attenna yo'o. Naa''u dumma dumma waabeti de'oosona.
Beettiya Waabiya: - xaaduqota, duuqettabata, gaazeexaa, maxiheetiya, h.h.m. wodala ganjjee bari ayfiya xeelli demmiyobata. 
Asaa Waabiya: - alaafeta, eranchchatanne allaaliya xeelliyo yo'uwa muukettidaageeta. Ha waabee wodala ganjjee akeekan ekki go''ettanaw bessees. Asaa pulttuwappe beettiyabati kehaa akeekan pilggidi go''ettanaw bessees ayssi giikko asi erennabaa odanaw danddayees woykko wodala ganjjiya ufayssiyabaa odana danddayees. Wodala ganjjee asaa pultto oottiyo wode he yo'uwa loytti eriya asa, ooso keettaa gadaawa woykko hanabay polettiyode sohuwan de'iya markkaa gidiya uraappe go''ettiyogee naqaashaa salo kessees; keehi xaphuwappe xeeraa gakkanaw daro qonccissees. Ha naa''u pulttotu dummatettaa Biritaaniya biitaa xaafee Keneeze Kilaarike giidoogaatto, ''taani issi hinxxaassi diya tumatettaa eranaassi koykko taassi tumanne gida naqaashaa immanay ambban diya keettatu moconayyee hinxxay gi oychchin hinxxaa,'' yaagiis. Wodala ganjjee ha''ikka hanabaa xaafiidi kehiippe akeekan oottanaw bessiyogee, leemisuwassi: xaafetti uttida gaazeexay woykko odoy kase xaafishin woykko he naqaashaa demmishin issibay zuubbaridabaa gidikko worddo naqaashay worddo markkaa mala meto medhdhanaw danddayees gi siridi tishsha pulttuwa demmidi seliseddabay diikko giigissidi xaafanaw koshshees.
2.8. WAABIYA DEMMI GO’’TTIYOGAA
Wodala ganjjee ba koyo naqaashaa immana danddayees giidi ammanettiyo asa oonanne paran tohuwan koyi demmanaw koshshees. Haray attoshin wodala ganjjee izaawa xaykko he I xaafiyo allaaliyassi lo''o pultto gidana gi qoppiyo hara heezzantta asa qatuwa malaatiya asaarakka gaytotaa medhdhanaw bessees. Kaamiya daafay gakkishin sohuwan de'iya asa sunttaa xaafi oykkidi he izaawa markkadan qoodidi appe hanabaw pulttuwa demmanaw danddayees. Hargganchchaa akamiyogaara gayttidaagan dottoree assi wolqqaama pultto. Issi issi hanabay wodala ganjjee pulttuwa demmi go''ettanaw danddayees. Ha waabiya/pulttuwa xeelliyagan wodala ganjjee akeekkanaw bessiyabati:
•	Ha bitanee daafay gakko wode bari ayfiyan be'ideeyyee ikkaa haraappe siyidee? 
•	Horoophphillee sa'an kunddi dippi gi ekkiyobaa xayin shemppoy hayqqoogaw pultto gidanaw danddayiyay horoophphille oosanchchayiyye, A keettayiyye, issi tamaare na''ay?
•	Ha pulttoy hanabaa qottan boreshshennan tumaa genttennan yootanaw danddayii?
Hara baggaara wodala ganjjee baassi naqaashaa immiya asati ooni ay yootiyakkonne kasetidi eranaw bessees. Ha wodala ganjjee pulttuwa doorana bessiyoy:
Yo'uwa eriyogan 
Izaawura gayttidaagaappe
Bitanee ammanettiya asa gidiyogaadan
Xaliyanne harggiyara gayttidabaa xeelliyagan aakimiya dottoree assi ooppenne adhdhiya pultto. Hagaadan wodala ganjjee koyrotidi allaallee xeelliyo izaawa eranaw bessees. Wodala ganjje pultto gidiya asa awaninne awdekka demmanaw assi hegee kana kaassa. Ne laggiya demmada galla galla gayttada A kaassada laggetaa minttiyogaa mala. Ambbaa kanttifan daro layttaa xaafe gididi ootta oosanchchaynne kanttifatettan ba layttaa wurssa bitanee assi he ambban hanabaa oychchi siyi xaafanaw kiise miishsha mala. Ha ambban diya gutaraa xeelliyagan wodala ganjjee benisappe kantifaa xaafe gididi diya bitaniya oychchidi A pulttodan go''ettikko A sunttay hanaban xaafettana xaykkokka ha izaawu wodala ganjjiyassi gutaraabaa yootanaw lo''o waabe. Hanabaw boolimay de'iyio pulttuwappe gidiyo gishshaw issi hanabaa oychchidi waabiya dooriyogan wodala ganjjee keehippe akeekan go''ettanaw bessees. Issi kobabay wodala ganjjiya gakkanaw danddayiyogee ha naqaashaa immida waabe giyo asi yo'uwa erennan coo malan hariya suqoy bulla giikko, hegaa ekkineekka deriya hayttan sissikko palabaa. Wodala ganjjee awdenne waabee koyees. Ay naqaasha gidikkonne wodala ganjjee ha waabiyappe hasidi demmees. Pulttoy wodala ganjjiyassi suuttaa xaphpho. Hegaa pulttoykka eranaw bessees. Kaseesappe ayyiyoo lo''o pultto gidiya asi woykko siraaway bari oosuwa laammiyo wodekka ha ba pulttuwa wodala ganjjee hanabaa oychchi yiggi xeellanaw danddayees. Issi issi tira baaxe gididabatussi pulttoy immo naqaashay gidana xaykko hara naa''antto pulttuwakka biidi oychchanaw danddayettees. Asappe ekkido naqaashay kase xaafetta oduwara issippe geedariyode tumakkonne worddokko shaakkanaw danddayettes. Ay wodala ganjjeenne asappe ekko naqaashaa ba biidi be''idoogaadan ammanettanaw danddayenna ayssi giikko asi issoy issuwa morggiya oyqqees woykko bari wozanaa koshshaa qonccissanaw danddayees.
2.9.	PISSIYA SHIISHSHIYO MAARAA
Wodala ganjje ha''ikko shenee shemppoo giidi biidi xeelliyogan kutuutanaw bessees. Xeelli shiishshiyo naqaashay assi koyro naqaashaa. Wodala ganjjee waati xeellanaakkonne luxi tamaarida eranchcha. I ay xeellidi ay ekkidi nabbabiyageetussi shiishshanaakkonne erees. Qaadadan ubbaabaa issi kutti xeelliyogee wodala ganjjiyassi danddayettennan ixxanaw danddayees. Darotoo wodala ganjjee muleera woykko bagga naqaashaa naa''antto pulttuwappe demmees. Pulttoti woykko asay muletoo haraakko zokkuwa zaaranawnne baassi he yo'uwa eqettiyo harshshuushiya de'iyogaa qonccissanaw danddayiyo gishshaw muletoo pultto kanchchiya bolli hidootaa wottiyogee lo''enna. Hegaa gishshaw pulttoppe shiishshobay ubbaykka tumu yo'o giidi ammanettanaw danddayettenna. Hegaassi wodala ganjjee pulttuwappe shiishsho naqaashay ay keena tumakkonne pude duge giidi shaakkana bessees. Wodala ganjjee polanaw attennabay pisse shiishsho kanchche gidenna waani hanidee (issibay waani polettidee?) Ayba gaasuwan hanidee? Ay maaduwa immidee woykko ay qohuwa gattidee? Giyogaa qonccissanaw koshshees. Hegaa gishshaw eti pulttoy de'iyo naqaashaa go''ettoosona.

Malvviini Menchcheeroy 'News Reporting and writing,' yaagiya bari maxaafan ha heezzu yo'ota malaati kanttiis.
1.	Sinttaa Tumaa: - pulttuwara de'iya miishshaa, jorinaaletussi giiga xuufiya, xaafettabaanne haasaya duuqqoogaa.
2.	Pissiya Shiiqabaa: - qonccissuwa, pilggi xeelli shiishsho pissiya, hani kanttabay xaafettaagaanne assi de'iya gedenuwa (guyye haydaa).
3.	Birshshi Qonccissobaa: - koshshiyabaa maacci kanttobaa, gaasuwanne A maaduwa woykko qohuwa.
2.10.	KIITTIIYO ODUWA
Geediyagee (kaalli xeelliyagee) kiittiyo oduwa zaarettidi balabi diikko diggirggidi kiittiyo naa''u gaasoti de'oosona. Hegeetikka koyruwan koshshennan gujjetabata denttiyogaa, naa''anttuwan ha xaafiyo odoy xekkaa naagidaagaa gidanaw bessiyonne oduwa xaafiyo wogaa kaalli xaafettoogaa geeshshi eranaasa. Koyro wodala ganjjee hanabaw kulkka yo'uwa demmiyogaa. Ha yo'uwa demmanaw wodala ganjjee ooni, ay, awan, ayssi, awdenne waanidi, yaagiya oyshata oychcanaw koshshees, hanabaa odoy darotoo ha oyshatu zaaro gidees.
2.11.	JORINAALE YAA'AA
Wodala ganjjee dere asaa citaa shiishshidi naqaashaa demmanaw oyshaa shiishshiyo konssoonuwa jorinaale yaa'aa geetettees. Ha yaa'an ubba wodala ganjjiyassikka ay oyshanne shiishshanaw maatay de'ees. Oychchiyobay issibay hani simmin he I kaaletto qohuwa woykko maaduwa gidanaw danddayees. He sohuwan qoodan guutta halaafetinne kawo ooso keettaa gadaawatikka shiiqi dendda oyshaw zaaruwa immoosona. Ha yaa'aa koyroti yameti dumma dumma koshshiya kifiliya erissanaw bessees. Yaa'ay poletto sohoy, gallassaynne wodee xaafettanaw attenna miishsha. Ha yaa'an jamay wodala ganjjiyassi ooni A hanabaa koshshaassi galafiya gakkiya zaaruwa immanaakkonne allaallee xelliyo izaawa malaati kanttees woy bana xeellikko tilla zaaruwa immees. Ha shiishshiyo naqaashaassikka dendduwa deree wodala ganjjiyassi yooti kanttees.

HANABAA PUULAYIYOGAA
Hanabaa qonccissiya naqaashaa puulay giigissidi deriyassi aattiyogee wodala ganjjiyassi aawu oytto toora. Hegee assi mule attenna gara geze. Ha shiishshiyo yaa'ay awan, awdee, kuushsha yo'uwanne woqu saatiyan polettidaakko deriyassi kasetidi qonccissanaw koshshees. Wodala ganjjeti he yaa'an beettiyogee laallanttenna yo'o gidishin ha yaa'an wodala ganjjee yo'uwa pilggidi ba koydo naqaashaa demmees. Kase dendduwassi de'iya hekkaynne ha kuushsha yo'uwa qonccissiya asati (pulttoti) ha dendda oyshaw tilla zaaro gidoosona. Ha pilggettaa wodiya wodala ganjjee dumma dumma maxaafata, anqqetstsetanne pultto gidiya asaassi de'iya guyyiya akeekidi eranaw koshshees. Wodala ganjjee yaa'aappe kase geediyageetuura haasayanaw bessees. Eti zaaruwa immiyo amarida oyshatikka de'oosona. He wodala ganjjeti hagaa mala yaa'an beettana xaykkonne kase yaa'iyo meezee baynnabaa gidikko hara kase meezee diyo wodala ganjjetuura yaa'anaw bessees. Ha yaa'an jamaara issippe yaa'idi shiishshiyo odoy wodala ganjjiya oosuwassi keehi lo''o; heede sohuwan pultto gidiya asi bessiyo bollaa qaattay oduwa ayfiyara gelees giyogaadan assi waggaga. Ha waabee assi naqaashaa immiidi qim''otiyogeenne siiriyan sim''iyogee hanabaa woykko oduwassi daro puulaa immees; boolimaakka darissees.
YAA'ETTIYO WODE
Ay wodala ganjjeekka issi hoolliya bolli tobbana yaa'ettiyogee attennabaa. Asa ubbaykka oduwa xeelliyagan oyshaa denttees. Ha gaytotan qaadaawa gidiya wodala ganjjeti oyshaa denttana danddayoosona. Asaappe naqaashaa oychchanaw televizhzhiiniya wodala ganjjeti haratuppe keehi ufayttoosona. Ayssi giikko televizhhzhiiniya masttootiyan beetiyogaa dosiyoynne siyettanaw koyiyo gishshaw. Xaafetti giigiya miidiya wodala ganjjee yaa'aa sohuwan jamaappe kasetidi beettanaw bessees. Hagee eti sinttan eqqidi oyshaa daxxana mala maaddees. Wodala ganjjee yaa'an asay oychchiyo wode hayttaa corggochchidi ezgganaw bessees. Hagee I hara asaykka issoy issuwa (allaallee xeelliyo asa oychchiyogaappe) zaaretti oychchana malanne naa''aw woykko heezzu oyshaw zaaruwa immana malanne shaaray iraa qashamiyogaadan wodala ganjjee yaa'aw kuushsha yo'uwa erana malaka keehi maaddees. Wodala ganjjiyappe halanaw bessennabay oyshay diishin assi oychchiyo qaaday imettana xaykko ha yaa'an tobettabaa kaasseetiyan duuqqi oyqqidi ha wozanan de'iya oyshaa zaaruwa duuqetta kaasseetiyappe demmanaw danddayees. Wodala ganjjeti oduwa giigissidi issi kutti corabaa oottanaw danddayoosona. Eti oyshaa shiishshoosona, harati oychchiyode xaafi oyqqidi naqaashaa demmoosona.
YAA'AAPPE SIMMIYODE
Yaani yaa'aa wurssi simmidikka wodala ganjjee ba beeruwa lawhu gees. Yaa gakkanaappe kasetidi ba oduwa waati xaafi asaa sissanaakkonne hanabaw (naqaashaw) kulkka yo'uwa qori shiishshees. Beeruwa bululiyaban woykko tohuwan hametti binneekka oosuwa waati maaraa oyttanaakko qoppees. Yaatiyo gishshaw beeruwa gakkinne oosuwan shukuluuliigees. Sohuwara oosuwa polinneekka ooso wodiya xuuggennan ha ootto oosuwawkka boolimaa naagidi hara koshshiyabaa gujjerettidi wurssidi sinttaw oottiyo oosuwawkka beni 'Daachcha uukkayda komppiyogaadan' naqaashaa shiishshuwa hayrees. Xaafoy ha oychchi shiishshobati guuggiyappe harchchidi halennan diishin haruwara doomettichchanaw bessees. Hegaassi wodala ganjjee ha oyshatussi zaaruwa demmanaw bessees.
•	Yaa'an dendda yo'otun oorattabi aybee?
•	Ay oyshati pissiyaw go''iyonaa?
•	Odiyagee oyshaa suure zaarii?
•	Odiyagee koshshiya naqaashaappe yedhdhi aadhdhobi dii?
•	Ha oyshaw kulkka yo'oy aybee?
•	haasayiyagaw Hanabay waani kosiya ekkanee?
Hagaa bolli gujjuwan, wodala ganjjeti ha yaa'an denddabaappe hanabaw kaafiyabaa akeekana koshshees. Hageeti hanabaa mucuuri giigissiyo wode keehi maaddoosona.
•	Haasayiyagaw ayfe yo'uwa (A haasayaw kuushsha qofaa) oyqqida qofa qashoy oychchin zaariyo wode kulkka qofa.
•	Haasayiyagaw sunttaa, A erissiyobaa, oosuwa qommuwanne aawatettaa.
•	Hoolliya, wodiya, sohuwanne yaa'ay takko wodiya.
•	Yo'uwassi kulkkaa dendduwa.
2.12.	HAASAYAN ODUWA AATTIYOGAA
Issi ooso keettaa woykko yamiya gadaaway shoobettidi haasayiyo wode koyruwan haasayiyoy kuushsha yo'uwa xaafidi he shoobetto yaa'aw immees. Ha xaafetta naqaashay wodala ganjjiyassi keehippe maaddees. Ha naqaashay wodala ganjjiyassi ay kuushsha yo'uwan I haasay daakkonne eranaw maaddees. Ha haasayan aadhdha oduwa aattanaappe kasetidi wodala ganjjee ayfe yo'uwa qori giigissanaw keehippe go''ees. Koyroora xaafettabaa ekkidi nabbabi simmidi qassi haasayiyo pissiya geedaridi ayfe yo'uwa pilgganawkkaa xaafetta naqaashaa ekkirggiyogee wodala ganjjiya ha haasayaakka luxi eranaw keehi go''ees. Ha ogiya kaallidi oduwa giigissiyogee wodala ganjjee oduwassi, koshshiyabaynne oorattabay diikko eranawkka maaddees. Wurssettan ha wodala ganjjee ayfe yo'uwa kasetidi ha xaafetta naqaashaappe qori kessidi haasayara walakkidi oduwa giigissees. Naqaashaykka haasayiyobaa muliya xaaxi waaxi oykkees.
KEEHI KOSHSHIYA YO'UWA
Mulekka wodala ganjjee xaafetta naqaasha kanchchiyan keten''i eqqidi odo giigissanaw koshshenna gaasoykka ooni erii ha haasayiya izaawu (gadaaway) haasayiidi aybakko baassi siyetabaa, ulo mishuwa, garanttiyabaa, gurum''iyabaa woykko ufayssiyabaa gujjanaw danddayees. Ha haasayiyagaw issibaa gujjanawnne denttanaw kumetta maatay de'ees. Wodala ganjjeti xaafettabaa kanchchiyappe oduwa giigissikko ha haasayida izaawu aybanne haasayidi gujjibeennaagaa eranaw bessees. Hagee qassi danddayettenna. Ayssi giikko haasayidi ba wozanaa mishuwa qonccissanaw woykko oduwa mal''ettanaw issibaa gujjanawnne denttanaw danddayees. Haasayishin laamettabay diikko sohuwara laammichchanaw koshshees.
 
Hara baggaara qassi wodala ganjjee haasaya kanchchiyappe oduwa giigissanaw danddayoosona. Etassi he haasayaappekka ayfe yo'uwa xaafi oyqqidi giigissanaagee attennabaa. Ha wodiyan wodala ganjjee teeppiyan duuqqi oyqqanaw koshshees; ha teeppiya duuqqo naqaashaappe ayfe yo'uwa maxi oduwa giigissanaw danddayeenna. Oduwa yaagaatoo koyro xaafidi giigissiyogee wodala ganjjiyaw baaso ooso. Yaati simmidi geedettan siqimmees.
2.13.	HAASAYIYODE KAALLIYO WOGATI
Haasayiyagee haasayiyo wode wodala ganjjeti kaallanaw bessiya wogati: -
Xaafuwa: - wodala ganjjee teeppiyan oyqqinikka hara xaafiyobati koshshoosona. Hagan keehippe koshshiyabay hayttaa corggochchidi ezggidi ha hanaban geliya haasayiyagee go''etto qaalaanne qofa qashota boroshennan gelissanaw xaafi oyqqanaw bessees. Ha teeppiya xaafi oyqqibeenna oyshata hanaban simmi kaallidi gelissanaw maaddees. 
Xeelaa: - haasayiyagaw maayuwa, A bollaa qaattaa (kushiya wuxaa wuxiyogaanne siiriyan qim''otiyogaa) odoy ayfiya geliyo gishshataw loytti xeellanaw bessees. Xeelay hanabaw puulaa immees. Yaa'an diya asaa qooday woyasakkonne malan eranaw koshshees. Jamay qoodan guyte gidikko maaraara diya wombbaraa qoodidi sintta yafaraanne gedeta yafaraa darissin asaa qooday wayssennan erettees. 
Ezgguwa: - Ha jamaa wodala ganjjee shaakkiyo wode hanabaw (oduwaw) giigisso koshshiyabi beettikko he sinttan qoxomidi malaataa wotti simmi giigissanaw danddayees. 
Ayfe Yo'uwa Qashamuwa: - haasayiyagee wurssettan woykko doomettan ayfe yo'uwa haasayees. He haasayay hanabaw kulkka yo'uwa oykkees. Ha ayfe yo'uwa haasayishin bayra qofa qashuwa balennan ezgganaw koshshees. Hegaw gaasotay hanabaw kulkka yo'oy aani huuxettiyo gishataassi. 
Wurssetta Oyshaa: - issi gadaawati haasayi simmidi wodala ganjjeti oyshaa shiishshana mala anttoosona. Heede ha gadaaway haasayan gelissibeenna yo'ota oychchanaw koshshees. Haasayiyagee gelibeennabaa oychchiyogaanne issi issi  A haasayaappe woygana koydidaakko erettenna (sirissiya) qofaa mulekka oychchanaw guyye gaana koshshenna.
2.14.	YAA'AA ODUWA
Yaa'ay darotoo salo gufantto, issi biitaa woykko issi heeraa xeelliyagaa gidanaw danddayees shin yaa'ettabay gutaraa, aqotaa, issipetettaanne hara allaalliya xeellana danddayees. Yaa'ay ba keeretto wodiyan tobettees shin issitoo issitoo tiran kiya odoti de'ikko keeruwa naagennan sohuwara ha kase keeruwa maaran yaa'etta oduwa bolli caridi koyroora odiigeettes. Hegeekka daafaa oduwa, meretan carkkoy, iray, away, di'oy, gotee, h.h.m. gatto qohuwa gidana danddayees. Ha tiran kiya odoy koyro miidee eriina gidenna kiyoy hegaa gidikkokka wodala ganjjee kuttoy haatta mittanaashin gattennan giigissi asaa sissana koshshees. Ha tiran kiya oduwa koyro carkkuwan peeshshi simmidi A hanuwadan zaareti zaarettidi ha oduwa giigissidi minttanaw danddayettees. Ha yaa'ay keehi koshshiyo gishshaw  oduwassi heezzu xekkati de'anaw danddayoosona. Hegeetikka: yaa'aappe kase, yaa'ettiyo wodenne yaa'aappe guyye. Yaa'aappe kase gidiyogee asay eranaasa, haniyabaa, haasayettiyabaa asaw kasetidi hekkay de'anaadan oottees. Deree kaseti haasay maacettidi oyshi diikko denttanaw giigettees. Ha yaa'ettin beettiya ooso ayfiya xeelliyagankka haasayettanaw danddayees. Ha haasayan tobbiyo wode aybi haniidi diyakko aybi qassi hananaw diyakko asay erees. Heede asaassi ha yaa'an haasayettiyagaw ooso ayfeekka haasayi simmin qoncciyan erettees.
2.14.1.	YAA'AAPPE KASE
Wodala ganjjee yaa'aa shaakkanaw xeessettikko, appe naagettiyay kuushsha qofaa pilggiyogaa. Kase gaazeexan xaafetti kiyabati hagaadan pilggiyo wode keehippe go'oosona. Laytta oosuwa oosuwa poluwa pissiya bolli yaa'iyo wode wodala ganjjee kase oosetti kanttabaa zaarettidi xeellees. Eketta tangguwakka wudissidi akeekanaw koshshees. Ha yaa'an go''etto miishshatakka moorettennadan loytti ushachcha kushiya oyqqidi naaganaw bessees. Ha yaa'ay keehippe koshshiya yaa'a gidishin koshshiya kifilee kasetidi haniyabaa jamaassi qonccissanaw bessees. Geediyagee wodala ganjjoya ha yaa'aa shaakkidi oduwa giigissana mala kiitettees. Hagee yaa'aw puulaa immees, ooso ayfiyakka minttees. Heede hanabaa demmiyo asaarakka gayttanaw maaddees. Ha gayttiyo asi hanabaassi pulttodan hanabaassi sinttappe haniyabaakka hani kanttabaakka wodala ganjjiyassi qonccissees. Haray qassi ha allaalliya xeelliyagan xaafetta naqaashay diikkokka wodala ganjjiyassi malaati kanttees. Ha yaa'aa shiishshiyagaara kasetidi gayttiyogee wodala ganjjiyassi daro lo''o. Ha shiishshiyageeti dumma yaa'aw kaafe gidiya naqaashata koyrotidi giigissanaw danddayoosona; hegee qassi kase hani kanttabaa xeelliyagan hekkay de'ana mala maaddees.
2.14.2.	YAA''ETTIYO WODE
Yaa'ay yaa'ettiyo bayra allaaleti:
•	Miishshaara gayttidaagan, dooruwa, maachchaa, polissiyara gayttidaagan h.h.m.
•	Hoolliya, wodiyanne yaa'aa sohuwa.
•	Ajanddan (yirchchan) de'iyabata.
•	Tobbiyanne palamaa (ekkiyo wodiya).
•	Markkatinne eranchchati haasayiyobata.
•	Xeelliya yarati, kawo ooso keettaa gadaawatinne hara xeesetta imatati immiyo qofaanne hayyuwa.
•	Gedenuwa (dendduwa)
•	Ajanddaa (yirchchaappe) kareera de'iyabata.
•	Naa''antto yiya yaa'aa anjjanddaa.
Wodala ganjjee ha bollan xaafetta yo'otu bolla deree tobbiyo wode hanabaa qori shiishshees. Ha yaa'an wodala ganjjee darobaa polanaw beessees. I hanabaa qoridi eranchchata, haasayidi woykko nabbabidi qofaa aattiyo wode oychchiyobi diikko oychchees. Wodala ganjjee ha yaa'aa sohuwan beettiyogee I he sohuwan asaara erettanaw, he yaa'an woxxi qaaxxabaa pissiya shiishshanaw injjettiya sohuwan uttanawnne heeraa meezettanaassi maaddees. Xeellidi yaa'an de'iya jamay muleera huuphphiyan oyqqiyogee hanabaa aattiyo wode ha wodala ganjjiya keehi wayssenna.
2.14.3.	YAA''AAPPE GUYYIYAN
Xaafuwa doommanaaappe kase wodala ganjjee oduwassi de'iya qottaa maacanaw bessees. Maaraara xaafettiyakko, heezzu zoozekko, coo yeda xuufekko eridi maacees. Hegaappe guyyiyan he yaa'aw ooso ayfeekka xaafettees. Xaafiidi issibaa kanchchiya gidennan diishin ubba baggakka bosheretti kanttanaw koshshees. Issitoo issitoo yaa'ay ekkidi galla galla hanabaa qonccissiyo meray de'ikko hegaakka wodala ganjjee maaraa oykkanaw bessees. Ha galla galla aattiyo oduwa woykko gaazeexaa kessiyagee issi yaa'an koyro gallassi hanabaa ezggiyageeta woykko nabbabiyageeta naa''antto gallassi shaakkissanaw danddayees. Hagee ubba coo hanabaa erennan woykko hassayennan aattiyogaappe issi gallassaagaa gidikkonne wozanan karhhi oottanaw he ezggiya woykko nabbabiya asaa maaddees.

QANTTA QOFAA
Wodala ganjjiyassi pulttoy (waabee) cora ginaara beettanaw danddayees. Heezzu naqaashaw pulttoti: Oyshaa, xeelaanne xaaduquwa. Oyshi baynnan naqaashi shiiqiyo wodee mulekka baawa gaanaw danddayettees. Lo''o oyshay sissaanne ero kanchchiya gidennan diishin deree ezgganaadan yeemoyees, boolimanne deriya garanttiya xuuraa kaashi laalees. Wodala ganjjee ba koyo naqaashaa immana danddayees giidi ammanettiyo asa oonanne paran tohuwan koyi demmanaw koshshees. Wodala ganjjiyassi waabiya oychchiyo allaalliya xeelliyagan hekkay (guuttay) eray de'iyogee attennabaa. Issi kobabay wodala ganjjiya gakkanaw danddayiyogee ha naqaashaa immida waabe giyo asi yo'uwa erennan coo malan hariya suqoy bulla giikko, hegaa ekkineekka deriya hayttan sissikko palabaa. Pulttoy wodala ganjjiyassi suuttaa xaphpho. Ay wodala ganjjeenne asappe ekko naqaashaa ba biidi be''idoogaadan ammanettanaw danddayenna ayssi giikko asi issoy issuwa morggiya oyqqees woykko bari wozanaa koshshaa qonccissanaw danddayees. Wodala ganjjee polanaw attennabay pisse shiishsho kanchche gidenna. Waani hanidee/polettidee? Ayba gaasuwan hanidee? Ay maaduwa immidee woykko ay qohuwa gattidee? Giyogaa qonccissanaw koshshees. Wodala ganjjee kulkka yo'uwa demmanaw ooni, ay, awan, ayssi, awdenne waanidi, yaagiya oyshata oychcanaw koshshees, hanabaa odoy darotoo ha oyshatu zaaro gidees. Yaa'ay poletto sohoy, gallassaynne wodee xaafettanaw attenna miishsha. Hanabaa qonccissiya naqaashaa puulay giigissidi deriyassi aattiyogee wodala ganjjiyassi aawu oytto toora. Wodala ganjjeti yaa'an beettana xaykkonne kase yaa'iyo meezee baynnabaa gidikko hara kase meezee diyo wodala ganjjetuura yaa'anaw bessees. Waabee assi naqaashaa immiidi qim''otiyogeenne siiriyan sim''iyogee hanabaa woykko oduwassi daro puulaa immees; boolimaakka darissees. Wodala ganjjiyappe halanaw bessennabay oyshay diishin assi oychchiyo qaaday imettana xaykko ha yaa'an tobettabaa kaasseetiyan duuqqi oyqqidi ha wozanan de'iya oyshaa zaaruwa duuqetta kaasseetiyappe demmanaw danddayees. Xaafoy ha oychchi shiishshobati guuggiyappe harchchichchenna diishin haruwara doomettichchanaw bessees. Mulekka wodala ganjjee xaafetta naqaasha kanchchiyan keten''i eqqidi odo giigissanaw koshshenna gaasoykka ooni erii ha haasayiya izaawu (gadaaway) haasayiidi aybakko baassi siyetabaa, ulo mishuwa, garanttiya, gurum''iyabaa woykko ufayssiyabaa gujjanaw danddayees. Oduwa yaagaatoo koyro xaafidi giigissiyogee wodala ganjjiyaw baaso ooso. Yaati simmidi geedettan siqimmees. Haasayiyo wode kaalliyo wogati: xaafuwa, xeelaa, ezgguwa, ayfe yo'uwa qashamuwanne wurssetta oyshaa. Haasayay hanabaw kulkka yo'uwa oykkees. Wodala ganjjee yaa'aa shaakkanaw xeessettikko, appe naagettiyay kuushsha qofaa pilggiyogaa. Xaafuwa doommanaaappe kase wodala ganjjee oduwassi de'iya qottaa maacanaw bessees.
                
 
























HEEZZANTTO SHEMPPUWA
MIIDIYA XAAFANAASSI KUNTTIYOBATA
3.1. HUUPHE MIIDIYA XAAFUWAW GELUWA
Toophiyo Saara Bazzuwappe xadeera diya Afirikaa biittatun ba pitalee de'iyogee keehippe ayyettiyabaa. Beni mayzzatu Gi'ize doonay Toophphiya pitaliyan xaafettikkonne, Toophpiya Orttoodokise woossa keettan hano gakkanaashin Amaarattuwadaaninne hara gita qaalatu leemisuwaw Tigirettuwadan wogaa naagidi haasayettiidinne xaafettiidi takkiis. 

Noriwoye biittan luxida iskkoolaaree R.K. Molbbaari bari ''BLACK LIONS' giya maxaafan “The creative lives of modern Ethiopian's Literature Gaits and pineers”' yaagiya kuushsha yo'uwan 32 dumma dumma issi ogiyan woykko haran, issi wodiyan woykko hara wodiyan jorinaaliizimiya meezetidaageetu duussaanne oosuwa pilggiyo wode Dottoree Kabbada Mikaali keehi bonchchettida dabbidaabbiya xaafiya asatuppe issuwa,'' giis.

Xaafonne nabbabo bilay hanno gakkanawkka Toophphiyan yiilloyiya hanotan de'ees; ubbaykka deriya miidiya xeelliyagan hagaa mala xekkan de'ees gi haasayanaw doonaa kumi otorissenns. Hagaappe sinttawkka ha oosuwan meezetiyageeti daro oosuwa oottanaw bessees. Hegee eti gatiya qanxxidi siiddanaw bessiya ooso.

Issi galla galla peeshshan keehippe xaafonne nabbabo bilaa dichchiyogee zamaanatettaw pinnanaw attenna yo'o. Miidee issi biittaassi gutaraa/polotikaanne issipetettaa laamiya ehanaw dooroy baynna ooso miishsha. Awrooppaaninne Huuphphessa Amerikaa biittan xaafetta miidee xaykko tamaare keettatu dichchay qofettenna. Huuphe miidiya xaafoy, ha sunttay bessiyogaadan xaafonne coraa gattiyo naqaashaa miidiyassi baaso. Beni asay haasayiidi, 'olay issi deriya bashshin odoy oyddu deriya bashshees.' giyogaadan ha wodiya yeletay qassi, ''xaafoy guuggiyan de'iya ubbabaassikka wozona ayfe,'' yaagees.


Meeziya 1
I.	Miidee issi biittaw gutaraanne issipetettaa laamiya ehanaw baaso miishsha gidiyo gaasota qantta birshshada xaafa.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- .
3.1.1. HUUPHE YO'OTA
Naqaashaa shiishshuwa, qonccissuwa, halchchuwanne xaaafi giigissuwa.
•	Jorinaale oosuwaw koshshiya ayfe yo'ot: loytti xaafiyogaa, oosuwan waati geliyakkonne qottaa quxariyogaa.
•	Oduwaw maaciyobata, usppun oyshatu (awan, ay, oonii, ayssi, waatidi/waanidinne awde) bolli wudissiyogaa, asaa nabbabanawnne siyanaw yeemoyiya hanabaa quxaruwanne lo''o xaafuwa wurssetta
•	Shiishsho naqaashaa pissee, pilggiyo pissiya, oyshanne birshshettaa immido pissiya.
•	Hanabaw ayfe yo'uwa xaafanaw koshshiyabati (ayfe yo'uwa quxariyogaanne heezzu ogiyan ayfe yo'uwa xaafiyogaa.
•	Deriya gaytotaassinne erissuwa xaafiyo wode.
•	Coraa gattiyo odo naqaashaa xaafiyo wode.
•	Xuufiyanne xaaduquwa xaafettaa.
3.1.2. KAAFIYA YO'OTA
Hagaappe kaallidi diya yo'oti coraa gattiyo naqaashaa miidiya pissiya giigissiyo wode eranaw bessoosona.
•	Geediyagaa, geedettaa, xuufiya pilggettaanne, xaafiyo xaraphpheezaa.
•	Qonccissuwa, jorinaaliya oosuwanne haraw bayzzuwa.
•	Oduwa, oduwassi kulkka yo'uwanne wudaa demmuwa.
•	Xaafiyagaa, gaasuwan qoncciyagaanne gaazeexaa.
•	Ajjanddaa shiishshuwanne orddiya xaafetta xuufiya.
•	Sitta oduwa oyshaanne yippaa giigissuwa.
•	Maattamuwa.
•	Oduwassi kulkkaa, heezzu zooze xaafo quxaruwanne usppun oyshatu zaaruwa beettiya ayfe yo'uwa.
•	Issoy, naa''ay woykko heezzu yippay diyo hanabaa.
•	Loytti geeshshin balay piggetti giigido xuufiya.
•	Maaraa mankkaa, haraa qofaa wuuqqiyo danuwa, oyshaanne ne qofan birshshi xaafiyogaa.













3.1.3. HANABAA QUXARUWA

 
















Sitta oduwaw hanabaa, sitta kuushshaa, usppun oyshatun demmiyo kuushsha qofaa, qofaawa-sophe-peesho (subject-verb-object) geluwa maaraa, naa''unne heezzu yippa hanabaa, 1, 2, 3, shiiqo hanabaa maarattuwanne, heezzu xuggunnida zooze huuphe miidiya xaafiyo wogata. Hagee timirtte keettan tamaare naati bantta luxi eriyo kifile wodiya gidennan diishin timirttiyappe kareera bantta wodiya yarshshidi keehi meezetiyo allaalle. Ha allaalliya xeelliyagan xaafo hiillaa loytti eranaw tamaare naati bantta huuphen lodaara xibennan oottanaw bessees. Hara baggaara ha dumma dumma xaafi shiishshiyo hiillan lo''o meezee de'ana gakkanaashin tamaare naati ha allaalliya xeelliyagan xaafetta maxaafata coraa nabbabanaw koshshees. Xaafuwa shiiquwappe aadhdhiya dumma dumma merati doosona. Muleera payya hanabay issi yo'uwa he oduwa heera allaallee keehi xeelliyo gishshaw oottidi wudissees. Huuphe yo'uwa bolli hara gujjo qofati keehi gujjo qofaappe keehi aahuwan (A xoqqissiyogan) qonccees. Xaafanchchay kulkka oosoy ayfe yo'uwa maacidi haraa kessi oliyogaa. 
•	Miidiya xaafiyo hiillay aybi ekettanawnne aybi olettanaw bessiyakko geeshshi eriyogaa. Eray qonccetettaw baaso.
•	Qaalaa dooroy keehi cimmeesinne cora dummatettaa medhdhees. Qaalaa dooroy xaafiyagaw de'iya minonne lefa miyyiya shaakki erissees.
•	Issi gaazeexaanne maxiheetiya boolimay palanttiyanne shaahotetta qofi de'anaw bessiyaba gidenna.
Meeziya 2
I.	Huuphe miidya xaafiyo wogatuppe naa’’aa doorada he ne dooridoogetun issi hanabaa mijjirssaa oottada xaafa.
