3.1.4. MIIDIYAN KOSHSHIYABATA
Issi yo'uwa ya baggawnne ha baggaw bixe ootti xeelliyogee miidiyan pissiya shiishshiyogaw baaso yo'o. Naa''u baggaw issi mala wudaa immi xeelliyogee, eratettan hallacciyogaanne, sittatettaa bessees. Ha bollaara qonccida yo'oti boolimaa naagida miidiya xuufiyan kunttanaw bessiyanne issi luxi loohida eranchchay kaallanaw bessiyabata. Qofan koyi demmidi wodala ganjjee ha baappe naagettiyabata eranaw koshshees. Xaafiyagee awdenne ha yo'ota guyye simmi qofiyagaa guyye gaanaw bessenna. Hageeta guyye simmiyogan wodala ganjjee ammanettiyogaa, maaciyogaa, issibaa polanaw (xaafanaw) yaanne haanne qel''i qel''ennaagaa tamaaridi erees. Xoqqa timirttiya asttamaareenne he tamaariyo timirtte garoy maxaafa keettaanne issi issi banttappe naagettiyabata kunttin wodala ganjjee timirttiyappe kareera coraa gattiyo naqaashaa miidiyawnne asaassi issibaa essanaw xaafiyogawkka ha hiillan go''ettees. Televizhzhiiniyawnne iraaduwaw xaafiyageeti hanabaa qanttayoosona; qaxiballo yo'uwa lefayidi asay galla galla qofqq laammiyo haasayaa go''ettoosona. Hegaassi gaasotaykka eti hayttan sissanaw xaafoosona. Eta ezggiyageetunne tamaariyageetussi naa''antto zaarettidi siyiyo qaadi baynna gishshaw koyro haasayishin oykkanaw koshshees.
Meeziya 3
II.	Miidiyaw koshshiyabata qantta qofa qashotu go’’ettada kaalliya mela sohuwan xaafa.
A.-----------------------------------------------------------------------------B.   ----------------------------------------------------------------------------
C. -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
D. -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
E. -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
3.1.5. MIIDIYA XAAFIYO MERAA
Miidiyassi xaafiyo meray, hiillaynne giigissi shiishshiyogee koshshiyogee ha aattiyo kiittaassi yesuwa naaganaasa. Hageekka miidiya xaafo hiillaa geetettees. Hageetuppe amaridaageeti:
•	Kessiyobaa (denttiyobaa) akeeki eriyogaa.
•	Attidabaa loytti gaccidi qanttiyogaa.
•	Payya xaafoy yo'uwa poluwa gakkanaashin porxxu ootti kessees; kessiyobaakka coo gede zaari toskkayennaadan naagees. Hegaa oosuwan peeshshanaagee wolqqaama baaxiyanne keehi oosuwa koyees. Yaatiyo gishshaw tamaare naati cora meezeta, so oosotanne dumma dumma ooso projekitetun loytti meezeetanaw bessoosona. 
•	Nabbaboy, nu biittanne kare biittaa gaazeexaanne maxiheetiya yo'uwa yippan batidi tobbiyogee tamaare naatussi galla galla saletenna ootti mali be''idi banttana yiggi xeellanaw bessoosona.
•	Issi xoqqa tamaare keettaa kolloojjiya gidiinkka universsittiya xeelliyagan xaafi kessiyo gaazeexaappe tamaare naati meeziya ekkanaw bessoosona. 
•	Danddayettiyakko citan oottiyo oosoy, projekitee, issi issi naqaasha maxaafata koyiyagaanne guutta pilggettan geliya oosoy polettana bessees. Attenna hanotan gitanne dumma dumma asaa meeziyan yelaga naatu oosuwa qaattaa xeelliyagan koyrotidi tamaare naati guyye geennan oottanaw bessees.
Proofeeseree Kawaane Karikari, Arggo Afrikkaa biittan miidiya baasuwassi huuphe dereteree (Pirankko Poonenne Anggiloopoone biittan) ha tamaare naatussi haasayiidi yaagiis, ''Taassi qaaday imettiyakko, taani nabbabana, zaara zaaradakka nabbana, heezzutoo oydutoo kase nabbaba kanttobaakka salettennan nabbabana.'' Ha proofeeseree daro layttaa Lenggoone Universsittiyan Akiraa biittan tamaarissiissinne miidiya xeelliyagan maxaafaakka xaafiis. Miidiya oottiyageeti balaa oottikko etassi ezggiya (nabbabiya) jamay atto geenna. Eta asay ubbabaa eriyadan qoppees. Hegaa gishshaw eti nabbabuwan siiddidi corabaa eriyogan banttana luxissanaw koshshees.
3.2. LO''O XAAFUWASSI KUNTTIYOBATA
Hagan 'lefaaninne qoncciyan' gi doomettidoogee miidiya xaafoy muleera ha yo'otun xaaxi waaxettiyogaasa. Lo''o xaafoy tamaariya izaawussi qofan de'iya haaho aymo gidenna kase eri aadhdhobaa gaanaasa. Lefayiyogeenne qonccissoy miidiya xaafanchchay guyye geennan shociyo hoolle.

Ha xaafo hiillay keehiippe meezettiyonne galla galla yedhdhi aadhdhennan poliyo miishsha. Luxissiyagaassi sohuwara lo''o xaafuwassi kunttanaw bessiyabati shiiqoosona; huuphe xaafuwa hiillaa luxiyagee eranaw bessiya ooso buussati yippan yippan shaahettidinne 'cheekilisttiyan' giigidi shiiqoosona. Hegee koshshiyogaw gaasoykka, xaafoy keehi deexo miishsha gidiyogaa. Ha demmido naqaashaa aara issippe biya qaalaatuura gattiyogee ufayssiya, qonccenne qantta qaalata koyi demmidi issippe waaxeettees. Ha yo'oy muleera ha heezzu qaalatun ciiyees.
Meeziya 4
I.	Lo’’o xaafuwassi hagee koshshee giyobata qantta qofa qashotu go’’ettada kaalliya mela sohuwan xaafa.
A.-----------------------------------------------------------------------------B.   ----------------------------------------------------------------------------
C. -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
D. -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
E. -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
3.2.1. LO''O XAAFOY OYKKIYOBATA
Ha shemppuwassi kulkka halchchoy nena luxiyagaa xaafiyogaa miidiya xaafo hiillaa luxissidi loohissanaasa. Hageekka keehi eranaw wayssiya xaaphaalo qofaa lefayidinne dumma xaafiyo hiillan amppidi yo'uwa lefayanawnne qonccissanaw hana keenaa baaxettiyogaana. Xaafoy deexo miishsha. Shiiqida naqaashaa coraa issippe biya milatiya qaalaara dabboyiyogee, ha tiraara sitti giya qaalata, paca qofa qashotanne qofa qashota lefayidi ufayssiya hanotan qonccissidi asaassi muccuuridi shiishshiyogee miidiya xaafuwaw attenna hiilla. Xaafoy asi ba wolqqaa oosuwan peeshuwa mali be'iyo oge. Beni nu aawati hayseyiidi, '' Naa''u biradhdhiyan yeessido maattay tammu biradhdhiyan guyye gelenna,'' giyogaadan ha xaafo hiillan issibay seliseddiichchikko zuuqqanaw daro meto. Hegaa gishshaw xaafuwa xeelliyagan maaray mankkay salo gufanttuwaninne nu biittan giigida seeray bonchchettanaw koshshees. Hinkkoodee yo'oy zuubbariichchikko akeekenna gereessay zaarishin metees giyogaa kiyi aggees. Ha lefanne qoncciyan xaafiyogan nabbabiyagee oonee? Yaagiya oyshay awdenne attenna miishsha. Qantta qofa qashuwan issi gaana koyidobaa qonccissanaagee adussanne yabaca qofa qashuwa issi lasttiqedan dafin aduqqiya qofa qashuwan xaafi qonccisannaagaappe meto. Issi yo'uwa pexi heezzu qaalatun xephidi shiishshanaagee keehi deexo; adussanne xaaphaalo qofa qashuwa go''ettiyogee oottanaw lefa shin caddenna qofa qashuwa oyqqidi kuushshi baynna yo'uwa coo gede zaari corddodayidi biddiyogaa gidees. 

Lo''o xaafoy loytti nabbanaadan wuttees. Miidiya xaafiyageeti bantta xuufiya siyanaw hayttan nooccu giya, nabbabishin wodiyanne wolqqa wurssenna, hachchi hachchi asay haasay go''ettiyo qaalatun xaafettida qantta qofa qashotun yiiccettida, oychchi zaaro haasaya, hanabaanne qanttan yootin asaa siyin siya siya giya hanabaa xaafanaw bessees. Xaafanchchati bantta hanabay asaassi porxxu gi odin (nabbabin) beettiyo wode he hanabaa shemppuwara diyabaa oottoogaadan ammanettoosona. 
3.2.2.	LO''O XAAFUWASSI ATTENNABATA
Lefa Qaalata: Qoodan keehi guutta gididi wolqqaama qaalata go''ettiyogee lo''o. 'Mulekka qantta qaalay diishin adussa qaalaa go''ettoppa.' -Jorjje Orweyla.
Lefa qofa qashota: Aybanne issi qofaawanne issi peeshoppe haraa qofa qashuwan go''ettoppa. Gitanne wolqqaama Ruusiya biittan qantta hanabaa xaafiya eranchchay, Yisaaqa Baabeeli yaagiis.
3.2.3. NABBABETUWA
Ha saaxinee wodala ganjjee haggaazaa immiyo qofaa ekkidi kachchi!

3.2.4. GITA QOFAA LAMMETTIYAGEETA
Haydan gita gutaraa kaallettiyageeti deriya loytti qofaa laamettiyogaaninne haasayidi ammanttiyogan erettoosona. Hagaappe kaallidi Winsstton Cherichchili na''antto olaa wode Birttaaniya biittaa xaatta moconay he wode olettiya yelagatanne horoophphilliya laagiyageeta galatanaassi haasayiidi, 'Asa na''i yo'uwan doomettiyogee keehi guuttanne daro gi eroppitte.' giyode lefanne guutta qofaa qasho shin wolqqaama haasaya. 
Assi baarigaara gidiya Uunayttide Istteetise biittaa kawo Pirankkiliin Ruusebeltti, hagaatoo giidi ziba haasaya he biittaa aqotaa metoy pelliyo wode minttettanaw haasayan, ''Nu aaho deriya medhdhana hanos; nu biittaappe oone kare kiyenna.'' He kawo lefa qofa qashuwa koyidi bari haasayan go''ettiyogan sintta xeera, A iraaduwa porogiraammee 'Fire Side Chats' geetetti salo guttanttuwan erettiis. I ba biittan keehi yaayama asa. Erettida kaalettiya asatuppekka issuwa. 

Ane hegaadan ziba haasayan erettida Hindde biittaa kaallettiyagee Mahatma Ganddi haasaayoogaa be''anaappe kasettidi Mahatma Ganddi daro hiraaga haasayan erettida, hanno gakkanaw salo gufanttuwan sa'a micettan A haasayaadan nashettiday baynnaagaa gidiyogaa erissays. Ha''i gakkanawkka sugetti baynna saro haasayan I qanttan go''etto qofa qashuwa asay ekkidi haasayees. Jorinaaliizimiya xeelliyagan Ganddi haasayido haasayay tamaare naati ha’’ikka siyanaw hayttaa wuqaawuqees. Nuuni ha haasayaa eranchchay lefanne wolqqaama bari qofaa qonccisso malaaliya qofa qashoy aattiyo kiittan ha''ikka keehippe malaalettos. I Jorinaliizimiyassi na'e haggaazaa. Ha hiraaganchchay zaarettidi yaagiis, ''Xaafetti kiyidabati gita wolqqa, yo'uwan qassi pilggi xeellennan coo tohayidi xaafiyo xaafoti kambban haattay  coo gede simmidi goggidi goshshanchchay waayetti zerido zerettaa shokki efiyogaa mala; ha bixaali baynna paradan go''ettiyo biiree nuussi haggaazaa immikkonne issitoo issitoo nuna xayssees. Ha bixaalaa oyqqennan yeddi bessiyo biiree guuttaa ganxxin tinkkiri ootti woriya marzze mala qassi loytti bixaalidi zawaappe kanttennan Piriissikko I woriya kaashshiyo miishsha A era haasayaw magani, haasay simmidi wurssettan laa ooni hagee qohees hagee maaddees yaagi pirddanee? Ooni qassi hagee lo''o hagee iita  yaagi wordduwanne tumaa dummayanaw oychchidi, maadiyageenne qohiyagee lo''onne iita geetettidi issippe go''ettobare asa na'i ba dooriyogaa doori eranaw bessees,'' yaagiis.




Meeziya 5
I.	Bixaalaa oyqqennan yeddi bessiyo biiree marzze mala giishin woyganaw koyettidee? Hegaa ne qofan qonccissada xaafa.

3.2.5. XAAFUWA YIPPAA
Xaafuwassi ichchashu yippay de'ees.
1.	Hanabaa kahan oyqqiyogaa
2.	Paxa naqaashaa pissiya
3.	Tuma birshshidi halchchiyogaa
4.	Harxxetta xaafuwa
5.	Zaaretti moliyogaa.
3.2.6. LO''O XAAFUWASSI GIIGA ‘CHEKILISTTIYA’
•	Xaafanchchati bantta hanabaappe balaa demmiyogan timirttiya demmoosona. Hagee tuma; xaafanchchati bantta balaappe tamaariyogee attenna gamma yo'o. Ha cheekilisttee nena ne xuufiyappe balaa demmanaw maaddees.
•	Qofaawan doommiya qofa qashuwa xaaf; ayssi giikko sophiyan doommiya qofa qashuwappe qonccees.
•	Wolqqaama sunttaanne peeshuwa go''etta. Sunqqotanne penqqota daro go''ettoppa. Wolqqaama peeshoy nabbabiyageetussi guuggiya misiliya medhdhees.
•	Dariya baggi lefa qofa qashuwa woykko sitta qofa qashuwa (qofaawa-sophe-peesho) go''ettanaw bessees.
•	Lefanne qantta qaalaa go''etta.
•	Ha''issaw asaa pashkkissiya leemiso haasayaa, siyanaw injjettenna, maatan yashissiyo, wogaa xaasiyogaanne issi issi dumma timirtte hiilla qaalata go''ettoppa.
•	Qofa qasho qanttanaw baaxettappe attin hum''o qaalay diikko xayssoppa. Darennaninne guuxxennan 18 qaalay issi qofa qashuwa go''ettikko gidees.
•	Peeshoy wodiyara issippe biyogaa akeeka. Leemisuwaw: Zino yiis, wontto yaana geetteesppe attin zino yaana woykko wontto yiis gookko.
•	Issi issi hanenna misiliyan kulkka oduwa sohuwan gelissoppa. Ha koshshiya xuufiya woykko misiliyan kaalliya menttuwan gelissanaw danddayettees.
•	Qoodan guuttanne mucurettida qonccissuwa go''etta. Nabbabiyageeta ufayssi wuttiyabaa xaafa.
•	Nabbabiyageetussi gelenna qaalaa issoynne attennan qonccissa.
•	Issi issi gelenna qaxiballo qaalaatussi mise qaalaa go''etta.
•	koyro oduwassi geluwa erissida izaawa simmadakka akeekissa. Leemisuwassi: Hegaa gishshaw Onakkoy .......................
•	Zaaroy imettibeenna oyshata aggaaga; oyshi denddaanne qassi sohuwara zaaruwa immanaw koshshees.
•	Ne polanaw danddayennabaa aybissinne qaalaa geloppa. Hegaa gishshaw neeni haasayayida asaa markkaw go''ettikko he izaawi immido markkatettaa leemisotoo go''etta.
•	Gita diraaman hanabaa asi siyidi oyqqana mala qantta qaalan xaafa. 
•	I haagaadan oottiis, yiilluwan xarapheezaa bubbuxiis, huuphiya buucciis, dereqiis, axiraariis, phenqqeshiis, otoruwa giiyiis yaagiya qofa qashota go''ettoppa.
•	Keehi koshshiya hum''o qaalaa qofa qashuwa doomettaninne wurssettan gelissa.
•	Waabee (pulttoy) haasayidoogaa sitta ogiyan akeekada gelissa. A haasayay keehippe koshshiyogaa erada ne I giidoogaa woygganaw koydaakkonne ne qofan (ne guussan) xaafiyogee cora qaalata go''ettanaadan oottees.
•	Asa haasayaa xaafayida ne qofaa (A guussaa) waabiyan amppada wotta.
•	Koshshenna qaalaa kessaychcha. Qoncce xaafoy qantta. Qofa qashuwa minttetta, ashilaalo qaalaa go''ettada nabbabiyagaw wuttissa.
•	Minttettoppa. Dariya baggi hanabaa lefaninne qoncciyan xaafa. Woyssa qaxiballo qofa qashuwa xeella demmada lefa qofa qashuwa gelissa.
•	Siyiyageerussi malaatada qoncciyan geliya qaalan wotta.
•	Cenggurssa xoqqu ootta nabbabada. Sitta oduwa sohuwara hayttan gelissanaw bessees.
Ha qommoora qonccida kaalliyo ogeta neeni kaallikko ne xuufee cora qaalaa go''ettennan corddodattidi siyanaw wayssenna qonccenne qantta gidees. Ane ha qommo qofan maayettidi kaalliyo ogeta go''ettoogaa be'oos. Wolqqaama peeshoti nabbabiyageetussi kahan misiliya medhdhoosona. Leemisuwaw: Kaamee mittaa dom''iis. Giyagaa: Kaamee keehi gita ankkaa dom''idi onggiis. Ha dom''iis giya peeshoy kaamiyaranne mittaara issippe biya qaala gidiyo gishshaw coraa qaalaa go''ettiyogaappe teqqees.
3.2.7. QANTTA QOFA QASHOY YO'UWAW KUUSHSHAA ERANAASSI MAADDEES
18 qaalaappe guuxxiyagaa issi qofa qashuwan go''ettiyogee nabbabiya asi qofaa waayettennan haasayanaw go''ees. Ubba qaalaa gede zaari qanttiyogaa gidennan diishin kulkka qofaappe kare kessenna ogiyan hara qaalaa sohuwan gelissana danddayettees. Ooni erii he qofa qashuwa qanttanaw gede zaari qeexiyo qaalay qofa qashuwassi tuussa qaala gidanaw danddayees. Naa''u woykko heezzu qofa qashuwa issippe xaaxi waaxo qofa qashoti attin lefa qofa qashuwa go''ettanaw bessees. Hegaa mala qofa qashuwassi 'nnenne shin' geetettiya gattiyageeta go''ettiyogee wodiyanne googaa guyye zaaretti inggaaziyogaa teqqanawnne qofa qashuwa qanttanaw maaddees. Issi issi golddodattidi lasttiqedan dafin aduqqi duuxxenna shida qaalata denttiichchiyogee qofa qashuwa molees.
3.3. MIIDIYA XAAFUWAW AYFE YO'OTA
Hanabaw koshshiyabatinne miidiya xaafuwan attenna bessiyabati asaassi, polettabaa woykko hanuwa xeelliyagan giigissiyogee miidiya xaafuwan ayfe yo'o geetettees. Hegeeta eridi xaafi oosuwan peeshshiyogee ha miidiya xaafanchchaw oosuwa keehippe lefayes. A oosuwakka xekkaa naagida, mulebay kumido aybinne kiyenna ooso oottees. Hanabaa xaafuwa kaalliyogee issi qofa qashuwa qanttan ziba qofa qashuwa qonccissa xaafa giyogaappe attin koshshiya qaalaa agganaassa gidenna. 
3.3.1. HANABAW KOSHSHIYABATA
Miidiya xaafoy naa''u ayfe baaso yo'otun giigees.
1.	Xaafuwaw koshshiyabati yedhdhi aadhdhennan geliyogee attennabaa. Leemisuwaw: Hayqqa asaa allaalliya xaafiyogee A sunttay, layttay woyssakkonnenne hayqquwaw gaasoy xaykko oottenna. Ha xaafetta yo'oti xaykko ha hanabay allaalle kessenna. Coo mera kiraara bidda gidees.
2.	Naa''antto baaso yo'oy ha bitaniya, hanuwa woykko polettabaa harabaappe laalettidi xaafettanaw bessees. Leemisuwaw: Onakko Onakkoy madaalaa xoonnidaagee .........
Hanabaw koshshiya yo'ota eriyogee xaafanchchaa poletabaa koyidi pilggettaa wococidi, haraa haasayaa gelissidi, qantta hanabaa geeshshidi eridi A haraappe dummayiyabaakka demmanaw ogiya malaattees.
3.3.2. DAAFAA
Koshshiyabata
Daafan hanabay keehi koshshiya odo. Hagee jorinaaliyassi keehi koyiyo allaallee giyaappe shammi go''ettiya shaqaxa mala. 
•	Sunttaanne ha hayqqida (masunxxida) bitaniya erissidi (anne A qatuwa qonccissiyogaa)
•	Daafay poletto wodiyanne sohuwa.
•	Bishikiliitiya daafa gidikko, bishikiliitiya qommoy.
•	Gaasoy (waabe gidiya allaallee xaafiya kifilee immidoogee).
•	Naqaashaa pulttoy (waabee).
•	Hayqqoynne masunxxiyogee awan hanidaakko sohoy.
•	Ay keena masunxxidaakkonne.
•	Yeeho gidikko yeehuwaw (baliyaw) giigettiyogaa qonccissiya naqaashay.
•	Markkaynne hanotaa kaalli xeellida beeruwa oosanchchay.
Naagetta: Hagee mooro, daafay gaasoy dirbbaa tamaa eexi laagoogaa ushshaa uuyidi laagoogaa yaagada ha daafa gattidaagaa boqosuwa (balaa) allaallee xeelliyo beero oosanchchay qonccissennan diishin ubbakka xaafanchchaappe naagettenna. 
3.3.3. DANUWA
Xaaciya wodala ganjjee danuwa pissiya oyqqees; danuwa oottaagaa oyqqidi qachchidi yo'uwa pilggees. Ha wodala ganjjee oyqqi qachcho balanchchaa xeelliyagan ambbaa giigisso woykko dano chilootan ha qashetta izaawa asay kaallanaadan oottees. Wodala ganjjee danuwa be'anaashin awdenne dano allaalliya xaafo naqaashaa markkatuppe demmanaw danddayees. Darotoo danuwa xeelliyagan beeruwa oosanchchata oychchin, danoy gakkoogeetuppenne markkatuppe naqaashay shiiqees.
KOSHSHIYABATA
•	Muleera qohoy gakkido uraa erissiyabay ubbay
•	Dano oosoy poletto hanotay
•	Gallassay, wodeenne sohoy
•	Hanttaara danoy, hayqquwaw woykko masunxxidogaw beeruwappe xaafetta gaasotay, aakime naqaashay danuwaw denttettoynne qohetta keettaawaw zokkuwan kase de'iyabay qoncce gidikko
•	Danuwa polo ooso miishshaa, xayabaassi gatiyanne, tilla gidikko wuussaa ogiya.
•	Sirettiyageetussi mootoy kumetta gidana xaykko sunttay xaafettenna shin malaatiyabati de'ikko
•	Ooratta hanotay (kase hani aadhdhabaappe dummabay diikko).
•	Markkaa qaalay, qohoy gakko izaawunne xaacee
•	Naqaashaw waabee (pulttoy)




Meeziya 6
I.	Issi kambban danoy polettidoogaa naqaashaa pultto gidiya asappe demmada oduwaw haniya hanabaa xaafa.

3.3.4. ISPPORTTIYA
Cora ispporttenne kaassa qommoti de'oosona. Xaafanchchaappe koyettiyabay hanabay wudissidi xeelliyo ha xeelliya attuma asanne macaasa he kaassa xeelliyageeta ezgganaw shoobettaaetanne ha kaassaa sohuwa hani kantta oorattabi diikko cenggurssaa xoqqu ootti haasay erissiyo wode qoncciyan odettees.
QUXARUWA
Kulkka yo'uwa kaalli geliyabata ispporttiyaw hanabaa gaazeexan xaafiyo wode maaddoosona. Nashshiyageetinne haratikka televizhzhiiniyappenne iraaduwappe gela gooliyanne issi issi wozanan noocu oottiyobaa be'oosona (siyoosona). Kulkka oduwa kaalliya oduwa kaalliya odoy hanabaa, ufayssiyanne garanttiyabaa, he kaassan hanida ayfe yo'oy, koshshiyo gishshaw issi kaassanchchaa kessidi haraa gelissiyogaa, kaassanchchay kunddi masunxxobay h.h.m. xaafettoosona. Ispporttiyan kulkka odoti xeellin beettiyanne naaqaashaw wayssennabata asi bana ufayssiyo gishshaw go''ettiyobata.
KOSHSHIYABATA
•	Gooliya (qoodaa)
•	Citatu sunttaa 
•	Ispportte qommuwa
•	Awdenne awan kaassay kaa''ettidaakko
•	Ayfe poletabata (kaassan)
•	Gooba kaassanchchata
•	Kaassan demmido ooso ayfeta
•	Xeelliya asaa qoodaa, eeshshaa
•	Masuxxidaagee (diikko) 
•	Kaassay doometti poletto wodiya
•	Kase kaa''etta kaassan hani kanttabaa.
NAAGETTA: Ispporttiya oduwa xeelliyageeti pashkkanne ufayttiya asa. Issi coraban coo geloppa. Ufayssiya (miichchiya) qaalata (qonccissuwa) go''etta. Olawnne olanchchatussi go''ettiyo qaalata gelissoppa.
Meeziya 8
I.	Issi citatay haraara adhdhida saaminttaa toho kuwaasiya kaa’’in doonaagaanne xoonettaaga qonccissiya oduwa xaafa.

3.4. DAASHSHAA XAAFUWA
Daashshay miidiyassi issi sintta (yo'uwa) gidishin daashshaa xaafoy ubba miidiyawkka wotto woga. Daashshaa xaafiyo wode xaafettanaw bessiyabaa aggi aadhdhanaagee daro meto. Xaafettabatuppe pacay beettikkokka lo''o gidenna. Daashshay miidiyan kuushsha qofa oyqqidaagaa gidishin xaafanchchaa qofaa oyqqidaagaa gidishin xaafanchchay daashshaassi diya tumu yo'uwa  qoridi, birshshettaa mucuridi xaafees.
Ha dumma porogiraamiya xaafiyogee Toophphiya miidiyan darotoo meezetido allaalle gidishin A xaafiyogee tamaariyageetikka meeziyan loohidi lo''o eranchcha gidanaw maaddees. Daashshaa xaafoy hara oduwa xaafuwappe lo''onne dumma. 
3.4.1. XAAFUWA HIILLAA
Qofaa qaalaw (qofa qashuwaw) birshshi laammiyogee xaafo hiilla geetettees. Xaafo hiillaw usppun xekkati de'oosona.
6.	Wozana ayfe xeelaa (qofaa ekuwa)
7.	xaafiyo deriya eriyogaa
8.	Qottaa demmi maaciyogaa
9.	Harxxetta xaafuwa
10.	Zaareto xaafuwa
11.	Geedettaa
Qofaa wozana ayfiya xeelliyogee ha xaafanaw koyido daashshaassi diya misiliya (yo'uwa issi diri shiishshi) qofan oyqqidi woraqatan wottanaw injjettiyagaa gidishin xaafanchchay ha issi diri shishshido yo'uwa xaafuwa gaacci aggees. Xaafiyobatussi daro qonccissiyobay de'anaw danddayees. Hegee ubbaykka yedhdhi aadhdhennan xaafettanaw bessees. Ha issi diri shiishsho yo'uwa ayfe yo'o kanchchiya gidennan diishin ekkidi qanttiyogee palanttenna allaalle. Neeni ayfe yo'uwa qoppiyo wode xaafiyo qofay tololattidi yees. Yaatiyo gishshaw xaafuwaw koyro xekkay xaafana qofaa kahan issi diri shiishshi huukkuriyogaa.

Awdekka xaafiyobatussi siyanaw giigida deree diyogee erettidabaa. Xaafanchchay ha deriya hayttan lawhu gi geliya yo'uwa mucuuridi shiishshees. Ha xaafiyo xekka demmidi maaraa kaallidi xaafiyogee miidiya xaafuwan keehi koshshiya allaalle. Harxxetta xaafoy simmidi zuuqqanaasa. Zuuqeti simmin xuufee xekkaa naagidanne boolimay de'iyogaa gidees. Zuuqayda koyro ne qofaa xeelloppa co''u gaada kokkorenna, qaalaa birshshettay meto medhdhees gaada yayyennan timettaakko gakkanaashin xaafa. Yaata simmada balaa harqqa giigissanaw koshshees. Issibay attennan ubbay yo'oy woraqatan keexettanaw koshsheesppe attin koyroora bali baynna qofa qashuwa xaafanaw baaxettoppa.

Zaareto xaafoy harxxettaa bolli diya ufuraa (senkkuwa) qizaggi diggichchidi geeshshiyogaa xeellees. Issi issi hanenna qaalay geellidan geelidaakkonne pixiri diggiichchiyogaa. Giido yo'uwa guyye zaarettiyogaa, xaafishin barqqidabay de'ikko diggiichchiyogaanne ha mucureti giigida yo'uwa qanttan menttuwan gelissiyogaa. Hegee geeshshanne sire baynna hanabaa xaafi giigissanaw maaddees. Hagaa xaafidi xaafanchchay issi issi xamassaasa qofa qashuwa maxi kessiichchidi harqqetti giigida yo'o kanchchiya xaafi oyqqanaw koshshees. Hegan balay de'ikko de'iyosaappe yaara haara maxi diggirggidi zaaretidi xaafiyo wode mucureti giigida yishkka xuufee (menttoy) giigees.

Ezggiya woykko nabbabiyageetussi ha shiishshidi qori giigissidi dooridi xaafiyo qaalay kahan misiliya medhdhees. Xaafanchchay ha misiliya medhdhiyogaa meezetidi dumma dumma xaafiyobatun asaassi misiliya medhdhiya qaalata doori go''ettiyogan halaale gidees. 

Ha qaalaa qoppidi guuggiyan medhdhiyo misilee ha oduwassi (hanabaw) meraa immees. Siyiyo wode yo'oykka ha qaalaa baggaara asaassi zambbettidi hayttan wodhdhees. Ha qaalan amppidi giigissiyogee odo kanchche gidenna malaataa qunxxissi bessees. Odiyogee qoncce. Beni nu aawati odoy ayfiyara gelees giyogaadan, odoy qofaa laamissees bessoy qassi yo'uwa wagaggissees.

Daashshaa xaafoy wayssees geetettiis. Issi issi ha xaafuwassi go'etto ogeti hagaadan qonccidosona. Daashshay issi oduwassi na'e (keehippe koshshiya kifilee). Koyro daashshaa demmi simmidi aara gayttabaa caridi gujjeettees. Haray qassi ha daashshaa xaafiyo wode kuushsha qofaappe kare kiyiyyogee keehi mooro. Daashshaa xaafiyo wode xaafanchchay awdenne kuushsha kare qofaappe kiyennan oottanaw bessees. Daashshaa xaafiyo wode haagaattoo ootta xaafa giya wogi baawa. Qofa qashota kasiya kaaluwa maaran xaafiidi bali de'ikko giigissidi ha bollaara qonccida usppun xekkata naagidi coo gede xaafuwa daxettees.
Leemisuwaw: Oduwassi hanabay hagaattoo xaafettees. Daraaritu Tuullu ba biittaw, Toophphiyassi hachchi naa''u worqqaa wottan qolchchada demmaasu. Yo'uwan qassi hanabaassi daashshay hagaattoo nabbabettees. 'Daraarita hachchi naa''u worqqaa xoonnaasu.

Odoy tumaa odiyogaappe attin darobaa corddodayidi biddiyogaa gidenna. Hegaa gishshaw odoy giigiyoy lefanne siyanaw deexxenna qofa qashota go''etteetesppe attin sunqqotanne penqqota miicciiridi xaafiyogee neeni gaana koyido qofaa siyiya asay erennaadan xubbiyo gishshaw ha qaalata go''ettennan aggigiyakko lo''o. Oduwa xaafoy wodala ganjjee bari huuphen hanabaa bari ayfiyan be''idinne siyoogaadan yo'uwa tillayees.
3.4.2. DAASHSHAA
Daashshay xaafuwa qonccissanaw kane yo'o. Xaafanchchay lefan erisso kanchche gidennan diishin nabbabuwaw injjettiya hanabaa qonccissidi xaafanaw bessees. Xaafanchchay issi baggi zokkuwa zaarenna woykko haraw morggiya oyqqenna. I tumaa baggi simmidi ayfe yo'uwa birshshees, xaafiidikka qonccissees. Daashshay wurssettan odo xalaalaa aattiyogaa gidennan diishin zokkuwara tumaakka gacci xillissidi kessees.

Daashshay oduwassi naqaashaa puullayees; maattamettiya gaazeexawkka boolimaa naaganaw baaso gidees. Daashshay xaafetta allaallee muleera nabbabiyageetussinne oduwa siyiyageeti allaxxanaadankka oottees. Daashshaa xaafoy yo'uwa erannaadan ay meraanakka gidanaw danddayees; xaafanchchaassikka qassi oottanaw giiganne pilggettaa hekkaa darissees. 

Ooratta odoy kuttoy haatta mittanaashin giigidi asaa hayttan wodhdhana koshshees. Daashshay xaafiyo wode keehi lefanne asi siyiyo wode allaxxissees. Daashshan oychchi zaaro haasayay, waabiya haasayaynne hanabay xaafettees. Oduwan tilla oychchi zaaroy nabbabiyagaw yo'uwa qonccissees. Haray qassi ha allaallee xeelliyo asi oosuwan de'iyogaanne haasayiyageeti go''ettiyo peeshshoykka asaassi kahan misiliya medhdhees. Oduwan kulkka yo'uwa kaafiya qofay daashshan xaafettees. Asaa siyanaw ufayssi noocu oottiya yo'oy koyruwan (doomettan) gelees. Xaafanchchay daashshaa xaafiidi asaa noocu oottiya qaalaa go''ettidi asi he hanabaa daashshan washidi geliyogaadan mikiikissi xaafiyo wode he izaawukka haraykka siyanaw ufayttees. Kulkka yo'oy oduwassi hum''o gidiyogaa palanttenna ogiyan wotta. Issitoo issitoo mikiikaa darissiyogee asaa siyishin salettiyo hanotaykka de'ees. Amarida dooretta qofa qashotinne hanabati oduwa mal''ettoosona. Qaalaa doori go''ettiyogee daashshaw keehippe koshshiya yo'o. Waabee immiyo naqaashaa issoynne attennan coo buuri gelissiyogee attennabaa gidenna. Oduwassi hum''oy hanabaassi zokko meqetta (uuttaw muqquuqulo mala). Aani keten''i eqqidi hanabati mittaw balaa mala oduwa dumma dumma ginaa xarccoosona. 

Xaafuwaw doometti meto miishsha. Koyruwan geliya qofa qashota bidinttaa giddoppe sulqqunttuwa qaphiyan qoriyogaadan maxa shiishshaasa. Hagee xaafana menttuwa huuphiyan mintti yishkki ootti oyqqanaw maaddees. Aybanne ne hanabaw kifiliyan kaaxettanaw danddayissees giyoban xaafuwa demmana danddayaasa. Ha kifilee neeni ha oduwa keehi akeekidoogaa qonccissinne neessi de'iya doonaa eraa qonccissiyo kifile. Hanabaassikka meraanne qottaa giigissi moliyo kifilee. Darotoo lo''o xaafoy lo''onne sitta gidiyogaa ne huuphiyan oyqqa; lefanne sitta qofa qashoy hanabaw tuussanne xuuqedan keehippe koshshiya allaalle.
3.4.3. DAASHSHAA QOMMOTA
Daashshaa xaafoy oduwassi hanabaw denddo gidishin issibaassi xaafetta naqaasha, odanaw doonaa kumiya, oduwassi puulaa immiyanne asaa sissishin allaxxissiyabaa. Daashshaa xaafiyogaa kanchchee bari huuphen barkka kumetta oduwa aattiyogaa gidenna. Daashshay aattiyo oduwa kaafees. A bolli kuushsha qofaappe garssaara hara yo'oykka carettin hanabay kumetta gidees.
DAASHSHAA QOMMUWA GARSSAN
•	Izaawssi (issibaw) kumetta naqaashay
•	Asay hashshukkonne giyo hanotan mucurettida hanabay
•	Laamiyassi (dichchaassi) hanabay
•	Ciima hanabati
•	Guyyiya/dendduwa (hanabaw) 
•	Deriya gaytotaa daashshaa
•	Mali be'o hanabaa (curtain raiser)
•	Hanabay poletto galla daashshaa
•	Haydaa daashshaa
•	Oychchi ekko naqaashaa daashshaa
Asaa kumetta naqaashay, oduwa daashshay, hanabay poletto gallassaa daashshay, haydaa daahshsaynne oychchi ekko naqaashaa daashshati Toophiyanne xaafonne coraa gattiyo naqaashaa miidiyan keehiippe meezettidosona. Hageetuppe wurssetta allaallee darotoo oosuwan pe'ees; oyshettiyagee aybanne hanabaw metootiyobi baawa oychchiyagee ha appe ekko naqaashaa simmidi siqimmees. Oyshaa daashshay darotoo asaa oychchiyobaa: oychchiyogeeti: erettida asaa, issibaa xeelliyagan dumma eray de'iyogeeta, wurssetta xekkaa gakkanaashin luxidaageetanne issiban allaallee xelliyogeeta. Hegaa gishshaa ha oychchi ekko daashshay waananaw danddayii giikko:
•	Xaafanchchay baw oychchi ekko daahsha kanchche.
•	Naqaashaa koyidi oychchin zaaro haasayaa ubbaa.
•	Issi guuttabaa xelliyagan corabaa oychchoogaa.
DAASHSHAA MAARAA OYTTUWA
Daashshay muletoo xaafiyo wode xuggunida heezzu zooze xaafo meran xaafettees. Hagaa wurssettan hanabay gakkosaa qonccissees. Xaafanchchay kase baassi de'iya xaafo hiillan go''etti xaafanaw danddayees. Hanabay xaafettiyo wode A garssan diya yo'uwaw doomettaappe poluwa gakkanaw issoy issuwara kiriyan ohetti uttiis. Hanabay xaafettanaappe kase assi qoncce ayfe yo'oynne hoollee daana bessees. Hegeekka issi asaw mule naqaashaa xaafiyogaa, issibaa tamaarissiyogaa, issi qoncciya kessiyogaanne issi muttaamuro yo'uwa qonccissiyogaa gidanaw danddayees. Hagee halchchidi pilggettaaninne halchchuwan polettees. Hanabay doomettan, gidduwaninne wurssettankka ayfe yo'uwa kelkkanaw danddayees. gidduwan kulkkaassi hum''uwan keehi koshshiya naqaashay, daashshay, kase guyyee (denddo) naqaashaynne ha oychchin zaaretabay issoy issuwara kiriyan sihettiya qofa qashoti xaafettoosona.

Hanabaw (oduwaw) wurssettan keehi akeekana koshshees. Ha gidduwan xaafettiyabati ubbay wurssettan asaassi ziba kiittaa hayttaw zambbana bessees. Daashshay wuriyode kulkka yo'oy doommees; yuuyi yuuyidi wurssettan qassi ha kulkka yo'uwan xaaxettees.

Ziba daashshaa xaafanaassi hanabay poletto sohuwa (hanuwa gakki be'iyogaa), naqaashaa oychchanaw yaa haa bichchaariyogaa, woxxi qaaxxabaa go''ettidi wodala ganjjee hanabaa gidiya keenaa shiishshanaw bessees. Nabbabiyageeti naqaasha kanchche gidennan diishin issi asassi diya assumatettaa, dentto yo'ota, ooratta demettabaa ooso miishshata, eta sohuwanne meretan hani kanttabata saamettidi eranaw koyiyoogaa xaafanchchay dogenna so ooso oottanaw bessees. 
3.4.4. DAASHSHAA SHIISHSHIYO WODE
•	Keettay ay malatiyakko, asay ay malaa maayidaakkonne waani haasayiyakko wodala ganjjee xeellan qonccissees.
•	Teeppiya go''ettanaw koshshiyo gaasaykka teeppiyan duuqqi oyqqidi wodala ganjjee bana laallanttiya yo'uwa kalkkotenna qoncciyan oottanaasa.
•	Danddayetta keenaa daro oyshaa oychcha, neessi gelennabaa qassi laa hagaa taassi oonee qonccissanaw danddayay?'' Yaagada oychcha.
•	Ay gaytotaanne waabiyara gattada sokisola.
•	Shiishsho qofaa sohuwara xuufiyaw laamma.
•	Koyro harxxetta oduwassi kuushsha yo'uwa xaafa.
•	Daashshay asaa xeelliyabaa gidikko ha asaa haasayaa go''ettada ne qofan aagaa waabee nabbabiyagaara qofaa laamettana gakkanaashin xaafa.
•	Ne xaafoogaa hana keenaa darotoo salettennan nabbabada wurssettaa gakkanaashin giigissuwan kutuuta.
3.4.5. LO''O XAAFUWASSI AYFE YO'OTA
1. Kulkka shoobiya qonccenne lefa ootta.
2. Lo''onne tishsha gidikko haraa haasayaa go''etta.
3. Leemisoti asaa paskkissikkonne hanabaa bessikko go''etta.
4. Hanabaa ne qofan laammada qantta qaalatun go''etta.
5. Lo''o xaafuwa besoy tishsha pissiya hegaassi waabiyara I diyo man''iya baada gaytta.
6. Ne gaana koyidobaa era simmada xaafuwa doomma.
7. Sinttan xaafettiyabati ayfe yo'uwa oyqqida amarida na'e qaalatu kanchchee xaafettin hanabaw quxaro gidees.
8.  Hanabaa suure maaraa oytta. Issi huuphe yo'uwappe haraw sinttawnne guyye yinggirada yo'uwa balbbuqoppa. Shooshshaa hemetaa oottada yaanne haanne biyogee oottenna; sitta ogiyan xaafa.
Meeziya 8
I.	Hara lo’o xaafuwassi ayfe yo’o gaada ne qoppiybi diikko ha imettida daa’otu xaafa.

3.5. CIIMMANNE PILGGIYO PISSIYA
Pilggi shiishshiyo pissee hara xuufiyappe muleera keehi dummattees. Dummatettay keehi wolqqaama yo'ota pilggi demmidi pissiya shiishshiyo gishshataassa. Pilggidi pissiya shishshiyogee daro wodiya ekkees gaasotaykka tuma yo'oy wayssennan lefan beettenna. Ha tumaa demmanay wodala ganjjee woxxi qaaxxiyo wode A cora metoti (pagalanaw wayssiyageeti) gakkoosona. Ha dumma dumma xubeta kanttidi wodala ganjjee tumaa wochchees. Hagee bookkidi biittaa xaggaappe shuchchay kiyin A shibiliqiyan phalqqidi tumaa koyiyoogaa mala. Hagaa bolli qassi ne qofaa gujjiyogee anttettenna.

Pilggidi pissiya shiishshiyogee bari huuphen bana danddayda tuugiya toossiya tiraara sitti giya ooso. Keehi dallo ooso. Geellidan cawaa xiiri tuggatidi wodala ganjjee ha tumaa demmiyode maaraa oyttanaw kana kaassa. Ha naqaashaa dendduwa guyyiya minttettiyogaa, waabiyappe naqaashaa koyi demmiyogaanne A qassi pissiya shiishshiyo wogaa kaalli maaraa oyttidi koyro harxxetta xuufiya xaafiyogaa, ciimma pilggettan pissiya demmiyogee waabiyappe shiishshidi naqaashaa birshshettay diyo tishsha ogiyan ushachcha kushiya oyqqidi giigissees. 
Meeziya 9
i.Naa’’u asati maqettidi wolqqaama kobabaa oottidi kammin ka’o giidoo allaalliya yo’uwa wayssiya hanotan pilgga demmido pissiya giigissada xaafa.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------.

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------.

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------.
3.5.1. PILGGETTAA HANOTAA 
Pilggi shiishshiyo pissee hara ubba pissetuura geedariyode xekkankka dummattees. Ha pissiya shiishshiyo wode go''ettiyo ooso miishshati (oyshaanne pilggettaa) ha ooso miishshati tishshatettan yedhdhi aadhdhennan go''ettiyogeeta. Pilggiyo pissee hani kanttabaanne polettabaa gidennan diishin yo'uwanne A hanotaa koyi demmin giigees. Ha wogata mule guppa kanttoppa.
•	Pissee wolqqa yo'uwa xeellees.
•	Daro metuwanne xubiya kanttidi naqaashaa demmees.
•	Yo'uwassi de'iya beeraa (go''aa) muleera xaphuwappe xeeraa gakkanaw qonccissees.
3.5.2. BOOKKIYO SO OOSUWA
Pilggiyo pissee hara qommo pissetuppe dariya baggi xaaduquwa koyees; xaafanchchay mooroynne balay beettenna mala keehi akeekaaninne balan ba xaafiyobaa hanabay moorettennaadan bollaw garssaw yeggidi geedettaa gittidi oottanaw bessees. Ha oosuwan xaafanchchay mazggabaa gede gelees. Ha oosoy daro danddayaanne genccaa koyees; wodiyakka ekkees; qamminne galla woraqatan sheekkidi oottiyo ooso. Tumay hegan xarapheezaa bolli deenna. Ubbay coo kumidi beettenna cora qommo xubeti de'oosona; hegaa ubbaa shuchchaa qeri kanttin tumay beettees. Hegee bookki demmiyo so ooso. Pilggi demmiyo pissee tumaa salettennan biittaa garssaw duge zaari boohaa tullayidi tumu yo'uwa demmiyogaa geetettees. Hegan xaafanchchay bari qofaa gelissidi go''ettanaw mulekka eenetenna. Hagee sayinise pilggettaa mala. Tumay tumaa bolla de'ees. Tumaaassi kuushshi tumaa bari huupheppe attin hara ogee baawa. 
3.5.3. LO''O, MINONNE DALBBA 
Ammanettiyo eranchchay yaagi xaafiis, ''Nuuni ciimma pissiya dariya baggi pilggi demmi shiishshiyo pisse geettees.'' Ayssi giikko nabbabiyageetussi yo'uwassi koshshiya tumaa, ogiya, ha tumay goossosaa, cora saara ne ha tumaa demmiyo qatuwanne tumaassi de'iya dendduwa qoncciya kessees. Nuuni tumi aybakkonne nabbabiyagaassi qonccissos. Ciimma pissee ha wodiya gaazeexaayyoo meraa immees, lefa, lo''o, minonne dalbba. pilggi shiishshiyo pissee asaassi geema gidanaw bessenna; qoncce gidana bessees. Ha pissee asaassi hayttaa haydaa wogaa xaassobaanne asaw hayttan geli malaaliya qofay qosetti attaagaa kaashi laallees. Issi asi issi boqosobaa unddenna wodiya biitti sa'i siyo giidi baridi wottanaw danddayees; hegaa ha pilggi shiishshiyo pissee ogiyan miccees. 'Hage asay giyay be''an parssuwa gillan kammay giyogaa mala. Leemisuwassi: Shemppuwa woridi muuman tuccido yo'uwa wodala ganjjee pilggidi qoncciya kessana danddayees.

Ciimmanne pilggettaa suulissidi demmiyo pissee eranchchatun issi ogiyappe aadhdhiya dumma dumma ogetun qol''on godaa baqqi attosaappe wuygiya oykkidi kare kiyees. Issi issi wolqqaamanne ammananaw deexxiya miidiyaw shiishshiyo pissee ha pilggettan demmoogaa. Hagee xeellin beettiya tumaassi wodala ganjjeti keehi xoqqanne koshshiya man''iya immidi salettenan meezetidi oone kashi geenna mali be'iyo oosuwaw marxxafi denddidi koyro, naa''antto, heezzantto zaaretti aatti yeggi xeellii xeellidi maataa garssan narppe xayin koyiyogaadan hayqqi halidi demmiyo tumaa. Yo'uwassi dendduwa oyssa golan quccidi waabiyan hidootaa wottidi koyi demmidi koshshees giyo pissiya shiishshiyo hiillan go''ettidi keehi ciimma pilggettaa gittidi demmi shiishshiyo pissee poletteesnne hani kanttabaanne pulttuwappe guyyeera giyan peeshshi kanttobaa bari garssan huukkurees. Keehi koshshiya allaalletinne yo'oti nabbabiyageetussi qoncciyan yo'uwara issippe biyanne ziba hanotan qonccissiyo wode qosettosaappe gaxaa kiyosona. Pilggi pissiya shiishshiya wodala ganjjeti muletoo asay kammi kanttanaw koyiyobaa dembbaa kessoosona. Hageetuppe amaridaageeti wogaa xayssiya, asaa qohiyanne asaa maataa yedhdhiya meeze oosota. Wolqqaama goshshanchchay ottaa phalqqi goyidi shooqaa muchchuwa ootti liiqissidi kataa zeridi murutaa demmiyogaadan wodala ganjjee sheniya mirqqidi maacidi naqaashaa shiishshanaw biittaa xaggaa gakkanaw duge zaari boohaa nohayidi yaa haa paniissidi kareppe waabiya oychchin zaaro zaaruwappe qaphiya qori issi waabee A koshshaa shayaa xaphuwan irxxissana xaykko haraa oyshan biyosaa yiyosaa teqqidi bari ayfiya maxiniyan meeccidi huuphiya yuushshiya oyshan wozanaa bashshin banan ammanettiya waabiyan wolqqan tumaa soofiya gelissees. 

Ha ooso buussan wodala ganjjee naqaashaa shiishshiyo hiillan baaxettidi oduwa xaafuwanne pissiya giigissuwa walalayi aggees. Ha oosuwan keehi koshshiyagee issibaa birshshiyo eraa poshiyogaa hani kanttabaa, yo'uwanne qofaa battidi qizaggiyogaa. Ha oosuwan waabiya beeray coo malan hariya suqoy bulla geennan naqaashaa demmuwanne tumaa shiishshuwa. 

Waabee godan kaqidi asay bari som''uwa xeelliyo herega mala ciimmanne pilggiyo pissiyan tumaassi dendduwa (doomettaanne) pilggettaa milxxi ootti bessees. Ay pissenne shiishshiyo wode waabiyakko biyogee attenna miishsha. 
3.5.4. WAABEE AY KEENA LO''O?
Waabee ammanettiyo tumakkanne wordduwa shaakkiyo cora ogeti doosona.
Kase Ammanettiyogaa – Ha waabee kase likke yo'uwa qonccissii?
Shatinttuwa – Waabee immido naqaashay tumakko worddokko palanttennan shatinttiya ooso miishshaa shiishshanaw danddayii?
Akeekaa _ Waabee bari immido tumu yo'uwa akeeki erii?
Issippe Biyogan _ Naqaashay tumaara issippe bii?
Gawaa Geshshatettaa _ Waabee yaanne haanne qel''i qel''enne (gawaa geeshshee?)
3.5.5. NAA''U DAAFABATA
A. Naqaashaa pissiya shiishshiyogaw luxettaa qommoy. Leemisuwassi: Dumma dumma xaleta xeelliyagan shiishshiyo naqaashay hara asaw (payyatettaa hiillaappe kareera diyageetussi gelenaagaa.
B. Wodala ganjjee paxa hanabaa xaafi bana yarshshidi demmo naqaashaa yedhdhi aadhdhanaw eenennaagaa.
3.5.6. PILGGIYONNE CIIMMA PISSIYAW KAALIYO ALLAALETA
1. Kuushshaa demma.
2. Ne xaafo allaalliya awaaninne coo gede zaara oloppa. Ne ola aggikko ha ne tiran ekkada shiishsho naqaashay xayana. Hegaa gishshaw ushachcha kushiyan oyqqa.
3. Ne awdenne go''ettiyo hiillan kulkka yo'uwa xaafa.
4. Ne oosoy maaraa oyqqidi neessi siree baynnan qonccana gakkanaashin haniira yaatana gaada nerkka ne huuphiyan haasaya.
5. Ne hanabay xeeraa gakki huuphiya kiyanaashin yigga xeelliyogaa aggoppa. 
6. Seliseddida hanabaa sittayana gakkanaashin yigga xeella. Seliseddaa neeni sokisollada sawettin lo''o leemiso gidees.
7. Pinnanaw koshshiya sohuwa yigga xeella. Issi issi wuttaalo hanabaa ne xaafikko nabbabiyageetussi haddiranaw dees; hegaa gishshaw waata laamma xaafanakko nenaara zoretta. Wodala ganjjee lefaappe biidi huuphiya kiyidi deexxiya hanabaa nabbabiyageeti sirennan ammaneti xaafidoogaa eranaw bessees. Wodala ganjjiyassi kulkka oosoy nabbabiyageetussi siree baynna naqaashan amppidi tumaa yootiyogaa. Tumay koyro xafuwa demmidi sohuwan sohuwan pilggiyo wode siree baynnan geeyi geeyi bees.
3.6. CORAA GATTIYO NAQAASHAA
Coraa gattiyo naqaashaa xaafoy hara qofaa laamettanaw xaafiyo meede qommuwappe dummattees.  Coraa gattiyo naqaashaa xaafanchchati xaqqayiyageeta geetettoosona. Naqaashaa xaafo hiillay xaphuwappe xeeraa gakkanaw oychchi zaaro haasayaa mala. Hagee Toophphiyan dariya baggi kambban diyageeti xaafidinne nabbabidi erenna hanotay de'iyo gishshaw beni wogan de'iyageeti siyidi oduwa allaalliya kiitaa eranaw maaddees. Hegaappe kaallidi ha coraa gattiya oduwa giigissi asaa sissanaw ay eeshshan go''ettanaakko, assi de'iya maaraa mankkaa seeraa deriyassi waatidi (ay hayyuwan) go''ettidi ooso ayfiya asa sintti aattanaakkonne woxxi qaaxxabaa kaalli xeelloos. Ha naqaashaa xaafuwa haraa xaafo bilatuppe ay keenaanne waani dummattiyakkonne qaalati waani ha kiitaa aattanaw go''ettiyo ogetuura (mereta cenggurssaa, qantta haasayaa, viiduwanne televizhzhiiniyassi) waatidi beettiyabata demmidi misiliyan amppidi kiitaa bessiidi aattanaakko ha oduwa giigissiyagee waatidi oduwa maaraa oyttiyakko ane kaallidi be'os.

Iraaduwana gidikko xaafanchchati misiliya medhdhanaw pootuwa go''ettokkona bantta qaalan, cenggurssaaninne haasayaa aleequwan qanttidi ezggiyageetussi kahan misiliya medhdhidi oduwa giigissanaw baaxettidi wurssettan hanabaa ezggiya jamaassi yo'oy qonccin misilee A kahan simerettees. Leemisuwaw: Booraa xeelliya oduwa aattikko kacaamanne zimotaara gaddulla booray ezggiyagaassi beettees woykko I kase heeran be'ido eriyo booray (eta soo booray) assi huuphe garssan karhhi gees. Hariyabaa odikko haree maataa miyagee, caanaa zokkuwa zebbin giyaa biyagee woykko caaggiya haree siyagaw kahan ha booraagaadan beettees. Yaatiyo gishshataw hagaatto ezggiyageetussi huuphiyan misiliya medhdhiya odoy iraadooniyan xaafi sissiyogee xaafanchchaassi wozanaa koshaa alees.
3.6.1. CORAA GATTIYO NAQAASHAW BAASO KOSHSHAA
Coraa gattiyo naqaashay cenggurssanne misile xeellin beettiyabaa, ubbaakka siyada be'aasa. Oduwassi de'iya qottaakka be'ada sissa kanchche gidennan allaxxissees. Leemisuwaw: Wottaanne ispporttiya xeelliyagan coraa gattiyo naqaashaappe dariya baggi sissaanne attin yo'uwa eriyogaappe kanttidi asaa allaxxissees. Kaameeran gelissanaappe kasetidi haasayaa mucuridi giigissiyo wodee keehi xuntta; coraa gattiyo naqaashay issi iitabaa qoncciya kessanaw halaale. Ha naqaashaa inddusttiree darotoo issi yo'uwa qoncciyaninne qanttan xaafiya uraa koyees.

3.6.2. ERISSO, QONCCISSO GIDENNA
Coraa gattiyo naqaashaa xaafiyageeti issibaa hayttan olidi lawhu gi wottaa shokkiyogaappe attin yo'uwa baqe ootta qonccissays giidi corddoday biddiyogee koyettenna. Ha xaafanchchati simmidi lefan asaw odanaw danddayettiyanne sitta hanuwan xaafetta hanabaa koyoosona. Keehi daro giishin issi hanabaa televizhzhiiniyan odiyogee naa''u daqiiqaa gidishin issibaa odanaw gida wodee 20ppe bi 30 sekondde. Ha wodee issi issi wulaato hanabata qonccissanaw gidenna shin I xaafettoy hayttaassa; guutta wodiyan hayttan odidi woykko kahan bessi kanttanaassa. Gidoshin adussanne keehi koshshiya allaalle gidikko loytti qonccissiyogee attenna. Ha naqaashaa xaafiyogee hachchi wontto geennan qofaa waati qanttan xaafi shiishshidi asaa sissanaakkonne wodala ganjjee koyrotidi meezetanaw bessiya allaalle.
Meeziya 11
I.	Coraa gattiyo naqaashay erissoppe attin qonccisso gidenna giishin woyganaw koyettidee? Hegaa ne qofan qonccissa.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
3.6.3. XAAFO EESHSHAA
Coraa gattiyo naqaashaa xaafiyageeti keehi cora qonccisso koshshenna siyiyageeti woykko xaafiyageeti qofaa ekkana mala qanttan xaafetta hanabaa koyoosona. Xaafiyobaykka jorinaaliizime usppun oyshata (aybee, awan, ayssi, ooni, awdenne waani/waatidi) yaagiya oyshatussi zaaro gidishin coraa gattiyo naqaashay qassi likketettaa, qonccetettaa, qonccetettaanne haasayiyogaa geetettiya oyddu yo'ota xaafuwassi xaafuwassi baaso ootti go''eteettees. Issi ha naqaashaa xaafiidi guyye gaana bessenna allaallee minttettuwanne eesuwa. Coraa gattiyo naqaashaa odoy guutta daqiiqan aadhdhanaw koshshees. Xaafuwan aadhdhida peeshuwa go''ettiyakko coraw gattiyo naqaashan ha''i wode peeshuwa go''etettees. Leemisuwaw gaazeexan hanabay hagaattoo doomettees. ''Xaata moconay zino parilaamay giiraa bolli gujjiyo kuushsha qofaa xeelliyagan yaa'ettiyo wode beettana yaagiis.''
Coraa gattiyo naqaashan qassi hagaattoo shiiqees.
''Xaata moconay giiraa bolli gujjiyogan ........................'' 



ichchashu oyshan demmiyo ayfe yo'uwa




 




ichchashu oyshan demmiyo ayfe yo'uwa

ayfe yo'uwa dendduwanne hara naa''antto ooso miishshaa xeelliyagaa



Hara koshshiya eeshshay hayttaassappe attin ayfiya xeellanaassa gidenna giyogaa. Xaafiyobati coo gede sholqqiyobaa gidennan diishi gaasuwara diyabaa gidanaw koshshees. Issi issi qonccenne lefa gaazeexaa xaafiyo maaraykka cenggurssaa xoqqu ootti nabbabiyo wode hayttan siyanawkka iitiya, coo issi issi deexo qaalaanne paca qofa qasho gidana danddayoosona. Coraa gattiya naaqaashaw xaafettiya qaalati mulekka hayttan siyanaw iitiyanne deexo qaala gidanaw bessenna ayssi giikko awaajjiyogee (sissiyogee) cenggurssaa xoqqu oottidi nabbabiyo gishshaw keehi xuntta qofa qashuwa go’’ettiyogee ha xaafuwaw meezettidobaa. Wodee keehaa xuntta gidiyogaappe denddidaagan coraa gattiya naqaashaaway qaalatanne paca qofa qashota coo gede zaari toskkayanaw koshshenna; doorettida zirxxa qaalatun cora qofaa xephidi shiishshanaw koshshees. Hegaa gishshaw guutta qaalatanne paca qofa qashota go’’ettiyogee ha coraa gattiyo naqaashaa xaafuwassi siree baynna dooro.  Hegaa gishshaw xaafanchchay salettennan xaqqayidi qanttanaw koshshees. Coraa gattiya naqaashaa xaafiyageeti xaqqayiyageeta geetettoy hegaa gaasotaassa. Issi issi qaxiballo qofa qashota xaqqayidi nu galla galla siyiyo qofa qashota xaafees. Hegaassi kulkka gaasotay hayttaassi xaafiyo gishshataassa. Ha xeelliya (be’’iya) woykko siya asaappe haliichchikko naa’’anttoo mule zaarettidi ezgganaagee hanennabaa. Cooraa gattiya naqaashaa xaafiyo wogay ne ne laggetuura gall galla haasayiyogaa mala woykko nu issoy issuwara oychchi zaaro haasayan qofaa laamettiyogaa mala.  Televizhzhiiniyassa gidikko viiduwa kiliippiya essi essi xaafiyogee muleera geetettabaa (polettabaa) eranaassi daro lo’’o. Ha duuqetta misileekka yo’oy harchchennaadan oyqqanaw wolqqaama kaafe. 
Tumay ooni, ay, ayssi, awan, awdenne waanidi giya oyshatu zaaruwa immiyo wode beettees. Ha beetta yo’uwa televizhzhiiniyan woykko iraaduwan oduwassi xaafeettees. Ha xaafiyo oduwassi kulkkay daro naqaashaa issi kutti huukkuri oyqqidaagaa asay ezggidi yo’uwa akeekkees.

3.6.4. CORAAYYO GATTIYO NAQAASHAW KULKKA ODUWA XAAFUWA
Coraayyo gattiyo naqaashaw kulkka yo’uwa xaafanaw ha allaalleta akeekanaw koshshees. 
•	Qaammikko lo’’o.
•	Qaxiballo qofa qashuwa qanttoppa. Shaakkada naa’’u woykko heezzu qofa qashota gaasota wottada qonccissa.
•	Coraa gattiya naqaashshaassi kulkkay xaafettiyoy ezggiyagaassi hanabaassi koshshiya baggaa ufayssi odi sissanaassa.
•	Muletoo haasayettiyanne lefa qofa qashoy (qofaawa-sophe-peesho) yaageti quxaretti xaafettiya qofa qashuwa go’’ettees.
•	Aadhdhibeenna (ha’’I wode peeshota) go’’ettiyogee ezggiyageeti aybi haniyakko eranaw daro lo’’o.
•	Waabiya go’’ettiyo wode qofa qashuwassi doomettan gelees. 
•	Poliyo peeshotanne qoodan ayfiya geli qum’’enna sunqqotanne penqqota go’’etta.
•	Poliyo peeshuwappe attin polettiyo peeshuwa mule go’’ettoppa.
Poliyo peeshuwa, “Haree bitaniya qakkiis.”
Polettiyo peeshuwa, “Bitanee hariyan qakettiis.”
3.6.5. ISSI ISSI XAAFIYO WOGATA
Ha amarida xaafiyo wogati coraa gattiyo naqaashaa nabbabiyo wode asaassi dabari geenna malanne odettabay sohuwara gelanaadan xaafanchchay go’’ettiyogeeta. Ha coraa gattiya naqaashaa xaafuwan erana koshshiya wogay qoodaa (payduwa). Hagaa xeelliyagan wudissanaw bessiya naa’’u qofay de’ees. 
1.	Issi issi hanabatun, leemisuwassi biitta xekka baajeetiya daro bati shiiqanaw bessoosona. Ha cora darobaa deriyassi biddiyogaappe wodala ganjjeti koshshenna yo’uwa yiggi xeellidi aggiiganaw bessoosona.
2.	Issi issi paydota xeelliyagan hanabay xaafettiyo wode sissiyagaw xeessanaw wayssennanne siyiyagawkka hayttan lawhu gi geliyo hanotan xaafettana bessees.
Awdenne gaasotay diikko tumurukko paydota xaqqaya. Muletoo hagaattoo yaagidi malan ,hagaappe dariya, hiqqa keenaa xaafikko injje; asankka ekettees.
Siyiyagaanne ezggiyagaakka wayssenna mala maaddanaw dumma dumma qaalata go’’etta. Bolli bolli googaa guyye zaarettidi giyo haasaya xayssanawnne qonccissanaw xoppu ootti oliis, xeetaappe 40 kushiya bashshiis, naa’’u kusheppe dariya, xeetaappe 15 kusheppe dariyagaa qanxxi ekkiis, hegaanne hegaa malatiya paca qofa qashota (qofa qashota) go’’etta. 

Sha’aa qonccissanaw some malaatan danttada go’’etta. Leemisuwassi: 25-sha’u tamaare naata. Cora paydo gidiyo wode qassi sinttawnne guyye belada nabbaba. Leemisuwassi: 2,001,897.46 yaagi xaafetta payduwa naa’’u miillooneppe dariya gaada nabbabikko lo’’o. Shaahetta payduwa issi qaaladan danttada nabbaba. Leemisuwassi: heezzaappe-naa’’u kushe.
Coraa gattiya naqaashaappe ha yo’ota diggargga.
•	Muuca qaalata muleera.
•	Dirattuwa, coo gelddefa haasayaa, tekinoolloojee eho qaalata, saayinisiya qaalatanne meezetibeennanne hiilla qaalata.
•	Issi issi qonccissiya qaalati (paca qofa qashoti) haraa haasayaappe kaallidi gelanaw bessees. 
•	Qofaaway peeshuwappe, peeshoy kaalliyagaappe aaho dummatettay daana bessenna.
•	Adussa qonccissiya qaalata.
Ha’’ikka Akeekanaw Bessiyabay:-
•	Kuushsha yo’oy sinttappe koyrotidi gelees.
•	Dumma dumma yametinne biittati erettidaageeta gidana xaykko. Leemisuwassi: ‘UNESCO’, ‘UNICEF’, ‘UK’, ‘USA’ h.h.m.
•	Haraa haasayay maara gartte malaatan wodhdhanaw bessees. Leemisuwassi: Xaata moconay yaagiis, “Hachchi ichchaw layttappe guyyiyan Abbaa zeeroy wuran.” Iraaduwan oduwa xaafissi sissiyo wode misilee koshshennaagee erettidabaa shin haasayaappe, qaalaa go’’ettiyogaappenne cenggurssaappe asaa kahan misilee merettin asay hanabaa sissa kanchche gidennan diishin be’ees. Hegaassi asay ha xaafanchchay hanabaa he sohuwan beettidoogaadan ootti micciiridi xaafees.
3.6.6. CORAA GATTIYO NAQAASHAY AYBIN HARAAPPE DUMMATTII?
Coraa gattiyo naqaashay haratuppe dummattiyo qaalaninne gattiyagan go’’ettiyo gishshattaassa. Mereta cenggurssaninne he cenggurssan go’’etti oduwa sissidi televizhzhiiniyaninne viiduwan go’’ettiyogan hagee haratuppe dummattees. Ha go’’ettiyo qaalati issoy issuwara waati go’’ettiyo wode koshshiya hara qaalaykka coo tololatidi yiyorinkka maaraa oytti go’’ettiigeettees. Ha coraa gattiya naqaashaa oduwa wurssetta qofa qashoy hanabaassi keehi koshshiya kifile gidoshin kulkka haraappe koshshiya kifile. Wurssetta qofa qashoy pugiyappe kofaappe carkkoy kiyiyogaadan loddaara hososayidi yo’uwa wurssidi asaassi qanttan kiitaa aattiya kifile. Ha wurssetta qofa qashoy yo’uwa qachchiyo kifile. Yo’uwassi kuushshaykka hegan erettees. Wodala ganjjee wurssettan kuushsha qofa oyqqida qofa qashuwa qanttan go’’ettanaw bessees.
Televizhzhiiniyan gidikko yo’uwa qonccissiya misilee beettiyo gishshaw ha nabbabiyogee bessiidi odiyogee asaassi dari wayssennan erettees. Issi metobay wodala ganjjee awppe ha misiliyan amppidi oduwa giigissanee yaagiyagaa gidishin misilee beettenna allaalle gidikko I misiliya siyaya asaw kahan medhdhiya qaalatanne paca qofa qashota woykko qofa qashota cenggurssaa go’’ettiyogaa. Ha qaalati hanabaara mise gidanaappe attin oduwa misiledan wagaggissokkona. Misileti hanabaa odoosona, qaalati qassi he yo’uwa asaassi gelanaadan kaafoosona guuggiyan misilee merettanaadankka oottoosona.

Hara merati cengurssaa xoqqu ziqqi oottidi nabbabiyo wode misilee asaassi kahan merettees. Iraaduwaninne televizhzhiiniyan ha cengurssay asaassi yo’oy gelanaw keehi maaddees.

Diraaman giigissiyagee, bessiyagee, xaafiyageekka keehi metootidi qaalaa doorees. Coo gede zaari demo qaalaa gelissiigenna; ayba qaala kanchchee cenggurssay oogee yo’uwa  hajibala ootti siyiyagawnne be’iyagaw qonccissii giyogee wolqqaama pilggettaa koyiya ooso. Hagee ubbaykka wallalliyo koyro xaafiyagee mijjirssaa ootti asaa kahaa wuuqqiya hanotan xaafikkoppe attin koyro xaafuwan handdarash giichchikko dulliya deshay ba’uwa deshissiyogaa mala.

3.6.7. GAYTTIYA ALLAALLETA
•	Coraa gattiya naqaashaa miidee daro asaassi yo’uwa gattees geetetti ammanettees; tamaaridi luxibeenna kambbaninne ambban diyageetinne hara dumma dumma dere asati salo gufanttuwan woxxi qaaxxabaa eriyo ha miidiya baggaara. 
•	Hara ha coraa gattiya naqaashaappenne xaafetta naqaashaappe gidduwan diya dumatettay ha xaafetta naqaashaa uttidi nabbabanaw sohuwa koyees; hankkuwa qassi awankko demmosan siyanaw danddayettees. 
•	Coraa gattiya naqaashan ha’’I wode peeshoy go’’ettikko xaafiyo naqaashan qassi adhdha wode peeshuwa go’’eteettees.
•	Yaanne haanne qel’’iqel’’enna tuma yo’oy oduwa xaafiyo wode keehi qoppanaw bessiya baaso miishsha. Hani kanttabaa xaafiya wodala ganjjee aybanne wora yedhdhennan sitta haasayaa (qofa qashuwa) xaafanaw bessees. Wodala ganjjee pilggettidi mucurettida tumu yo’o markkan shatimmana danddayiyo allaalliya xaafanaw bessees. Xaafe yaa’ay (press conference), dere yaa’ay, olan dumma dumma salppiyaninne anjjissuwan wodala ganjjee hanabaw tumaa pilggees. “I xaafiidi gaanay diishin gayttay miiccees, ba’’anne goochcha h.h.m. leemiso haasayata go’’ettiyogaappe naagettanaw koshshees. Xamassaasa qaalaa go’’ettiyogee oduwassi diya kiluwa guuttees, mala calaakka moorees. Issi issi wolqqaamanne hanttaara asata nashshiyogaanne toochchiyogaappe tilla yo’uwa xaafuwa wayqqanaw koshshees. Gaasotaykka heegee miide oosuwan ixettiyanne dallo ooso.
•	Pilggiyageeti bantta demmido allaalliya lefanne qantta qofa qashotun poliya peeshotun (active Voice) qaxiballo qaalatun go’’ettiyogee coraa gattiyo naqaashaa miidiyassi wotto woga.
•	Layttaa giddon cora porogiraameti giigoosona. Ha giigissiyo miidiya oosuwan kase meezee keehippe koshshees. Kase meeziyan keedidi xaafiyogee qofaa laammanaassi halaale. Issi issi porogiraameti deriyasa, issoy issoy yettaa, diraamaa, oduwa hegaanne hegaa malatiyageetuppe amaridaageeti issi issi dumma allaallee xeelliyo asatussa gidishin asay darotoo naatu porogiraamiya, macaasaanne goshshaa xeelliyagan odettiya yo’ota sianaw ufayttees.
•	Xaafetti giigabaassi qottay giigana xaykko, ooso ayfee keehi kalissenna; siyanaw hayttaakka corggochchissenna. Xaafiyagee wolqqaama gittaa minttidi daafuri oottidi coo donchchol’’a oduwa shiishshanaw bessenna. Hegaassi gittidi oottana bessees. Oduwa oosoy maara mankkaa kaallidi oottikko daro wodiyanne wolqqaa xeegenna qanttan aakkidi gidenna ayfidi gidees giyogaadan mal’’onne tishsha oduwa giigissidi ba ooso ayfiya deriya allaxxissidi sissanaw danddayees.
•	Dumma dumma yo’ota xeelliyaga xaafetti uttabata woykko xaaduqota demmi ekkidi kuushsha qofaa shaakkennan go’’ettiyogee, leemisuwaw ha xaaduqoy issi heeraa (yaraa) toochchiyagaa gidanaw danddayees, tiraafikiya balaa, ogiya doonnan eqqidi zin’’idi aqi pe’’iya naata, kawotaa oosuwa qaattaanne maaraa mankkaa ogee baynna hanotan bori kanttobaa gidanaw danddayees, issi asa deriya garssappe bohissiya allaallekka gidanaw danddayees, ha xaaduqoy deriya garssan za’aa medhdhiyagaa gidikkonne issi deriyassi (yaraassi) de’iya wozanaa koshshaa duchchissiyabaa gidikko he odoy haatta pinttenna odo gidiyo gishshaw ha ufuraara diya yo’uwa suullaa kattaa garssape harqqiyogaadan pixiridi diggirgganaw bessees.
•	Wurssettan ha coraa gattiya naqaashaa nabbabi sissiya wodala ganjjee qulxxuxi maayiidi miichchaa poocamennan, axiraarennan, piikkatennan, yiillo giyo miishshappe naagettidi, som’’uwa tukkennan, yo’uwa midiidissiyogaappekka naagettidi asaa sinttan birshshetti pashkkidi ashilaalonne ashanqqa qaalatanne paca qofa qashota nabbabuwa tololayanaw bessees.
3.7. GEEDIYAGAA QOFAA XAAFUWA
Hagee waanidinne ayssi geedettaa qofaa xaafoy koshshiyakko ay keena oduwa oosuwan ha allaalle ayfissidaakkonne qonccissees. A qommoykka hagaappe kaallidi qoncciis. 
Ha geedaagaa qofaa xaafiyo wode ammanettanaw erissanaw woykko ufayssiyabaa gujjanaassa. Ha oosuwan kaallanaw bessiya baaso gidiya seerati de’oosona. Hegeekka qori shiishshi gujjobati woykko denttobati yo’uwa mal’’ettanawnne odoy asaassi wayssennan gelanaadan minttettuwanne xaafetta naqaashaa xekkaa naagissidi kiluwa xoqqissanaw geediyo ooso. Daro baggi geemmi uttida asaa qofay de’ikko geediyo wode kaashetti laalettees. Hagee qassi deriya garssan de’iya dimokiraase dichchaa gaxa kessanaassa.

3.7.1. DERIYA QOFAY OGIYA OYKKIYOGAA
Adhdhida xeetu layttaa doometta heeran salo gufanttuwan diya wolqqay (maatay) kawotaappe deriya qofaassi simmiis. Ha buussay (deriya qofaassi sohoy imettiyogee) loddaara kosiya ekkiya allaallee gidikkonne kushiyan gelidi sinttaw biidides. Hagee sa’a micettan deriya qofay keehippe koshiyogaa bessees. Deree ufayttidi bari qofaa qonccissiyogee kawotaa shemppuwara daanaadan oottees woykko issi yamee sinttaw kiyanaadan oottees. Dimokiraasee dicciis giyogee deriya qofaw sohoy imettiyogee attenna miishsha. Deriya qofay xubettana danddayoyoy hagaappe kaallidi diya heezzu yo’otuuna:
•	Dosettenna woykko phalqqiya qofa gidikko.
•	Kase malaw madaw erennanne ehettenna qofa gidikko.
•	Mitettenna qofaa wolqqan ammanttanaw baaxettikko.
3.7.2. GEEDETTAA GO’’AA
Geedettaa qofaw daro go’’ay de’ees. Hegan nashshanaw phalqqanaw minttettanaw, denttanaw, wottanaw, toochchanaw, sabbanaw, sittissanaw ( zuuqqanaw), amarida qofaa (polisiya) phenqqeshshanaw danddayettees. La’aninne eratettan kumida qofay deriya qofaa molees; geediyagankka ekettiya miishsha. Ha oosuwan geediyagee keehi luxida eranchcha gidanawnne A qofay deriyan ekettiyanne coraa ufayssiya asa gidanaw bessees. Geediyagee bari oosoy keehi koshshiyogaa kiyida gaazeexaappe akeekidi shaakki erees. Geedettaa oosuwan geediyagee ha allaalliyara issippe biya bari qofaa qonccissees. Dariya baggi geediyagee gaazeexaa polisiya qonccissees. Ha nabbabiya ubbay geediyagaa qofaa nabbabenna polisiya giigissiyageeti nabbaboosona. 

Geediyagee tumaa siree baynnan wottanaw koshshees. Tumi ay ogiyanikka hambbalaashettanaw koshshenna. Hagee nabbabiyageeta kaalettanaassappe attin cimmanaassa gidenna. Ha ubbaappe aadhdhi geediyagee qofaa qanttan maaraa mankkaa naagidi, sitta ogiyan ufayssiyanne tilla ogiyan nabbabiyageetussi qonccissiyogaa.

Geediyagaw cenggurssaa qonccissiyanne yo’uwa birshshiya ayfe yo’uwa qonccissiya, A oosuwa nabbabiyageeti eranaadan oottiyagaa gidanaw koshshees. Cenggurssay xoqqu ootti siyanaw shonggaara diyagaa gidanaw koshshees. Geediyagee biittaassi metuwa kaalettiya qofaa keehippe bores; aadhdhennaadaanikka teqqees. Yo’uwa xanna’idi tumaa ooraxxissidi naa’’u ginaara misiliya medhdhidi siyanaadan oottiyogee geedettaa qofaa xaafuwassi keehi koshshiya allaalle, hagee kuushsha yo’uwa aallaaliya xaafidi woga oottidi go’’ettiyobaa.

3.7.3. GEEDETTAA/QOFAA XAAFUWA
Ha oduwassi go’’iyabaa hayyoyidi mucuri giigissiyogaa xeellees. Ha xaafuwan gaazeexan dendda allaalliya pilggees, nabbabiyageetikka oonee gi qoppidi etassi hanabaa shonggayidi shiishshiyogaa. Geedettay asaa cenggurssay qoncciyogaa gidishin issitoo issitoo asay aani ufayttanaw koyees. Issi asi geedo qofaa xaafiyo wode, woykko ammanananw erissanawnne ufayssanaw go’etees shin ha seerata oosuwan peeshshanaw koshshees. 
•	Geedi xaafo yo’oy ha’’I wode hanabaa go’’aynne ufayssiyagaa gidanaw bessees. 
•	Palamaw baaso gidiyabati tumakka giyobaa , sittanne ammanttiya allaalle, yo’o ubban googaa phalqqennan kaafiyanne kuushsha gaanaw hiillan go’’ettiyogaa gidanaw bessees. 
•	Shiishshanaw bayra qofay de’anaw bessees hegaa xaafiyagee sohuwara ayfe yo’uwa laammanaw bessees; hegee aggi aadhdhanaw danddayettenna yo’o.
Geedettaa xaafuwa muletoo erissiya qofaa qashoy hara kaafiya qofa qashotuura issippe waati oduwa minttanaw de’ana bessees. Tumay qanttan mucureti giiganaw bessees. Geedettay dariya baggi pissiyaw shiiqida hanabaa kaalli xeelliyogaa. Giddoshin hani kanttabaw ha geediyagaassi kase eray (hekkay) daana bessees. He geedettay nabbabiyagaw wayssiya yo’uakka loytti nabbabettanaadan zuuqqesppe attin A oosuwa oduwa gidennan diishin seliseddabaa giigissiyogaara gayttees. Geediyageeti muletoo heezzu shemppuwan shaakkidi bantta oosuwa oottoosona. Koyro shemppoy ha geediyo tumaa (oduwa) shiishshiyogaa, naa’’antto shemppoy ha koyro shiishshido tumaa yiggi xeelli geedidi xaafiyogaa, heezzantto shemppoy qassi hayyoti mucurettida geeshsha yo’uwa wurssetta xaafuwa xaafiyogaa. 
3.7.4. GEEDETTAA QOMMUWA
Afrikkaa biittan gaazeexaakko som’’uwa zaariyo wode geedettaa hosppun dumma dumma eeshshan shaakkeettees. Ha issoy issuwa malatidi dummatettaanne gaytotaa eranaw wayssiya geedetta qommota asa na’I guuggiyan oyqqanaw bessiyabay ha geedetta qommon issoy issuwara sittan woykko geella ogiyankka gayttiyogaa. 
•	Palamaanne Ammanttuwa: Afrikkaa biittan dariya baggi gaazeexaa geediyageeti kawotaa ammanttidi tangguwa ekissiyo hidootaa wottidi palamaa sitti giyo yo’o. He geediyageeti kawotaanne nabbabiyageeta ammanttanaw baaxettiyogaa. Hegaassi ha geediyageeti ushachchaanne haddirssaa yiggi xeellidi tishsha yo’uwa xeelliyagan palamettana koshshees.
•	Erissiya Woykko Poo’issiya: Ha geediyageeti tumaa zaarettidi kase assi diya naqaashan amppidi asaassi qonccissoosona. He geediyagee wottido naqaashay gelenna tuhettida allaalliya nabbabiyageetussi birshshi yeddees. Birshshiyogaa kanchche gidennan diishshin geediyagee kuushshaa demmees. 
•	Birshshiya woykko Shaahuwa: Ha geediyagee muletoo eranaw tiraara sitti giida yo’uwa woykko allaalliya bari qofan birshshi qonccissees. 
•	Maayettenna Yo’o: Hagaa mala geediyagee issi baggi simmennan maacettibeenna yo’uwa bolli tobbees. Palaman deree maayettenna yo’oy attennan denddanaw bessees.
•	Anjjiya woykko Nashshiya: Ha geediyageeti asata woykko yametaw leemiso gidanaw danddayiyay tangguwa sabboosona woykko galatoosona. 
•	Allaxissiya: Asaa ufayssanaw xaafetta hanabaa woykko issippe xaphuwappe xeeraa gakkanaashin qonccissi xaafo allaalle gidana danddayees. Hegaa lefa hanotan xaafanaw bessees gaasotaykka nabbabiyagaa ufayssanaw xaafiyo gishshataassa. 
•	Oosuwaw denttettiya: Hagee dumma hoolliyaw xaafettiyagaa ba dosiyo citaa denttettanaw, wottanchchaa xoonnissanawnne ooso ayfiya demmanaw baaxettiyogaa kaafanaw go’’ettiyo xaafuwa. Hagee he allaallee xeelliyo uraa go’’anaassikka wolqqaama kaafe. 
•	Dumma Wodiya Geediya: Hagee dumma gallassaa woykko wodiya geedidi xaafiyogaa. Leemisuwassi: Deretettaa Gallassaa, Ooratta Layttaa, Yesuusa Yeletaa, Ootti aqidaageetunne macaasaa xeelliyagan bonchchettiya gallassa h.h.m. muletoo geediyagee bari qofan xaafi giigissees.
Meeziya 16
I. Hosppun geedetta qommota neessi gelida birshshettaa immada xaafa.
