H.	--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- .

I.	--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- .

J.	--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- . 
4.5. QANTTA QOFAA
Ha asi oone bari qofaa qonccissanaw imetta zawi baynna la’atettay ha deriya jorinaaliizimee dumma dumma xaafeti bantta koyido allaalliya xaafin deriya jorinaaliizimee biittaappe porxxu giidi kiyanaw baaso gaaso gidiis. Ha miidiyan asay hekkaa demmin miidiya timirttee naa’’u tohuwan eqqin asay miidiya xeelliyagan beegotaa demmiyo gishshaw miidiya halchchuwa eqettenna hanotan miidiya polisee eqqin deriya jorinaaliizimeekka hara ay xaafettiyabatuura sohuwa oyqqidi xekkaanne boolimaa naagidi giigiyogaa doommiis; biittaa gaxxan yiida laametussinne tekinoolloojje dechchaassi miidee ootto wulatay qoodan haga keena gaanaw danddayettenna. AI asaassi dichchan oottiyo kaafee hagaa keena gaanaw danddayettenna; gita maaduwa immees.

Jiorinaaleti asaa penggiyappe gaxaara eqqanaw bessoosona; deriya giddo gelidi bantta tamaari luxido hiillan amppidi tumaanne markki macari de’iyo naqaashaa demmidi hanabaa oduwassi xaafidi asaa sissanaw bessiyo gishshaw. Ha miidiya maaraa mankkaa xeelliyagan daro asatussi daro qofay de’ees; ay keenaa qofaa dummatettay diikkokka ha cora qofay de’iyogeeta galla galla jorinaaletu oosoy sinttaw kiyi porxxu giidi baanaw teqqin ubbay issi baggi deriya go’’aakko simmidi maabaray maayi  aggiis. Yaati issootu issootu dummatettaa qofay hagan muuhettiigiis. Xaafanchchati miidiya maaraa mankkan deriya wozanaa qofaa ezggoosona shin gutaraa (polotikaa) hemettissiyageetikka deriya qofaa hemettissiyo gishshaw hegan issippe gayttoosona.  Jorinaaliizimee deriya qofaa ezggi hemettissiyogee oonee maayanaw bessiyanne attenna allaalle.

Jorinnaleti deriya qofaappe kaareeraa biidisona giyogee wolqqaama ciima shaafa zarphphee baynnan pinniyogaa mala. Ha oosuwan gelishin jorinaaletussi daro asay buzo koshshaa qonccissiya naqaashaa (qofaa) immanaw danddayees shin jorinaaleti issi asa qofi dere qofa gidenna ixxanaw danddayiyo gishshataw aagaa A qofaattoo ekkidi bari tamaaridi luxidogaa maaran ba oossuwa polanaw bessesppe attin issi asa woykko naa’’u asa ebeloynne ebeloy yaagiis giidi deriya go’’enna (xeellenna) qofaa qelekki aadhdhana besses qassi ooni erii ha qofaa immidaagaa (immidaagetu) qofay deressi dichchawnne laamiya allalle kessiya ekkettiya qofaa gidikko hegaa aadhdhanaw bessenna. Jorinaalizime lo”o gaanaw assi koyro halchchoy lo”o gidanaw bessees. Jorinaalee ba naqaashaa shiishshiyo wode ay asinne kelttiya gelennan ba tamaari loohido hiillan amppidi oottanaw bessesppe attin A ay asinne hagaa yaata giidi zoridi kaalettanaw bessenna. Ha jorinaaliizime siree bayna asay issoy issuwara qofa lamettiyo oge.

Ha wodiyan naqaashaw pulttwa maaraa oyttanaw danddayyettnna xekkaa gakkiis.
















ICHCHASHANTTO SHEMPPUWA
TUMAANNE HALCHCHUWA
Tumi qonccissanaw dari metenna ayssi giikko naqaashay salo gupanttuwappe yaara haara xoohiyo gishshaw nuuni nu eran go’’ettidi tumaa wordduwappe dumayanaagee nuussi kana kaassa (Burns 2002, S. 53).
5.1. JORINAALIIZIMIYA TUMAA
Miidiya maaraa mankkaa oduwanne assi de’iya birshshettaa, ha miidiyasi asaa xeelliyagan de’iya halchchuwa, ha miidee qassi ay keena asaa garssan dimokiraassiya dichchaw oottido go’’aara issppe xaaxi waaxi xeelloos. Hegaa gishshaw miidiya maaraa mankkay jorinaaliizimiyassi kase diya meeziyara issippe gatti xeelliyo wode issi issi palanttiya yo’oti de’oosona. Miidiyaw maaray mankkay jorinaaliizimiya go’’aaranne oduwa hoolliyara issippe gayttees. Hegaara gayttidaagan jorinaaliizimiyassi qoncce oosoy oduwa shiishshiyo meeziyanne giigissuwa gidishin ha shemppuwan ane ha oosuwa hoolliya waati shocanaakkonne be’oos. Ha halchchuwa hoolliya shocanaw wolqqan geliyabatinne hara baggaara issi issi qassi oosuwa poliyo hoolliya shocanaw kaafiyabatikka de’oosona. Pissiya shiishshiyo halchchoy keehi koshshiya ha miidiya halchchoy keehi koshshiya ha miidiya maaraa mankkay oosuwan pe’iyonne ha tumaa hoolliya shociyo ooso. Tumaanne halchchuwa tobbiyo wode jorinaaliizimiyassinne oduwaw de’iya halchchoynne birshshettay denddiyogee attennabaa. Haray qassi jorinaaliizimeenne odoy oosuwan pe’iyo wode palanttiya gaasotay halchchoy xaykko odo shiishshiyogee waanidi puranaw dandday? Hegan odoy ziggirssaappe asi coo qoppi haasayiyogaappe dummattees. Tumatettayiyo de’iya xeelay bari huuphen keehi koshshiya maaray mankkay oosuwan pe’iyonne wurssettan halchchuwa poluwanne ha kaseesappe de’iya tumaa pilggi kessiyogaa. 

Miidiya maaraa mankkanne issi issi A xeelliyagan tumaanne halchchuwa issippe gatti xeelliyo wode denddiya muttaamuro qofay de’ees. Miidiya maaray mankkay timirttiyan demmiya era gidiyo gishshaw hagaa xeelliyagan daro palanttiyabi deenna shin hagee hachchi hachchi jorinaalee oosuwan pe’ii giyogee zaarettidi qoppanaw bessiya allaalle. Issi jorinaaliya xeelliyagan qoncce palanttiya allaallee jorinaaliizimee giigi simmin zaari kaalli xeelli geediyagee, ha oosoy ay keena caddiyabaakkonne xeelliyagee David Randall (1996)1  giidoogaadan ha miidiya geedettay salo gufanttuwan diya tumaa xaasidi xaafetta qofaa pilggiyogaa gidishin hagee keehi palanttiya allaalle tuma gidenna yo’o gidikko deree ekkenna. Deree ekkenna jorinaaliizimee qassi allaalle kessenna. Ha jorinaaliizimee sinttanaw minni xigididi bees giidi ammanettanawkka danddayettenna. Haray qassi xaafi kessiyo aybaappekka jorinaaliizimiyan birshshetti baynnan haasayiyobikka xaafiyobikka mule qofettenna. (Dring 2000, s. 311ppe) ekettidoogaadan haraykka gujjuwan (ibid., s. 312) ha coo hannenna haasayayanne xaafoy jorinaaliizime oosuwan oottenna ayssi giikko tumanne zirxxa yo’o gidana xaykko miidiya maaraa mankkay issi biittay aani aqiyo ano seeraa mala pala miishsha. Ha maaraa mankka xeelliyo wode odoy deriyassi aadhdhin woykko xaafetta gaazeexaa asi nabbabidi issi hanenna yo’oy xaafanchchaakka he ooso buussaa gadaawakka, allaallee xeelliyo ubbaa issippe geedidaageekka attennan oyshissees. Ha bala gaasuwan qasho qaaphoy gakkanaw danddayees. Hagee maahiya goynaa oyqqiyogaa mala guye zaarettidi mes. ‘Randall’ qonccissidoogaadan hagee darotoo haniyogee jorinaaliizimiyassi de’iya dumma dumma maaraa mankkaanne I aqiyo seeraa era (hekkaa) pacaappe denddidaagaana. Dumma dumma qaalaa (paca qofa qashuwa) go’’ettiyogaa gidikko hagee daro wode meeziyappenne timirttiyappe demmiyo allaalle. Gidikkonne ha meeziya demmiyogaappe jorinaaliizimee timirttiyan demmiyo eraynne pilggettay keehi zooxees. Ha jorinaaliizimiya inddusttiriyanne assi de’iya maaraa mankkaa xeelliyagan hiraaga eranchchay Andrew Besey (1998) ha jorinaalizime ooso miishsha demmanaw woykko zal’’iya oottiyo ooso gidennaaga mala palamettidi xaafiis. Ha yo’uwappe ‘Randall’ qassi poxettan pilggiis. Hegaappe simmidi qassikka ‘Randall’ ay odoynne ammanettiyonne tumu yo’uwa koyiyagaa gidanaw bessees giidi bana guye phalqqiya qofaa wottiis. Tumay dees shin A waatidi oosuwa peeshshanee yaagiyagee jorinaaliizime oosuwan wolqqaama oysha gidishin halchchoy qassi tumaa demmanaw malaatiya ginaa bessees yaagiyagaa. Hagee jorinaaleti awdenne bantta oosuwa oottiidi tumaynne ammanttiya yo’oy awgee yaagiya oyshaa bantta huuphiyan denttanaw bessoosona. Jorinaaliizime oosuwan awdenne halanaw danddayenna allaallee tuma giyo miishsha; oone ay wodekka tumaa yedhdhi hemettanaw danddayenna. Hagee kuushsha qofa gididi ‘The fourth Eastate and The Future of Truth (Gronbach 2007) yaagiya maxaafan qoncci xaafetti uttiis.

Zino qammi taani haahuwan televizhzhiiniyappe koyiyo ooso miishshan go’’ettada ‘CBS,’ ‘AbC’nne ‘NBC’ geetettiya porogiraametun oduwa koyayda pe’aas. Hegaassi gaasotay odoy keehi koshshiya miishsha gidiyogaa taani ammaniyo gishshataassi. Ay miide oosotuppekka taassi odoy keehi koshshiya miishsha. Beni wode Inggilandde biittan xaafi kessiyo allaallee dariya sohuwa geliya allaalle gididi go’ettiis. Hagee UI biittankka oosuwan pe’ida allaalle. Hegaa gishshaw taani oduwa koshshan kutuutays. Odoy issitoo issitoo neetiworkkiyappe beettees shin muletoo neetiworkke kanchchiyappe beettees gaanaw danddayettenna. Neetiworkkee ba zal’’iyaw corabaa yaappe haappe shifaariyogee nuussi galafiya gakkiya naqaashaa immanaw danddayeesppe attin muletoo odossi neetiworkkee xuussa gaanaagee daro meto. Neetiworkkee muletoo asay I aattin naqaashaa koshshan busubullidi kaallanaadan asaa wutissees; hagan ubban bari zal’’iya kiitaa aattees. Hegaa maaran neetiworkkee jorinaalee oduwa wochchidi demmiyo qato gididi hanno gakkanaw wurenna haggaazaa immiidi takkidoogee erettidabaa. Jorinaaliizimiya qaattay silidi hayqqikko (kunddikko) kawotaa oosuwa deree eridi ammanettanay aybiinee? Kawotay bari oottiyo oosuwa (gutaraa qaattaa) deriyassi erissiyoy jorinaaliizimiya baggaara gidiyogee sirissenna yo’o (Garyzidaho 2007).

Gordon et al. (1996), tumi jorinaaliizimiyassi ayfe yo’o. ‘Hariam Johnsenkka A qofan maayetti palamettiidi tumay olaassi baaso gaaso yaagiis. Tumi baynna odoy markki baynna yo’oy xontta giyogaa mala. Tumaa koyoyogee miidiya maara mankkan koyro xekka sohuwa immidi oottiyo ooso. Tumay koyro jorinaaliizimiya oosuwassi gaasotaa immidi kaalliyo oge (ibid, ss. 113-114). Issi yo’oy muleera aybinne seliseddennan tuma gaanaagee keehi meto gidikkonne jorinaaliizimiyan worddo yo’uwa tumaa gaccidi demmennan coo sholomidi kessiyogee dano ooso. Miidiya loohissiya timirtte keettati muleera wudissidi tamaarissiyogee issi xaafanchchay hagee deriyassi go’’iya qofeeyye gidennee giidi bantta huuphiyan daro oyshaa simerettissidi jorinaaleti shiishshiyo hanabay asaassi immiyo maaduwa woykko go’’aa xaafanaadan loohissees. ‘Rotty’ (1998) la’a haasayaappe naqaashaa qashamanaassi keehi tilla oge yaagiis. Heede ‘Rotty’ he naqaashaa qashamanaassi issi ajandday imettobaassi he kuushsha qofan eqqidi haasaayiyo la’a haasayay woykko tobee naqaashaa demmanaassi injje ogeppe attin ooninne ay kuushsha qofinne halchchettennan haasaayiyo haasayay naqaasha pultto gaanaw danddayettenna (Rotty 1998, s. 51).

La’a tobbiyogaa giishin la’a qofaa giyogaa gidenna. Issi asi imettida ajanddaa xeelliyagan haasayiyo wode ezggidi eta qofaa xaafiyogaa. Leemisuwaw univeristtiya tamaare naati bantta timirttiya xeelliyagan qofaa denttidi haasayishin eti gaanaw koyidobaa jorinaalee coo ekkidi xaafenna woppatettaa xeelliyagan I xaafanaw koyikko he univeristtiyan de’iya woppatettaa allaalliya, tamaaretu timirttiya hanotaa xeelliyagan xaafanaw koyikko bari koyido kuushsha qofaa baassi pultto gidanaw danddayiya izaawussi qoncce oottidi he allaalliya xeelliyagan naa’’u uraa (citaa) la’an oychchidi haasayanaadan qaadaa immanaw bessees. Issooti issooti naqaashaa demmanaw keehi xuntta ogiya go’’ettanaw danddayoosona; hegee keehi bala. Hara baggaara qassi issi sitta naqaashay oduwassi koshshiyo wodeekka de’ees. Leemisuwaw wodala ganjjee ammanuwa allaalliya xeelliyagan pakisiya naqaashaa issi pultto gidiya asaappe woykko yamiyappe ekkanaw danddayees; hegee issi sitta oge xalaalaappe naqaashaa demmiyogaa geetettees (World Public Opinion 2003).

‘Rotty gujjidi qonccissidoogaadan cora asay woykko issi uraykka ha naqaashaw waabe woykko pultto (gidanaw) danddayees. Leemisuwaw biittaa wogaa aqotaa dichchaa gutaraa woykko garaa gezziya qaattaa xeelliyagan asi haasayishin woykko citay dabaaban biddishin wodala ganjjee naqaashaa ekkanaw danddayees. Gidikkokka wontta ‘Rotty’ qonccissidoogaadan jorinaalee ha asati (citay) woykko issi asi haasayaa la’atettan tololayidi biddishin tumu yo’o xalaalaa qoridi xaafees; iita woykko tumaa eqettiya yo’oy diikko pixiridi diggirggidi suulli baynna mucurettida yo’uwa shiishshiyogee jorinaaliyassi kulkka ooso. Issi oduwan/jorinaaliya oosuwan guuttabi hanenna woykko woykko siyanawnne nabbabanaw made made giya hanabay (qofay) diikko jorinaalee hegaa diggirggiyogee siree baynna yo’o. Ubba guuttaa zuuqqi giigissido tumaykka jorinaaliizime oosuwan haatta pinttenna. Ha jorinaalee ubbatoo woxxi qaaxabaa xeellidi yeeso maattan buuxa koyidi oduwa mal’’ettiyogee asaa wozanaa koshshaa alanaassa. Ha tumaa koshshaa tattaafiyogee aybanne ufuri baynna oosuwa oottanaassa. Tumay kase diyabaa shin A qassi asi molidi qoncce oottana danddayees. Yaatiyo gishshaw ha jorinaalee Haban xomppee to’oogaadan tippi gi xayida tumaa karchchiidi karchchiidi deriyassi qoncciya kessi bessees. Ha tumaa demmana gakkanaashin zaaretti zaarettidi oyshan salettennan toliyogee jorinaaliyassi baaso; ha geemmida tumay kiyanawkka bana danddayida tilla oge. Tumay hagaattoo warettay tiraara sitti gin beettiyabaappe attin haree caanidi awppekko ehiyobaa gidenna. Ha tuma yo’uwa demmidi asaa sissiyogee dottoree uluwan diya harggiya shukki diggin hargganchchay paxidaagaa be’’idi ufayttiyogaadan jorinaaliya ufayssees; A kanchche gidennan dere asaakka siyanaw yeemoyees. Jorinaalee hagaadan deriyassi haggaazaa immiyanne asay bari sooni kiitti go’’ettiyo oosanchcha mala gididi oottiidi hara baggaara qassi siree baynna qoncce xaaduquwakka sinttappe pilggettaa oosuwa go’’ana mala issi diran kuuridi wotteee. Hagee ubbay muleera xaaxi waaxin go’’ettido qoncissoy jorinaaliizimiya oosuwan halchchidi waati tumaa demmiyakkonne ha demetta tumay qassi waanidi asaa wozanaa mishuwa irxxissiyakkonne eranaassa gidishin worddo qonccissoy qassi ay keena borettiyanne wogan ekettenna dano ooso gidiyogaa erissanaassa. Hegee ayssee giikko tumaa koshshay deree baassi wazanaa koshshaw zaaro gi ammanettidi naagiyo allaallee tuma gidiyogaakka zaarettidi akeekanaassa. Hagaadan tumaa koyi demmidi oduwa asaayiyo giigissiyogaa aggidi coo sholomidi oottiyo oosoy jorinaaliizimiya era pacaa bessees. Ha qonccissoy oduwa waati giigissidi asaa sissanaakkonne he odoy qassi deriyan waani ekettiyakkonne amarida qofaa immanaassa. Ha tumaa oyqqida naqaashaa demmidi asaassi siyanaw giigissiyo wode jorinaalee muletoo ha oduwa ezggiya deriya bari guuggiyan qoppees. A kanchche gidennan diishin A oosuwa geediyagaassikka ezggiya jamay oottishin huuphiyan simerettees. Ha tumu yo’uwa koshshay muletoo jorinaalee galla galla oottiyo oosuwa barchchiya be’iyo allaallee gidiyogee issi tamarida jorinaaliyappe naagettees. Ha bari huuphen bana danddayida deriya bagga gididi deriyassi wozanaa koshshaa oduwan qonccissiyo hiilla. Jorinaaliizime oosuwan tumaa koyidi demmiyogee harggiyassi suuttaa pilggid xaliya demmiyogaa mala; dano oosuwa oottidaagaa seeranaw ano seeraa go’’ettiyogaa mala. Yaatiyo gishshaw tumaa odiyogee he biittaa ayssiya gutaraa dichchaassi huuphe halchcho. Tumay jorinaaliizimiyan hagee dooro geenna halchcho. Jorinaaletussi tumaa demmiyogaa (ibid, s. 14); hagee etassi gutarawnne deriyassi eti aggennan oottanaw bessiya allaalle. Hagee gutara allaalle ayssi giikko gutaran deree yayinidoogeeti bana dooridi maataa xam’’aa oyttida deriyassi tumu yo’uwa odana bessees; he gutaran tumaa odiyogee qassi dimokiraasee asaa giddon kumidi walxxi gi uttoogaa qonccissees. Issi issi xaafanchchati Allan (2004, s. 191) ha jorinaaleti tumu yo’uwa asaa ammanttiyonaayye giidi oyshaa shiishshiis. Haray qassi issi yo’oy beettiya tumaynne kase de’iya tumay issippe gayttiyye gayttennee giyagaa haray qassi ha jorinaaleti woxxi qaaxxabay ubbay tumaa koyiyogaa yaagiya oyshaa gidishin hagaw zaaroy A ayssi giikko tumi baynna yo’oy akeekenna gereesaa mala; isstoo barqqiichchikko A simmidi zuuqqi zaaranaagee keehi daro meto. Ubbakka tumi seliseddichchin halittay noggin haniira aadhdharikkinaa giyogaa mala guyye simmi maaddenna. Haray attoshin jorinaalee ha A oyshaw ooninne coo zaaruwa immoogaa coo onakkoppe ekkaas giidi xaafuwa daxana; kase meretan diya tumaara issippe gattidi xeellidi, asaa wogaa (macaa, attumaa, cimaa, naatuwa) laa sugiishsha gi oyshan kumidi giigissana xaykko yo’iya A guye zaarada mawsu. Issi hanabay waani polettidaakkonne maaraa oyttidi asaw geliya qaalan go’’ettidi qonccissiyo wode asay tumaa siree baynnan erees; hegeekka ayssi hanidee? Waani hanidee ooni ay oottidee yaagi oyshan toliyo wode maaraa oyqqees. Jorinaalee bagga tumaa shiishshiyye hanabaw aybaynne attennan diya tumaa qociri xaafii giyo wode bagga tumi xapho worddo yaagiya zaaroy imettiyo gishshaw tumaa demmanaashin ha tumay kare kiyenna mala teqqiya zarphphee de’ees; hegeekka meretaa tumaa leemisuwassi iray bukkiis giikko torqqoynne deellee meretan diya tumaa hegaattoo ha meretay bari huuphen hanabaw tumaa demmanaw malaatiyo hanotay de’ees. Hegaassi jorinaaleti yaappe haappe shiishshido naqaashaa tumay awgee yaagi demmanaw wayssenna mala kase meretan diya tumay maaddees giyogaa. 
Meeziya 1
I.	Neetiworkkiyappe koyaya demmada issi biittaa gutaraa, aqotaa woykko issipetettaa qonccissiya oduwa deriya sissanawa xaafa.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------.

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------.
Meeziya 2
I.	Issi sitta oge xalaalaappe naqaashaa demmido oduwa xaafada giigissada ne kifiya miiretu sintta nabbaba.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------.

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------.


  5.2. JORINAALIIZIMIYAN HALCHCHUWA
Jorinaale oosuwa halchchoy, tumaynne deriya koshshay bayra allaalle. Ha allaalleti gaazeexaa giigissiyo wodekka hara oosuwadan keehi koshshiya allaalle Williams (2002, s. 3). Ay polissiya hoolliya shocanaw giigissiyo gaazeexaassinne ha heezzu allaalleti attenna miishsha. Tuma yo’uwa xaafidi maattamiyogee jorinaaliyassi imetta aawatetta gidikkonne jorinaaliizimee qassi ha tumaa koshshaayyo gattiya zarphphe mala. Gidoshin tumay cora baggaara naqaashay ximaaziya naqaashaappe wottin denttin beettiyogee erettidabaa. Leemisuwassi UI biittan miishshaa maattamoy demettidoy 1833 layttaana. Ha qofay wottennan denttennan coo beettiya tuma gidenna. Ayssi giikko tiriya demmarggaassi giidi mittiyogaa mala gidenna. Haray attoshin ogiyara aadhdhiidi issoy awgaakko haasayido qofaa gidikkokka jorinaaliyassi allaalle kessenna; yo’uwa malaataa qunxxissiya naqaashaa koyi demmi giigissanaappe attin odo giigissoy ogiyara biyagee haasayo haasayaa ekkinee bogeretti sholomi xaafinnee kessiigikko yo’oy zuubbaranaw de’ees; hegaa gidikkokka ogiya haasayettiis giidi yo’o karanaw bessenna; hegaw xalee ay keena tumee giidi gamma yo’uwa woykko siree baynna allaalliya wochchiyogaa.   

Ha miishshaa maattamuwa xeelliyagan miishshay koyro awan biittan maattamettidee giya oyshaa shiishshikko naqaasha demmanaage kana kaassa (ibid, s. 7). Asa oychchennan baappe mal’’etti xaafiyogee qassi tumaa seliseddissana danddayees hegaassi gaasoy jorinaaliizime oosoy oyshaara giigiyo gishshataassi naqaashaa pilggidi kase diya xaaduquwappe woykko allaalle xeelliyo asaa (yamiya) oychchidi demmiyo naqaashaa loytti pilggidi qanttan yo’uwa mucuridi giigissi xaafeettees Aucoin (2002, s. 215). Jorinaaliizimiya oosuwan tumaa pilggidi demmiyogee halchchuwa hoollee polettiis giyogaa. Saynisiyan pilggeti giigidabaa gidikko he tumay pilggeti qonccidabaa gidiyo gishshaw hegaa xeelliyagan oduwa giigissiyogee jorinaaliya darin mettenna aybissi giikko ha mucuretti giigida tumaa oli aggidi hara tumaa medhdhanaagee hannenna yo’o. Tumay awdenne jorinaalee bayra sohuwa immin beettiya allaalle gidishi ha tumaw qassi A baassan kessiyay halchchidi tanggiyogaa. Wurssettan ha jorinaaliya oosoy siyiyanne nabbabiya deriyassi oysha medhdhennan hashshukkonne giya kiitaa aattikko hegan tumay shatimmiis giyogaa. Halchchuwa hoolliya shociyogeekka he tumay shatimmiyo wode kanchche. Ha dumma dumma ginaara xoohiya naqaashaappe wodala ganjjee oduwa giigissiyo wode asaappe ekkido qofaa bari qofan birshshees. Hagee yo’oy ayye waayi likkanaakkonne giidi palamettees; yaatidi yo’oy gelana xaykko oychchid wurssettan gaccidi tumaa demmees; worddo yo’o gidikko qassi asa sintti aattanaw borssiyabaadan oli aggees. Tumay halchchuwa maaran hoolliya shocanaassi woxeretti demmiyobaa gidikkonne kase de’ees shin hegaa oonee deriyassi qonccissanay yaagiya oyshaassi jorinaaliizimee tilla zaaro. Tumi wurssettan asi kasha geennan pashkkidi ekkidi palami baynnan shatimiigees. McNair (2003, s.33) qonccissidoogaadan halchchoy jorinaaliizimiyassi maaraa mankka yo’otuppe issuwa. Halchchoy jorinaaliizimiyassi baaso woga gidaappe attin jorinaalee gutaraabaa, aqotaabaanne issipetettaabaa ha ubbaa xaaxi waaxin oduwa giigissiyo wode aynnekka tumi zuubbaranaw (keehi koyin beettennan) ixxanawkka danddayenna. Odoy ootti simmin palamissiyanne deriyanne kawotaa gutaraa (dere asaanne kawotaa) shaalliyabaa gidikko heede tumay muumman tuccettiis gaanaw danddayettees. Hegaa gishshaw tumay markkan macaran palanttiya yo’uwa guye zaaridi ammanttiyo ooso miishsha. Hegaassi qassi halchchidi marxxi denddidi oottiyogee kul’’idosaa sittissanaw keehi maaddees. Issi issi siyanaw wayssiyanne odin gelenna yo’uwa ogiya oytti kalalayidi asaassi qonccissanaw tumay huuphe gadaawa. Halchcho giyogee naqaashaa oduwassi hanabaa xaafanayiyo gixxi denddidi biyogaa. Ha biidi qassi waabiya (naqaashaw pultto gidiya asa) oychchidi xekkaa naagida naqaashaa qoncciyan xaafeettees. Hagee ubbay xaaxi waaxxin oduwa ammanttanaassa, gaasotaa qonccissanaassinne ha odetta oduwappe deriyassi sissa kanchche gidennan diishin go’’iyabaakka tamaarissi kanttanaassa. Xekkaa naagida oosuwa oottanaw ay jorinaaleekka koyro halchchidi qaaxxiyogee assi baaso ooso. Jorinaaleti oduwa giigissi simmidi hagee bala hagee qassi likke giidi maaci simmanaappe guyyiyan etappe geediyagaa ekkidi naa’’anttoo zaarettidi balay beettikko giigissees. Jorinaalee oosuwan bari halchchido kuushsha qofaappe kareera he yo’uwa timennan diidi haraa gelissiyogee ekkidi naa’’antto zaarettidi balay beettikko giigissees. Jorinaale oosuwa bari halchchido kuushsha qofaappe kareera he yo’uwa timennan diidi haraa gelissiyoy daro ixettiya hano. Stephens (2007, S. 256). Halchchoy jorinaaliyassi I ba oottana koyidobaakka kaalettees (ibid). Halchchoynne tumay issippe waattan boosona; halchchoy tumaa demmanaw kaalliyo oge. Yaatiyo gishshaw ha tumaa demmiyo hoollee shocettiyo koyro halchchoy de’iina. Odoy bari huuphen asaassi naqaashaa hayttan oli aadhdhiyobaa gidishin odettanaw bessishin attabaw diikkokka asay he demo naqaashan amppidi halchchuwappe demmana danddayees. Hegaa gishshaw halchchuwappe demmanaw danddayees. Hegaa gishshaw halchchoy oduwa shiishshiyo hiillatuppe issuwa (ibid).   Ha halchchidi oottiyogee jorinaale oosuwa giigisso kanchchiya gidenna; simmidi ha xaafetta gaazeexaa nabbabiyageetussikka yo’oy qonccana mala maaddees; hinkkoode hagaa waati nabbabi eranee giidi nabbabiyageetikka banttassi gelennabay xaafettikko jorinaaliya oosuwa toochchanaw danddayoosona. Issi jorinaale oosoy cora baggaara xeelliyakko likke, yaaganawnne hagaa issi ayfiyan xeelliyanne heede hani kanttabaa aybanne boroshshennan qonccissiyagaa gidanaw bessees (ibid, s. 264).  Ha odettiya odoy dariya baggi deriya xeelliya allaalle gidiyo gishshsw deree darotoo saamettidi ezggees; hegeekka leemisuwaw he biittay kaaletettiyo gutaraa, timirttiya, heeraa payyatetta, aqotaa dichchaa, heeraa sarotaa h.h.m. muleera deriyappe aybininne shaahettennan deriyara ohetti uttabaa gidiyo gishshaw asay dariya baggi ha qommoora qonccida allaaleta odiyo gishshaw deree hayttaa corggochchidi ezggees. Miidiyassi diya abbee deriyassi naqaashaa gattanaw baaxettiyogaa. Oduwa giigissiyo wode ay jorinaaleekka dogennan poliyobay halchchoogaa maaran tumu yo’uwa koyiyogaa. Lo’’o jorinaale oosoy tumaa demmiyogan erettees; hegaappe denddidi deree hanabaa koshshikkonne giyo oosuwa oottees. Wurssettan deree oduwa siyidi ay oyshshanne denttennan ufayttidi ekkiyogee odo ooson keehippe ufayssiya allaalle. 

Biittan Jorinaaletu Issipetettay (BJI) seeraa kessidi naagettiyobati doosona. Hegeekka hagaappe kaallidi diya yo’oti jorinaaleti biitta xekkan polenna mala teqettidosona.
Gaazeexan likkenna bala qofay maattamettenna mala, cimmiyanne asaa oonatettaa bochchiya qofay misiliya gidikkonne gaazeexan kiyenna mala maacetti uttiis. 
Issitoo issitoo morettida, asaa bochchiya (asaa maataa yedhdhiyanne) likke gidenna yo’oy xaafettida gaazeexay de’anaw danddayees; hegaa sohuwara geedichchanaw bessees. 
Gaazeexay dumma dumma hayyoy shiiqin ha jorinaaletu issipetettay maayido allaalliya xaafi oyqqidaagaa gidanaw bessees.
Gaazeexan xaafetta yo’oy likkenne asaa ubbaa issi ayfiyan xeelliyagaa gidanaw bessees…………………….
BJI awdenne jorinaaleti xaafi kessiyo naqaashay likkenne tumu yo’uwa oyqqidaagaa gidanaw bessees yaagiis. Hegaa gidikko ha nabbabiya deriyan gaazeexaa oosoy sabetteesnne nashettees. Ha halchchi denddidi kessikko dereekka shammidi nabbabanaw ufayttees; eta oosoy nashettidi deriyaninne kawotankka ekettees. Hegaa gishshaw jorinaaletu oosoy muletoo deriya sabettiya oosuwa oottidi asaa ufayssanaw baaxettiyogaa. 
Bosten (1937nne White 1057) naa’’aykka giidoogaadan oduwa dooroy bari huuphen bana danddayida ooso. Hegee odossi hanees; hagee qassi hanenna kiyo maachchaa koyees. Hageekka jorinaaletussi wolqqaama ooso ayssi giikko hegaadan dooridi shiishshesttesppe attin demmobaa ubaa gede zaari coo xaafettenna. Halchchoy oduwassi tumaa demmanaw efiya sitta oge; ooninne ha ogiya kaallidi biidi wurssettan tumaa xaafi kessees (Schadson 1978). Hagee mintetto qofa gidennan diishin wurssettan demmiyo tumaa. Oduwa issi galla biittaa sa’aa gattanaagee meto miishsha gidikkonne halchchidi marxxidi denddidi gittaa minttidi wodiya immidi loytti oottikko mucurettidi giigida oduwa asaassi issanaw danddayettees.

Jorinaaliizimiyaw maaray mankkay bari huuphen halchchidi oottiyogee  attenna yo’o gidiyogaa mala qonccissees. Jorinaaliizimiya wogay issuwa issuwappe shaakkennan, issuwa yuu’idi haraa qassi xoqqissenna tillanne sitta ogiya, yo’uwa yaanne haanne qel’’iqel’’enna sitti oottidi polanaw bessees yaagees (ibid, s. 19). Jirinaaliizime oosuwan ooninne bari qofaa coo qonccissanaw danddayees shin jorinaalee hegaappe jorinaalee/wodala ganjjee baassi birshshettaa immiyagaa awgaakkonne gacci ekkidi deriyassi qonccissees. 

Halchchoy jorinaaliiziya saynisiyan ekettiyanne jorinaaletti awdenne yedhdhi aadhdhanaw danddayenna miishsha gidiyo gishshaw hegaa ooninne guppy adhdhennan oosuwa peeshshiyo ay jorinaaliyassinne wotto woga. Ha halchchogaappe kareera dumma qofaa qonccissiya yo’uwa jorinaalee muleera dichchanaw koshshees; hegaa gidana xaykko jorinaalee issi qofan eqqennan yaanne haanne qel’’iqel’’ees; giyogaa hegee qassi jorinaaliizimiya maara mankkan ixettees. Hagee oduwa giigissuwa mule attenna dooroy baynna dooroy baynna qofa.   


Jorinaalee bari oosuwaw denddidi awaninne oonaaranne gayttidi qofaa laamettiya asa gidanaw bessees. I asaara eesuwan qofaa laamettanaw deexxiya asa gidikko asay assi oychcho naqaashaa immanaw antenna. Hegee qassi jorinaaliizimiya oosuwassi iita gome. Ayssi giikko jorinaalee asaara ogiyan kariyan gayttidi paskkidi sarotidi asaappe bari halchchuwa qoncciyan odidi naqaashaa demmanaw koshshees. Naqaashi xaykko jorinaaliizimiya oosoy xomppee xayido ambbaa mala. Jorinaaliizime oosoy iitaa kehaa, wordduwa woykko tumaa qoncciyan erissidi ha naa’’u issoy issuwa phalqqiya yo’oti hirxxiyan shaakkidi naa’’u yo’otu dummatettaa bessiya zawaa essidi kanttiyo ooso. Ha oosoy issuwa ziqqissid isswua qassi xoqqissiyogaa gidenna; issuwa bonchchidi issuwa qassi toochchiyo gutara gidenna; guuttaa, gitaa, duriyanne manqquwa ubbaa issi ayfiyan xeelliyonne lo’’o pirddaa immiyo ooso. Issi akeekanaw bessiyabaa televizhzhiiniya oduwa shiishshiyo wode issi jorinaalee suulla keene wordduwa gujjikko A ezggiya asay cora gidiyo gishshaw sohuwara biittay adhdhi wodhdhees. Jorinaaleti xaafiyo qofay asaw gelenna wayssiyanne issoy issuwa phalqqiyagaa gidanaw bessenna worddo yo’oy xaafettikko issi issi mattaaye oosuwan eretida gutaraa hemettissiyageeti asaa garssan daranaadan oottees; hegaa gishshaw hanabaa aybane seliseddissennan milxxi ootti xeellin beettiya tumu yo’uwa wottikko aybane metoy merettenna ha iita oosuwaw halchchi qaaxxiyageetussikka sohoy imettenna. Jorinaalee issi yo’uwa pissiya shiishshanaappe kasettidi loytti pilggidi qociridi shiishshiyogee assi diya era aahotettaa qonccissees; wurssettan A oosoy ezggiyageetussikka gididi deriyan ekettees. Oduwa shiishshiyo wode jorinaalee issi yo’uwassi gaasuwa demmidi he gaasotan eqqidi qonccissuwa immidi xaafiyo gishshaw ay metoynne ufuri baynnan bari oosuwa polanaw danddayees ( Lloyd 2004,  S. 18). Jorinaaliizimiya oosoy genccaa, danddayaa, ammanettiyagaa, xalatettaanne gawaa geeshshatettaa koyees.

Asaa garssan koyro dummattettaa medhdhiday wogaa gidiyo gishataw issi wogay issuwa sugenna malakka jorinaalee akeekidi oottanaw bessiyogee attenna allaalle Egleton (2003, S.158). Halchchoy miidiyaw maaraa mankkan sintta xeera wogatuppe issuwa gidiyogee erettidabaa yaatiyo gishshaw jorinaalee awdenne ha allaalliyappe kareera bari oosuwa efanaw danddayenna.
5.3. DERIYA XEELAA
Frost (2007, S. 71) halchcho ooso ayfiya jorinaalizimiyara gayttidaagaan yaagidi palametti haasayiis. Jorinaaliizimee ooso ayfiya demmiis giyogee tumaa koyidi wurssettan demmiyogaa yaagidi (ibid, s. 75) A palamaassi kaafiya qofaa wottiis. ‘Frost’ qofay ‘Ward’ qofaara ha yo’uwa xeelliyagan mise. Frost ha jorinaalee oosuwa xeelliyagan ‘xeelaa’ giya qaalaa go’’ettin Ward qassi ‘birshshettaa’ giya qaalaa go’’ettiis. Ha naa’’u eranchchatikka naa’’u dumma qaalatun go’’ettidi bantta qofaa birshshonappe aattin qanttan issippe gatti xeelliyo wode naa’’aa qofaykka ha jorinaaliizimiya bolli deriyassi diya xeelaa/qofaa xeelliyagan eti naa’’aykka gaanaw koyidoogee issuwa. ‘Ward’ bari birshshettaa go’’ettoogee issi asi ha jorinaaliizimiya xeelliyagan he izaawussi bari qofan (assi giidoogaa maaran) birshshiyo woykko akeekiyo gishshataassa. Hankkoy qassi xeelaa go’’ettidoy ha jorinaaliizimiya bolli asaassi/deriyassi de’iya xeelaa garssa qofaa qonccissanaassa. He naa’’u eranchchati bantta qofaa qonccissidoogaadan salo gufanttuwan jorinaaliizimiya bolli cora asaa woykko eranchchatussi cora xeelay woykko birshshettay de’anaw danddayees shin xeellin beettiya tumaa ooninne kasha gaanaw danddayenna; hegaa gishshaw ha ubbaakka tumay haarees. Tumay awdenne hagan like hagan qassi like gidenna gaanaw danddayettenna sitta qofa gidiyo gishshataw maabaray issippe maayidi aani aqees. Taassi doonaa eray paca giyogee taassi jorinaaliizimiyan de’iya hekkay dol’’a giyogaa Tractus 1963, ss. 5-6) yaatiyo gishshaw doonaa eray assi diya gelaa kessa loytti eriyogee jorinaaliizimiyassi diya hekkaa beegoyanaw daro maaddees. Wurssettan issi jorinaalee halchchuwa hoolliya shocanaw wurssettan tumaa demmanaw tiraara sitti giida oosuwa gawhayiyo wode assi bari huuphen jorinaaliizimiya bolla A xeelay de’ees; I hegaa maaran tumaa qonccissees. Hegaa gishshaw I wurssettan bari xeelaa qonccissoppe attin tumaappe kareera oottanaw danddayenna. Hara baggaara jorinaalee baassi gelo ogiya kaallidi tumaa demmees giyogaa. Qanttan tumaassi ba huuphen asaa qommoy coraa gidiyo gishshaw coraassi cora birshshettay/xeelay de’ees.



Meeziya 1
Issi wulaato yo’uwara diya hanabaappe tumaa keehi wayssiya hanotan pinqqila kessido oduwa xaafada deriya sissa.

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------.












5.4. QANTTA QOFAA
Deree ekkenna jorinaaliizimee qassi allaalle kessenna. Haray qassi xaafi kessiyo aybaappekka jorinaaliizimiyan birshshetti baynnan haasayiyobikka xaafiyobikka mule qofettenna. 

Jorinaaliizime oosuwan awdenne halanaw danddayenna allaallee tuma giyo miishsha; oone ay wodekka tumaa yedhdhi hemettanaw danddayenna. Tumi jorinaaliizimiyassi ayfe yo’o. Tumaanne halchchuwa tobbiyo wode jorinaaliizimiyassinne oduwaw de’iya halchchoynne birshshettay denddiyogee attennabaa. Jorinaale oosuwa halchchoy, tumaynne deriya koshshay bayra allaalle. Tuma yo’uwa xaafidi maattamiyogee jorinaaliyassi imetta aawatetta gidikkonne jorinaaliizimee qassi ha tumaa koshshaayyo gattiya zarphphe mala. Tumay awdenne jorinaalee bayra sohuwa immin beettiya allaalle gidishi ha tumaw qassi A baassan kessiyay halchchidi tanggiyogaa. Tumay halchchuwa maaran hoolliya shocanaassi woxeretti demmiyobaa gidikkonne kase de’ees shin hegaa oonee deriyassi qonccissanay yaagiya oyshaassi jorinaaliizimee tilla zaaro. Tumay awdenne hagan like hagan qassi like gidenna gaanaw danddayettenna sitta qofa gidiyo gishshataw maabaray issippe maayidi aani aqees. Jorinaaliizimee ooso ayfiya demmiis giyogee tumaa koyidi wurssettan demmiyogaa


Issi hanabay waani polettidaakkonne maaraa oyttidi asaw geliya qaalan go’’ettidi qonccissiyo wode asay tumaa siree baynnan erees; hegeekka ayssi hanidee? Waani hanidee ooni ay oottidee yaagi oyshan toliyo wode maaraa oyqqees.
